===== God Spoke to Zechariah [22-01] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-22-01.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=580b51?nolink&640x360}}


In the past, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** had spoken to **his people** through his **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/angel|angels]]** and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/prophet|prophets]]**. But then **400 years went by when he did not speak to them**. Suddenly an angel came with a message from God to an old **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/priest|priest]]** named **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/zechariah-nt|Zechariah]]**. Zechariah and his wife, Elizabeth, were **godly people**, but she had not been able to have any children.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**his people**  - This could be translated as, “his people, the Israelites” or “his people, the Jews.” But only include the added information if it is not clearly understood who these people were.
    * 


**400 years went by**  - Another way to say this would be, “400 years passed” or “there were 400 years.” 400 years had passed since the last Old Testament prophet, Malachi.
    * 


**when he did not speak to them**  – That is, “during which God did not give any messages to the prophets for his people.”
    * 


**godly people**  - That is, “people who obeyed God.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__21-15|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/22-the-birth-of-john|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__22-02|>>]]**


===== You Will Have a Son [22-02] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-22-02.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=bae93d?nolink&640x360}}


**The [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/angel|angel]]** said to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/zechariah-nt|Zechariah]]**, “Your wife will have a son. You will name him **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/john-baptist|John]]**. He will be **filled with the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/holy-spirit|Holy Spirit]]**, and will **prepare the people for the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/messiah|Messiah]]**!” Zechariah responded, “My wife and I are too old to have children! How will I know this will happen?”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**The angel**  - This refers to the angel that came to Zechariah in **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__22-01|[22-01]]]**.
    * 


**filled with the Holy Spirit**  - That is, “controlled by the Holy Spirit” or, “given wisdom and power by the Holy Spirit.”
    * 


**How will I know this will happen?**  - Another way to translate this would be, “How can I be sure that this will truly happen?”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__22-01|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/22-the-birth-of-john|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__22-03|>>]]**


===== Unable to Speak [22-03] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-22-03.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=52776e?nolink&640x360}}


The **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/angel|angel]]** responded to Zechariah, “I was sent by **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** to bring you this good news. Because you did not **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/believe|believe]]** me, you will not be able to speak until the child is born.” Immediately, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/zechariah-nt|Zechariah]]** was unable to speak. Then the angel left Zechariah. After this, Zechariah returned home and his wife **became pregnant**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**became pregnant**  - Some languages have polite ways of saying “become pregnant.” Use an expression that will not be embarrassing to readers.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__22-02|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/22-the-birth-of-john|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__22-04|>>]]**


===== An Angel Spoke to Mary [22-04] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-22-04.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=6e0107?nolink&640x360}}


When **Elizabeth**  was **six months pregnant**, the same **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/angel|angel]]** suddenly appeared to **Elizabeth’s relative**, whose name was **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/mary|Mary]]**. She was a **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/virgin|virgin]]** and **was engaged**  to be married to a man named **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/joseph-nt|Joseph]]**. The angel said, “You will become pregnant and give birth to a son. You are to name him **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** and he will be the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/messiah|Messiah]]**.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**six months pregnant**  - Either she had already been pregnant for six months or she was in the sixth month of her pregnancy.
    * 


**pregnant**  - Different languages have different idioms to talk about pregnancy, such as “she was with child” or, “she had one in her body” or, “she had belly.” Some languages have special ways of speaking about it politely, such as “she was expecting.” Use an expression that will not be embarrassing to readers.
    * 


**Elizabeth**  - She was Zechariah's wife. An angel told Zechariah that Elizabeth would give birth to a son.
    * 


**Elizabeth’s relative**  - Many translations say, “cousin” here but we don't know exactly how these two women were related. A general term like, “relative,” “kin” or, “cousin” could be used.
    * 


**was engaged**  - That is, “was promised.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__22-03|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/22-the-birth-of-john|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__22-05|>>]]**


===== The Mother of the Messiah [22-05] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-22-05.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=974ec0?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/mary|Mary]]** replied, “**How can this be**, since I am a **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/virgin|virgin]]**?” The **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/angel|angel]]** explained, “The **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/holy-spirit|Holy Spirit]]** will **come to you, and the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/power|power]] of [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]] will overshadow you**. So the baby will be **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/holy|holy]]**, the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god-son|Son of God]]**.” Mary **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/believe|believed]]** and accepted what the angel said.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**How can this be**  - That is, “How can I become pregnant?” Mary was not doubting the truth of the angel's words, but asking how it would happen.
    * 


**Holy Spirit will come to you, and the power of God will overshadow you**  - These are two ways of saying the same thing: “By the power of God, the Holy Spirit will miraculously cause you to become pregnant.” Make sure the translation of this sentence does not sound like there was any physical contact involved. This was a miracle.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__22-04|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/22-the-birth-of-john|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__22-06|>>]]**


===== Mary and Elizabeth [22-06] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-22-06.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=1f9c59?nolink&640x360}}


Soon after the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/angel|angel]]** spoke to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/mary|Mary]]**, she went and visited **Elizabeth**. **As soon as Elizabeth heard Mary’s greeting**, Elizabeth’s **baby jumped inside her**. The women rejoiced together about **what [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]] had done for them**. After Mary visited Elizabeth for three months, Mary returned home.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**Elizabeth**  - See the note about Elizabeth on **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__22-05|[22-04]]]**.
    * 


**As soon as Elizabeth heard Mary’s greeting**  - For some languages it may be better to say, “Mary greeted Elizabeth and as soon as Elizabeth heard her.”
    * 


**baby jumped inside her**  - The baby moved suddenly inside Elizabeth's womb in response to Mary's greeting to Elizabeth.
    * 


**what God had done for them**  - This refers to the fact that both women were pregnant through God's supernatural intervention. Mary had conceived without a man, and Elizabeth had conceived with Zechariah after she was past the age of childbearing.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__22-05|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/22-the-birth-of-john|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__22-07|>>]]**


===== The Birth of John [22-07] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-22-07.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=60a8f5?nolink&640x360}}


After **Elizabeth**  gave birth to her baby boy, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/zechariah-nt|Zechariah]]** and Elizabeth named the baby **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/john-baptist|John]]**, as the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/angel|angel]]** had commanded. Then **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** allowed **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/zechariah-nt|Zechariah]]** to speak again. Zechariah said, “**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/praise|Praise]] God**, because he has remembered his people! You, my son, **will be called**  **the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/prophet|prophet]]** of the **Most High God**  who will prepare the people to receive the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/messiah|Messiah]]**!”


//A Bible story from: Luke 1//


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**Elizabeth**  - See the note about Elizabeth on **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__22-05|[22-04]]]**.
    * 


**Praise God**  - That is, “We should all praise God.”
    * 


**will be called**  - This is another way of saying, “will be” or, “will be known as.” John would actually be the Prophet of the Most High God.
    * 


**the prophet**  - That is, “the very important prophet.” John would be the prophet that the Old Testament prophets had predicted would come before the Messiah.
    * 


**Most High God**  - Another way to say this would be, “the God who is greater than everything” or, “the God who rules over everything.”
    * 


//A Bible story from//  - These references may be slightly different in some Bible translations.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__22-06|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/22-the-birth-of-john|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__23-01|>>]]**


===== Mary Was Pregnant [23-01] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-23-01.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=6fec5f?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/mary|Mary]]** was engaged to a **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/righteous|righteous]]** man named **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/joseph-nt|Joseph]]**. When he heard that Mary was pregnant, **he knew it was not his baby**. He did not want **to shame Mary**, so **he planned to quietly divorce her**. Before he could do that, an **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/angel|angel]]** came and spoke to him **in a [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/dream|dream]]**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**he knew it was not his baby**  - That is, “he knew that he was not the one who had caused her to be pregnant.”
    * 


**to shame Mary**  - That is, “to cause Mary to be publicly disgraced” or “to embarrass Mary publicly.” Joseph was merciful to Mary, even though it seemed like she was an adulterer.
    * 


**he planned to quietly divorce her**  - This could also be translated as, “He planned to divorce her without telling others why,” or, “He planned to divorce her without telling others about her pregnancy.” Because Joseph was righteous, he wanted to resolve the situation in the best way possible, which in this culture would be to divorce her quietly.
    * 


**divorce her**  - For some languages it may be better to say, “break their engagement.” Joseph and Mary were engaged or, “pledged to be married.” But in Jewish culture a divorce was required in order to break off an engagement.
    * 


**in a dream**  – That is, “while he was asleep and dreaming.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__22-07|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/23-the-birth-of-jesus|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__23-02|>>]]**


===== Take Mary as Your Wife [23-02] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-23-02.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=905132?nolink&640x360}}


The **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/angel|angel]]** said, “**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/joseph-nt|Joseph]]**, **do not be afraid to take [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/mary|Mary]] as your wife**. The baby that is in her **is from the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/holy-spirit|Holy Spirit]]**. She will give birth to a **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/son|son]]**. Name him **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** (which means, '**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/yahweh|Yahweh]] [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/save|saves]]**'), because he will save the people from their **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sin|sins]]**.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**do not be afraid to take Mary as your wife**  - This can also be translated as, “Stop thinking that you shouldn't marry Mary” or, “Do not hesitate to have Mary as your wife.”
    * 


**is from the Holy Spirit**  - That is, “was conceived by a miracle of the Holy Spirit.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__23-01|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/23-the-birth-of-jesus|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__23-03|>>]]**


===== Joseph Married Mary [23-03] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-23-03.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=f44f6b?nolink&640x360}}


So **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/joseph-nt|Joseph]]** married **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/mary|Mary]]** and took her home as his wife, but **he did not sleep with her**  until she had given birth.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**he did not sleep with her**  - That is, “he did not have sexual relations with her.” He kept her a virgin until the birth of the baby.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__23-02|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/23-the-birth-of-jesus|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__23-04|>>]]**


===== The Trip to Bethlehem [23-04] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-23-04.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=9840f8?nolink&640x360}}


**When the time was near for [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/mary|Mary]] to give birth**, the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/rome|Roman]] government**told everyone to go **for a census**  to the town where their ancestors had lived. **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/joseph-nt|Joseph]]** and Mary had to make a long journey from where they lived in **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/nazareth|Nazareth]]** to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/bethlehem|Bethlehem]]** because their ancestor was **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/david|David]]** whose hometown was Bethlehem.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**When the time was near for Mary to give birth**  - That is, “When it was near the end of Mary's pregnancy.”
    * 


**Roman government**  - Rome had conquered and ruled over Israel at this time.
    * 


**for a census**  - That is, “to be counted for the government record” or, “so that the government could write their names on a list” or, “to be counted by the government.” This census was probably made for the purpose of taxing the people.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__23-03|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/23-the-birth-of-jesus|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__23-05|>>]]**


===== The Birth of Jesus [23-05] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-23-05.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=6a0935?nolink&640x360}}


When they arrived in **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/bethlehem|Bethlehem]]**, there was **no place to stay**. The only room they could find was a **place where animals stayed**. The baby was born there and his mother laid him in a **feeding trough**, since they did not have a bed for him. They named him **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**no place to stay**  - That is, “no usual place to stay.” Because Bethlehem was so crowded at that time, the usual rooms for guests were already full of people.
    * 


**place where animals stayed**  - This was a place for sheltering animals, not a place where people lived. Translate this with a term that would normally be used for a place where animals were kept.
    * 


**feeding trough**  - That is, “animal feed box” or, “wooden or stone box for feeding animals.” The box could have been filled with hay to provide a padded surface for the baby to lie on.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__23-04|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/23-the-birth-of-jesus|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__23-06|>>]]**


===== The Angel and the Shepherds [23-06] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-23-06.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=512d98?nolink&640x360}}


That night, there were some **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/shepherd|shepherds]]** in a nearby field **guarding their flocks**. Suddenly, **a shining [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/angel|angel]]** appeared to them, and **they were terrified**. The angel said, “**Do not be afraid**, because I have some good news for you. The **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/messiah|Messiah]]**, the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/lord|Master]]**, has been born in **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/bethlehem|Bethlehem]]**!”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**guarding their flocks**  - A “flock” is a group of sheep. The shepherds were caring for their sheep, and protecting them from harm or theft.
    * 


**a shining angel**  - This could also be translated as, “an angel surrounded by a bright light.” The shining light would have seemed even brighter in contrast to the darkness of the night.
    * 


**they were terrified**  - The appearance of the supernatural angel was extremely frightening.
    * 


**Do not be afraid**  - This often means, “stop being afraid.” The shepherds were very afraid when they saw the angel so he was telling them they did not need to be afraid.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__23-05|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/23-the-birth-of-jesus|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__23-07|>>]]**


===== The Angels Praised God [23-07] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-23-07.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=47084a?nolink&640x360}}


“Go search for the baby, and you will find him **wrapped in pieces of cloth**  and lying in a feeding trough.” Suddenly, the skies were **filled with [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/angel|angels]]** praising **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]**, saying, “**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/glory|Glory]] to God**in **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/heaven|heaven]]** and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/peace|peace]] on earth**to **the people he favors**!”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


(The angel continued speaking.)


    * 


**wrapped in pieces of cloth**  - The custom of that time was to tightly wrap newborn babies in long strips of cloth. It may be necessary to say, “wrapped in long strips of cloth, in the customary way.”
    * 


**feeding trough**  - That is, “animal feeding box.” Also see how you translated this in **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__23-05|[23-05]]]**.
    * 


**filled with angels**  - This means that there were so many angels that they seemed to fill the sky.
    * 


**Glory to God**  - This can also be translated as, “Let us all give glory to God!” or, “Our God deserves all glory and honor!” or, “We all give glory to God!”
    * 


**peace on earth**  - Another way to say this would be, “may there be peace on earth.”
    * 


**the people he favors**  - This might be translated as, “people that God looks upon with favor, delight, or good will.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__23-06|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/23-the-birth-of-jesus|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__23-08|>>]]**


===== The Shepherds Visited Jesus [23-08] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-23-08.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=ee4d64?nolink&640x360}}


The **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/shepherd|shepherds]]** soon arrived at the place where **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** was and they found him lying in a feeding trough, just as the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/angel|angel]]** had told them. They were very excited. **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/mary|Mary]]** was very happy, too. The shepherds returned to the fields where their sheep were, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/praise|praising]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** for **all they had heard and seen**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**all they had heard and seen**  - That is, “for everything they had heard and seen.” This included the glorious angels and their amazing message, as well as seeing the newborn Messiah himself.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__23-07|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/23-the-birth-of-jesus|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__23-09|>>]]**


===== The Wise Men Visited Jesus [23-09] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-23-09.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=d9bb69?nolink&640x360}}


**Sometime later**, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/wise|wise]] men**from countries far to the east saw an **unusual star**  in the sky. **They realized**  it meant a new **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/king-of-jews|king of the Jews]]** had been born. So, they traveled a great distance to see this king. They came to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/bethlehem|Bethlehem]]** and found **the house**  where **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** and his parents were staying.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**Sometime later**  - It is not clear how long it was after the birth of Jesus before the wise men saw the star, but it may have taken as long as two years for them to prepare for the trip and then travel to Bethlehem.
    * 


**wise men**  - The “wise men” were probably astrologers who studied the stars. They may also have had access to the Old Testament prophets' writings that predicted the birth of the Messiah.
    * 


**unusual star**  - The star that they noticed was not a normal star. It was something that appeared at the time of Jesus' birth.
    * 


**They realized**  - Some languages may add, “From their studies, these scholars realized.”
    * 


**the house**  - They were no longer staying in the place for animals where he was born.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__23-08|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/23-the-birth-of-jesus|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__23-10|>>]]**


===== Worship for the Baby [23-10] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-23-10.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=01995c?nolink&640x360}}


When the **wise men**  saw **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** with his mother, they **bowed down**  and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/worship|worshiped]]** him. They gave Jesus **expensive**  gifts. Then they returned home.


//A Bible story from: Matthew 1; Luke 2//


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**wise men**  - See how you translated this term in **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__23-09|[23-09]]]**.
    * 


**bowed down**  - That is, “bowed low to the ground.” At that time, this was the customary way of showing great respect or reverence.
    * 


**expensive**  – That is, “very valuable.”
    * 


//A Bible story from//  - These references may be slightly different in some Bible translations.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__23-09|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/23-the-birth-of-jesus|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__24-01|>>]]**


===== John the Prophet [24-01] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-24-01.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=f47d22?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/john-baptist|John]]**, the son of **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/zechariah-nt|Zechariah]]** and Elizabeth, grew up and became a **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/prophet|prophet]]**. He lived in the **wilderness**, ate **wild honey**  and **locusts**, and wore **clothes made from camel hair**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**wilderness**  - That is, “the desert” or, “a remote, desert-like place.” There were few people living out in this area.
    * 


**wild honey**  - This honey was the natural product of bees in the wilderness; it was not cultivated by people. If that is what people would understand by the word “honey,” you may not need to call it “wild.”
    * 


**locusts**  - These were large, hopping insects with wings, like very large grasshoppers. Some people who live in the desert eat them.
    * 


**camel hair**  - A camel is an animal that has very rough hair. People could make clothing out of it. This could be translated as “rough animal hair.”
    * 


**clothes made from camel hair**  - That is, “coarse clothes made of camel hair.” These clothes would not quickly wear out in the wilderness as other clothes would.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__23-10|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/24-john-baptizes-jesus|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__24-02|>>]]**


===== A Call to Repent [24-02] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-24-02.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=e30743?nolink&640x360}}


Many people came out to the **wilderness**  to listen to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/john-baptist|John]]**. He **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/preach|preached]]** to them, saying, “**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/repent|Repent]]**, for **the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/kingdom-of-god|kingdom of God]] is near**!”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**wilderness**  - See how you translated this word in **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__24-01|[24-01]]]**.
    * 


**Repent**  - It might be better to say, “Repent from your sins.”
    * 


**the kingdom of God is near**  - That is, “the kingdom of God is ready to appear” or, “the kingdom of God will arrive soon.” This refers to God's ruling over people. This can also be translated as, “God's reign is about to begin” or, “God will soon rule over us as king.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__24-01|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/24-john-baptizes-jesus|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__24-03|>>]]**


===== A Baptism of Repentance [24-03] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-24-03.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=5ed13b?nolink&640x360}}


When people heard **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/john-baptist|John's]]** message, many of them **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/repent|repented]] from their [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sin|sins]]**, and John **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/baptize|baptized]]** them. Many **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jewish-leaders|religious leaders]]** also came to be baptized by John, but they **did not repent**  or **confess their sins**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**repented from their sins**  - This could also be translated as, “repented concerning their sins” or, “changed their minds about their sins” or, “turned away from their sins.”
    * 


**did not repent**  - That is, “did not turn away from their sins.”
    * 


**confess their sins**  - To confess is to acknowledge that something is true. These leaders did not want to acknowledge that they had sinned. This may be translated as, “confess that they had sinned.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__24-02|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/24-john-baptizes-jesus|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__24-04|>>]]**


===== Preparing the Way [24-04] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-24-04.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=fa4917?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/john-baptist|John]]** said to the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jewish-leaders|religious leaders]]**, “**You poisonous snakes**! **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/repent|Repent]]** and change your behavior. **Every tree that does not bear good fruit**  **will be cut down and thrown into the fire**.” **John [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/fulfill|fulfilled]]** what the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/prophet|prophets]]** said, “**See**, I send **my messenger**  **ahead of you**, who will **prepare your way**.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**You poisonous snakes**  - This could be translated as, “You are like lying poisonous snakes!” John was calling them poisonous snakes because they were dangerous and deceptive.
    * 


**Every tree that does not bear good fruit**  - John is not really talking about trees. This is an expression that compares good fruit to good actions and attitudes that come from God.
    * 


**will be cut down and thrown into the fire**  – This means, “will be judged and punished by God.”
    * 


**John fulfilled**  - That is, “John was doing” what the prophet said God's messenger would do.
    * 


**See**  - This could be translated as “Look and see” or, “Pay attention!”
    * 


**my messenger**  - That is, “I, Yahweh, will send my messenger.” In some languages it would be more natural to use an indirect quote for this sentence, such as: “what the prophet Isaiah predicted when he said that God would send his messenger.”
    * 


**ahead of you**  - In this phrase, the word “you” refers to the Messiah.
    * 


**prepare your way**  - God's messenger will prepare the people to listen to the Messiah.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__24-03|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/24-john-baptizes-jesus|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__24-05|>>]]**


===== Not the Messiah [24-05] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-24-05.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=26c3b4?nolink&640x360}}


Some **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jew|Jews]]** asked **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/john-baptist|John]]** if he was the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/messiah|Messiah]]**. John replied, “I am not the Messiah, but there is someone coming after me. **He is so great**  that I am **not even worthy to untie his sandals**.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**He is so great**  - This could be translated as, “He is so important.”
    * 


**not even worthy to untie his sandals**  - In other words, “compared to him, I am not important enough to do even the most menial task for him.” Untying sandals was a very low job, something a slave would do.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__24-04|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/24-john-baptizes-jesus|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__24-06|>>]]**


===== Jesus Is the Lamb of God [24-06] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-24-06.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=095361?nolink&640x360}}


The next day, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** came to be **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/baptize|baptized]]** by **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/john-baptist|John]]**. When John saw him, he said, “Look! **There is**  the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/lamb|Lamb]] of [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** who **will take away**  the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sin|sin]] of the world**.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**There is**  – For some languages this would be, “Here is” or, “That man is.”
    * 


**Lamb of God**  - This could also be translated as, “the Lamb from God” or, “the sacrifice Lamb that God has provided.” Jesus was the perfect sacrifice for sin that God promised to provide. He fulfills the image that was presented by the sacrifice of lambs in the Old Testament.
    * 


**will take away**  - The sacrifice of Jesus causes God to look at our sin as if it never existed.
    * 


**sin of the world**  - That is, “the sin of the people in the world.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__24-05|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/24-john-baptizes-jesus|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__24-07|>>]]**


===== John Baptized Jesus [24-07] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-24-07.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=2e7f38?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/john-baptist|John]]** said to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]**, “**I am not worthy to [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/baptize|baptize]] you**. You should baptize me instead.” But Jesus said, “You should baptize me, because **it is the right thing to do**.” So John baptized him, even though Jesus had never **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sin|sinned]]**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**I am not worthy to baptize you**  - This could be translated as, “I am not good enough to baptize you” or, “I am sinful, so I should not baptize you.”
    * 


**it is the right thing to do**  - This might also be translated as, “it is the proper thing to do” or, “this is what God wants me to do.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__24-06|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/24-john-baptizes-jesus|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__24-08|>>]]**


===== You Are My Beloved Son [24-08] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-24-08.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=21222d?nolink&640x360}}


When **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** came up out of the water after being **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/baptize|baptized]]**, the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/holy-spirit|Spirit of God]] appeared in the form of a dove**and came down and rested on him. At the same time, God's voice spoke from **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/heaven|heaven]]**, saying, “You are **my [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god-son|Son]] whom I [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/love|love]]**, and I am very pleased with you.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**my Son whom I love**  - Make sure the translation of this does not sound like there was another son. It may be necessary to say, “You are my Son. I love you very much and am very pleased with you.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__24-07|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/24-john-baptizes-jesus|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__24-09|>>]]**


===== Jesus Is the Son of God [24-09] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-24-09.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=660c08?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]] had told [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/john-baptist|John]]**, “The **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/holy-spirit|Holy Spirit]]****will come down and rest on**  someone you **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/baptize|baptize]]**. That person is the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god-son|Son of God]]**.” There is only one God. But John heard **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god-father|God the Father]]** speak, and saw **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god-son|Son]]** and the Holy Spirit when he baptized Jesus.


//A Bible story from: Matthew 3; Mark 1:9-11; Luke 3:1-23//


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**God had told John**  - That is, “Before this, God had told John” or, “Before Jesus came to be baptized, God had told John.”
    * 


//A Bible story from//  - These references may be slightly different in some Bible translations.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__24-08|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/24-john-baptizes-jesus|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__25-01|>>]]**


===== Satan Tempted Jesus [25-01] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-25-01.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=56d0cb?nolink&640x360}}


Immediately after **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** was **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/baptize|baptized]]**, **the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/holy-spirit|Holy Spirit]] led him**out into **the wilderness**, where he **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/fast|fasted]]** for **forty days and forty nights**. Then **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/satan|Satan]]** came to Jesus and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/tempt|tempted]] him to [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sin|sin]]**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**the Holy Spirit led him**  – That is, “the Holy Spirit guided him” or, “the Holy Spirit prompted him to go.”
    * 


**the wilderness**  - This could also be translated as, “the desert” or, “a remote, barren place with few people.” This place probably had very few trees or other plants, so most people would not be able to live there.
    * 


**forty days and forty nights**  - This means “forty days, both during the day and during the night.” Make sure the translation of this phrase does not sound like a period of eighty days.
    * 


**tempted him to sin**  - Since Jesus did not sin, make sure you use a word that does not imply that Satan succeeded in convincing Jesus to sin. This phrase could also be translated as, “tried to convince him to sin.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__24-09|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/25-satan-tempts-jesus|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__25-02|>>]]**


===== The First Temptation [25-02] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-25-02.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=a527e2?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/satan|Satan]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/tempt|tempted]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** by saying, “If you are the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god-son|Son of God]]**, **turn these rocks into bread**  so you can eat!”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**turn these rocks into bread**  - This may also be translated as, “make these rocks become bread” or, “supernaturally change these rocks into bread.”
    * 


**bread**  – This could be translated as, “food” for languages where bread is not a common food. In the Jews' culture, bread was the main food.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__25-01|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/25-satan-tempts-jesus|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__25-03|>>]]**


===== God's Word Gives Life [25-03] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-25-03.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=d2db67?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** replied, “It is written in **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/word-of-god|God’s word,]]** ‘People do not only need **bread**  in order to live, **but they need every word that [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]] speaks!**’”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**bread**  – Make sure that you use the same word to translate “bread” here as you did in **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__25-02|[25-02]]]**.
    * 


**but they need every word that God speaks!**  - Another way to translate this would be, “Rather, people need to listen to and obey everything God says” or, “Rather, people have real life by believing and obeying what God says.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__25-02|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/25-satan-tempts-jesus|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__25-04|>>]]**


===== The Second Temptation [25-04] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-25-04.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=db76a1?nolink&640x360}}


Then **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/satan|Satan]]** took **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** to the highest point on the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/temple|Temple]]** and said, “If you are the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god-son|Son of God]]**, **throw yourself down**, because **it is written**, ‘**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** will command his **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/angel|angels]]** to carry you **so your foot does not hit a stone**.’”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**throw yourself down**  - That is, “jump off this building to the ground.”
    * 


**it is written**  – That is, “a prophet of God wrote long ago.”
    * 


**so your foot does not hit a stone**  - This means, “so that you will not be hurt at all; not even your foot will be injured on a stone.” It could also be translated as, “so that even your foot will not strike against a stone; you will not be injured at all.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__25-03|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/25-satan-tempts-jesus|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__25-05|>>]]**


===== Do Not Test God [25-05] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-25-05.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=7c0318?nolink&640x360}}


But **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** replied to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/satan|Satan]]** by quoting from the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/word-of-god|scriptures.]]** He said, “**In [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/word-of-god|God's word]], he commands his people, ‘Do not test the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/lord|Lord]] your [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]**.’”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**In God’s word, he commands his people, ‘Do not test the Lord, your God.’”**  – This could be translated as an indirect quote: “God commands us in his word that we should not test the Lord our God.”
    * 


**Do not test the Lord your God**  - This could be translated as, “Do not make the Lord your God prove himself to you” or, “Do not make the Lord your God prove that he is good.”
    * 


**Lord your God**  – That is, “Yahweh, your God” or, “Yahweh, who is God and has authority over you.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__25-04|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/25-satan-tempts-jesus|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__25-06|>>]]**


===== The Third Temptation [25-06] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-25-06.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=6eca17?nolink&640x360}}


Then **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/satan|Satan]]** showed **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** all the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/kingdom|kingdoms]] of the world**and all **their [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/glory|glory]]** and said, “**I will give you all this**  if you bow down and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/worship|worship]]** me.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**kingdoms of the world**  - This refers to all the greatest cities, countries, and other territories of the world.
    * 


**their glory**  - That is, “their power and wealth.”
    * 


**I will give you all this**  - This could be translated as, “I will give you all the wealth and power of these kingdoms” or, “I will make you the ruler over all these countries, cities and people.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__25-05|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/25-satan-tempts-jesus|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__25-07|>>]]**


===== Worship Only God [25-07] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-25-07.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=a62a59?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** replied, “**Get away from me**, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/satan|Satan]]**! **In [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/word-of-god|God’s word]] he commands his people, ‘[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/worship|Worship]] only the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/lord|Lord]] your [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]] and only serve him**.’”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**Get away from me**  - This may also be translated as, “Leave me” or, “Leave me alone.”
    * 


**In God’s word he commands his people, “Worship only the Lord your God and only serve him”**  – This could be written as an indirect quote, “In God's word, he commands us that we must worship and serve only the Lord God, who rules over us.”
    * 


**Lord your God**  – Translate this phrase the same way as you did in **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__25-05|[25-05]]]**.
    * 


**and only serve him**  – Another way to say this would be, “He is the only one you should serve.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__25-06|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/25-satan-tempts-jesus|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__25-08|>>]]**


===== Angels Ministered to Jesus [25-08] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-25-08.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=4c4bf5?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]****did not give in to**  **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/satan|Satan's]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/tempt|temptations]]**, so Satan left him. Then **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/angel|angels]]** came and took care of Jesus.


//A Bible story from: Matthew 4:1-11; Mark 1:12-13; Luke 4:1-13//


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**did not give in to**  - This could be translated as, “did not do the things that Satan was tempting him to do.”
    * 


//A Bible story from//  - These references may be slightly different in some Bible translations.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__25-07|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/25-satan-tempts-jesus|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__26-01|>>]]**


===== Jesus in Galilee [26-01] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-26-01.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=ef1705?nolink&640x360}}


**After overcoming [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/satan|Satan's]] [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/tempt|temptations]], [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]] returned****in the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/power|power]] of the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/holy-spirit|Holy Spirit]]** to the region of **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/galilee|Galilee]]** where he lived. Jesus **went from place to place teaching**. **Everyone**  **spoke well of him**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**After overcoming Satan's temptations, Jesus returned**  – You may prefer to make this into two sentences and say, “Jesus did not do the wrong things Satan tried to get him to do and so defeated him. After that, Jesus returned.” The word “overcoming” can also be translated with “resisting” or, “rejecting” or, “refusing.”
    * 


**in the power of the Holy Spirit**  - This may be translated as, “as the power of the Holy Spirit worked through him” or, “and the Holy Spirit was powerfully guiding him.”
    * 


**went from place to place teaching**  – That is, he “traveled to different towns and other places and taught the people there.”
    * 


**Everyone**  - That is, “Everyone who knew him or heard about him.”
    * 


**spoke well of him**  - That is, “said good things about him.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__25-08|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/26-jesus-starts-his-ministry|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__26-02|>>]]**


===== Jesus in Nazareth [26-02] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-26-02.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=248ee3?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** went to the town of **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/nazareth|Nazareth]]** where he had lived during his childhood. On the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sabbath|Sabbath]]**, he went to the **place of [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/worship|worship]]**. They handed him the **scroll of the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/prophet|prophet]] [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/isaiah|Isaiah]]** so that he would read from it. Jesus **opened up the scroll**  and read part of it to the people.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**place of worship**  – That is, “the building where the Jews gathered to worship God.” This can also be translated as, “worship building.”
    * 


**scroll**  - A scroll was a long sheet of paper or leather that was rolled up and had writing on it.
    * 


**the scroll of the prophet Isaiah**  – That is, “the scroll that had the words that the prophet Isaiah had written.” Isaiah had written on a scroll hundreds of years before. This was a copy of that scroll.
    * 


**opened up the scroll**  – This could be translated as, “rolled open the scroll” or, “unrolled the scroll.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__26-01|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/26-jesus-starts-his-ministry|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__26-03|>>]]**


===== Jesus Read the Scriptures [26-03] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-26-03.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=95a9e6?nolink&640x360}}


Jesus read, “**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** has given me his **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/holy-spirit|Spirit]]** so that I can **proclaim [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/good-news|good news]] to the poor**, **freedom to captives**, **recovery of sight for the blind**, and **release to the oppressed**. This is **the year of the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/lord|Lord's]] favor**.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**proclaim good news to the poor**  - That is, “to tell poor and needy people the good message that God will help them.”
    * 


**freedom to captives**  - That is, “to tell people who are wrongfully in prison that they will be released.”
    * 


**recovery of sight for the blind**  - This could be translated as, “that those who are blind will receive their sight.”
    * 


**release to the oppressed**  - That is, “freedom for those who are mistreated in life.”
    * 


**the year of the Lord's favor**  - This may be translated as, “the time when the Lord will be merciful to us” or, “the time when the Lord will be very gracious to us.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__26-02|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/26-jesus-starts-his-ministry|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__26-04|>>]]**


===== The Prophesy about Jesus [26-04] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-26-04.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=092768?nolink&640x360}}


Then **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** sat down. Everybody watched him closely. They knew the passage of **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/word-of-god|scripture]]** that he had just read referred to the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/messiah|Messiah]]**. Jesus said, “**The words I just read to you are happening right now**.” All the people were **amazed**. “**Isn’t this the son of [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/joseph-nt|Joseph]]**?” they said.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**The words I just read to you are happening right now**  - Other ways to translate this would be, “The words you just heard me read are being fulfilled right now” or, “Today the words I read to you came true as you heard them.”
    * 


**amazed**  - Translate the word “amazed” with a term that means that they were surprised, shocked, and confused about how this could be possible.
    * 


**Isn't this the son of Joseph?**  –This could also be translated as, “This man is only the son of Joseph!” or, “Everyone knows he is just Joseph's son!” The people were not asking if he was Joseph's son or not. They were wondering how he could be the Messiah since they thought he was only the son of an ordinary man.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__26-03|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/26-jesus-starts-his-ministry|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__26-05|>>]]**


===== The Ministry of Elijah [26-05] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-26-05.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=ef1a2a?nolink&640x360}}


Then **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** said, “It is **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/true|true]]** that **no [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/prophet|prophet]] is accepted in his own hometown**. During the time of the prophet **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/elijah|Elijah]]**, there were many widows in **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israel]]**. But when it did not rain for three and a half years, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** did not send Elijah to help a widow from Israel, but rather to a widow from a different nation.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**no prophet is accepted in his hometown**  - This phrase means, “people do not recognize the authority of a prophet that has grown up among them.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__26-04|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/26-jesus-starts-his-ministry|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__26-06|>>]]**


===== The Ministry of Elisha [26-06] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-26-06.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=861454?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** continued saying, “And during the time of the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/prophet|prophet]]****Elisha**, there were many people in **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israel]]** with skin diseases. But Elisha did not **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/heal|heal]]** any of them. He only healed the skin disease of **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/naaman|Naaman]]**, **a commander**  of Israel’s enemies.” The people who were listening to Jesus were **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jew|Jews]]**. So when they heard him say this, **they were furious at him**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**Elisha**  - Elisha was God's prophet who came after Elijah. Like Elijah, Elisha confronted Israelite kings who were sinning against God and he did miracles that God gave him power to do.
    * 


**a commander**  – That is, “a military leader.”
    * 


**they were furious at him**  - The Jews did not want to hear that God had blessed any people group besides themselves, so they were very angry at what Jesus said.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__26-05|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/26-jesus-starts-his-ministry|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__26-07|>>]]**


===== The Attempt to Kill Jesus [26-07] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-26-07.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=8709a8?nolink&640x360}}


The people of **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/nazareth|Nazareth]]** dragged **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** out of the **place of [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/worship|worship]]** and brought him to the edge of a cliff to throw him off of it in order to kill him. **But Jesus walked through the crowd**  and left the town of Nazareth.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**place of worship**  - That is, “the building where the Jewish people gathered to worship God.” This can also be translated as “worship building.” See how you translated it in **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__26-02|[26-02]]]**.
    * 


**But Jesus walked through the crowd**  - “But” could be translated with a strong contrast word or phrase such as “But instead” or, “However” to show that the people were not able to do to Jesus what they had planned to do.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__26-06|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/26-jesus-starts-his-ministry|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__26-08|>>]]**


===== Jesus Healed the Sick [26-08] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-26-08.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=91c7b1?nolink&640x360}}


Then **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]****went throughout the region of [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/galilee|Galilee]]**, and large crowds came to him. They brought many people who were sick or handicapped, including those who could not see, walk, hear, or speak, and Jesus **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/heal|healed]]** them.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**went throughout the region of Galilee**  - That is, “all around in Galilee” or, “from place to place in Galilee.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__26-07|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/26-jesus-starts-his-ministry|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__26-09|>>]]**


===== Jesus Removed the Demons [26-09] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-26-09.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=99726f?nolink&640x360}}


Many people **who had [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/demon|demons]] in them**were brought to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]**. **At Jesus' command**, the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/demon|demons]]** came out of the people, and often shouted, “You are the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god-son|Son of God]]**!” The crowds of people were amazed and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/worship|worshiped]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**who had demons in them**  –That is, “who were controlled by evil spirits.”
    * 


**When Jesus commanded them**  - This could also be translated as, “When Jesus gave the command to them.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__26-08|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/26-jesus-starts-his-ministry|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__26-10|>>]]**


===== The Twelve Disciples [26-10] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-26-10.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=273162?nolink&640x360}}


Then **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** chose twelve men **who were called his [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/apostle|apostles]]**. The apostles traveled with Jesus and **learned from him**.


//A Bible story from: Matthew 4:12-25; Mark 1:14-15, 35-39; 3:13-21; Luke 4:14-30, 38-44//


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**learned from him**  – That is, “learned from what he taught them” or, “learned from everything he said and did.”
    * 


//A Bible story from//  - These references may be slightly different in some Bible translations.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__26-09|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/26-jesus-starts-his-ministry|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__27-01|>>]]**


===== The Lawyer's Question [27-01] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-27-01.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=91543c?nolink&640x360}}


**One day**, an **expert in the Jewish law**  came to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]****to test him**, saying, “**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/teacher|Teacher]]**, what must I do **to [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/inherit|inherit]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/eternal-life|eternal life]]**?” Jesus answered, “**What is written in [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/gods-law|God's law]]**?”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**One day**  - This phrase introduces an event that happened in the past, but does not state the specific time. Many languages have a similar way to begin telling a true story.
    * 


**expert in the Jewish law**  - This man was someone who studied and taught the laws God had given the Israelites, as well as other Jewish laws.
    * 


**to test him**  - That is, “to see if Jesus would give a good answer.”
    * 


**to inherit eternal life**  - That is, “to have life with God forever” or, “so that God will give me life with him forever” or, “to receive eternal life from God.” The law expert was asking how he could be worthy to receive eternal life as an inheritance from God the Father.
    * 


**eternal life**  - This refers to life forever with God after the mortal body dies. See the key term page for eternal life.
    * 


**What is written in God's law?**  - That is, “What is written in God's law about this?” Jesus asked this question because he wanted the man to think about what God's law really teaches.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__26-10|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/27-the-story-of-the-good-samaritan|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__27-02|>>]]**


===== Obey the Commandments [27-02] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-27-02.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=10afbc?nolink&640x360}}


The **law expert**  replied that **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/gods-law|God's law]]** says, “**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/love|Love]] the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/lord|Lord]] your [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]****with all your heart, soul, strength, and mind**. And **love your neighbor as yourself**.” **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** answered, “You are correct! Do this and you will **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/life|live]]**.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**law expert**  - That is, “an expert in the Jewish law.” See how you translated this term in **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__27-01|[27-01]]]**.
    * 


**Love the Lord your God**  – You may choose to say, “We must love the Lord our God.” Make sure it does not sound like the man is commanding Jesus. Rather, he is quoting what God's law commands people to do.
    * 


**with all your heart, soul, strength, and mind**  - That is, “with your whole self” or, “with every part of yourself.” In some languages this might be translated as, “with all your liver, breath, strength, and thoughts.” The focus is not on each of these parts, but on all of us. Use the concepts in your language that make up the whole person.
    * 


**heart**  - The heart refers to the part of a person that has desires and emotions.
    * 


**soul**  - The soul refers to the nonphysical, spiritual part of a person.
    * 


**strength**  - Strength refers to the physical body and all of its abilities.
    * 


**mind**  - The mind refers to the part of a person that thinks, plans, and has ideas.
    * 


**neighbor**  - The word “neighbor” normally refers to a person who lives near us. The Jews applied the term to someone who was neither a close relative nor a foreigner or enemy.
    * 


**love your neighbor as yourself**  – That is, “love your neighbor to the same extent that you love yourself.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__27-01|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/27-the-story-of-the-good-samaritan|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__27-03|>>]]**


===== Who Is My Neighbor? [27-03] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-27-03.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=c8e5eb?nolink&640x360}}


But the **law expert**  wanted to prove that he was **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/righteous|righteous]]**, so he asked, “**Who is my neighbor?**


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**law expert**  - That is, “an expert in the Jewish law.” See how you translated this term in **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__27-01|[27-01]]]**.
    * 


**Who is my neighbor?**  – This could also be translated as, “What do you mean by 'neighbor'?” or, “Which people are my neighbors?” He knew that he did not love everyone, and was asking which people he needed to love.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__27-02|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/27-the-story-of-the-good-samaritan|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__27-04|>>]]**


===== The Jewish Traveler [27-04] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-27-04.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=a7a839?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** answered the **law expert**  by telling a story. “There was a **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jew|Jewish]]** man who was traveling along the road **from [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jerusalem|Jerusalem]] to [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jericho|Jericho]]**.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


(The cloud-like frame around this picture indicates that Jesus is telling a story, and not necessarily explaining a historical event.)


    * 


**law expert**  - See how you translated this term in **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__27-01|[27-01]]]**.
    * 


**from Jerusalem to Jericho**  – In some languages you could translate this as, “from the city of Jerusalem to the city of Jericho” or, “from Jerusalem City to Jericho City.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__27-03|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/27-the-story-of-the-good-samaritan|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__27-05|>>]]**


===== The Robbers [27-05] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-27-05.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=37b80d?nolink&640x360}}


“While the man was traveling, he was attacked by a group of robbers. They took **everything he had**  and beat him until he was almost dead. Then they went away.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


(Jesus continues to tell the story.)


    * 


**everything he had**  – That is, “everything he had with him, including the clothes he was wearing.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__27-04|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/27-the-story-of-the-good-samaritan|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__27-06|>>]]**


===== The Priest [27-06] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-27-06.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=902ff3?nolink&640x360}}


“Soon after that, a **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jew|Jewish]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/priest|priest]]****happened to walk down**  that same road. When this **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jewish-leaders|religious leader]]** saw the man who had been robbed and beaten, he moved to the other side of the road, **ignored the man**  who needed help, and **kept on going**.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


(Jesus continues to tell the story.)


    * 


**happened to walk down**  – That is, “happened to be traveling along.” For some languages it may be necessary to use a word like “travel” rather than “walk” since the priest was not just walking on the road but was traveling to get to another city.
    * 


**ignored the man**  - That is, “did not help the man” or, “showed no concern for the man.”
    * 


**kept on going**  - That is, “continued traveling down the road.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__27-05|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/27-the-story-of-the-good-samaritan|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__27-07|>>]]**


===== The Levite [27-07] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-27-07.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=01b161?nolink&640x360}}


“Not long after that, a Levite **came down the road**. (**Levites were a tribe of [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jew|Jews]]** who helped the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/priest|priests]]** at the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/temple|Temple]]**.) The Levite also crossed over to the other side of the road and **ignored**  the man who had been robbed and beaten.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


(Jesus continues to tell the story.)


    * 


**came down the road**  – That is, “was traveling down that same road.”
    * 


**Levites were a tribe of Jews**  – That is, “Levites were from the Israelite tribe of Levi” or, “Levites were from the Israelite clan of Levi.”
    * 


**ignored**  – That is, “did not help.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__27-06|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/27-the-story-of-the-good-samaritan|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__27-08|>>]]**


===== The Samaritan [27-08] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-27-08.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=9a665f?nolink&640x360}}


“The next person to **walk down**  that road was a **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/samaria|Samaritan]]**. (Samaritans were the descendants of **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jew|Jews]]** who had married people from other nations. Samaritans and Jews hated each other.) But when the Samaritan saw the Jewish man, he felt very strong compassion for him. So he cared for him and bandaged his wounds.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


(Jesus continues to tell the story.)


    * 


**walk down**  – That is, “travel along.” These people were traveling from one city to another. Make sure that it does not sound like they were just taking a walk.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__27-07|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/27-the-story-of-the-good-samaritan|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__27-09|>>]]**


===== Help for the Victim [27-09] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-27-09.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=24e8af?nolink&640x360}}


“The **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/samaria|Samaritan]]** then lifted the man onto **his own donkey**  and took him to a **roadside inn**  **where he took care of him**.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


(Jesus continues to tell the story.)


    * 


**his own donkey**  – Make sure it is clear that “his” refers to the Samaritan.
    * 


**roadside inn**  – That is, “a lodging place.” This is a place where travelers could get food and stay overnight.
    * 


**where he took care of him**  – This could also be translated as, “where he continued to take care of him.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__27-08|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/27-the-story-of-the-good-samaritan|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__27-10|>>]]**


===== Generous Help [27-10] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-27-10.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=13ac79?nolink&640x360}}


“The next day, the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/samaria|Samaritan]]** needed to **continue his journey**. He gave some money to the person **in charge of**  the inn and said, ‘**Take care of him**, and if you spend any more money than this, I will **repay those expenses**  when I return.’”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


(Jesus continues to tell the story.)


    * 


**continue his journey**  – This could be translated as, “continue traveling toward his destination.”
    * 


**in charge of**  – That is, “who managed.” It could be that this person also owned this lodging place.
    * 


**Take care of him**  – For some languages it may be preferable to say, “Please take care of him” in order for it to be clear that this was a polite request, not an order.
    * 


**repay those expenses**  – This could also be translated as, “repay you” or, “repay that money” or, “repay it.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__27-09|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/27-the-story-of-the-good-samaritan|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__27-11|>>]]**


===== Do the Same [27-11] =====
