{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-27-11.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=0c6853?nolink&640x360}}


Then **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** asked the **law expert**, “What do you think? Which one of **the three men**  **was a neighbor**  to the man who was robbed and beaten?” He replied, “The one who was **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/mercy|merciful]]** to him.” Jesus told him, “**You go and do the same**.”


//A Bible story from: Luke 10:25-37//


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**law expert**  - That is, “an expert in the Jewish law.” See how you translated this term in **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__27-01|[27-01]]]**.
    * 


**the three men**  - The three men were the priest, the Levite, and the Samaritan.
    * 


**neighbor**  - Jesus is using the word “neighbor” in a broader sense than in **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__27-02|[27-02]]]**. “Neighbor” here refers to anyone that we meet who needs our help.
    * 


**was a neighbor**  - This can also be translated as, “behaved as a neighbor” or, “was a friend” or, “acted in a loving way”. See how you translated “neighbor” in **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__27-02|[27-02]]]** and **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__27-03|[27-03]]]**.
    * 


**You go and do**  – That is, “You, too, should go and do” or, “Now you must do.” Jesus was commanding the law expert to do as the Samaritan did.
    * 


**do the same**  – That is, “love others, even your enemies.” Make sure it does not sound like “the same” is only referring to helping a wounded man.
    * 


//A Bible story from//  - These references may be slightly different in some Bible translations.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__27-10|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/27-the-story-of-the-good-samaritan|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__28-01|>>]]**


===== What Must I Do? [28-01] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-28-01.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=374896?nolink&640x360}}


**One day**, a **rich young ruler**  **came up to [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** and asked him, “**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/good|Good]] [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/teacher|teacher]]**, what must I do **to have [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/eternal-life|eternal life]]**?” Jesus said to him, “**Why do you call me 'good'**? **There is only one who is good, and that is [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]**. But if you want to have eternal life, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/obey|obey]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/gods-law|God's laws]]**.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**One day**  - This phrase introduces an event that happened in the past, but does not state the specific time. Many languages have a similar way to begin telling a true story.
    * 


**rich young ruler**  - This man was already a rich and powerful political official, even though he was still young.
    * 


**came up to Jesus**  - That is, “approached Jesus.”
    * 


**Good teacher**  - That is, “righteous teacher.” He was not saying that Jesus was simply a skilled teacher.
    * 


**to have eternal life**  - That is, “to receive eternal life” or, “to live with God forever.” Also consider how “eternal life” was translated on **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__27-01|[27-01]]]** and see the note about that there.
    * 


**Why do you call me 'good'**  - Jesus is not denying that he is God. Rather, he is asking if the ruler understands that Jesus is God.
    * 


**There is only one who is good, and that is God**  - Another way to say this would be, “The only one who is truly good is God” or, “God is the only one who is truly good.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__27-11|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/28-the-rich-young-ruler|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__28-02|>>]]**


===== God's Commandments [28-02] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-28-02.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=9f8bb0?nolink&640x360}}


“**Which ones do I need to obey?**” he asked. **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** replied, “Do not murder. Do not commit **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/adultery|adultery]]**. Do not steal. Do not lie. Honor your father and mother, and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/love|love]]** your neighbor **as you love yourself**.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**Which ones do I need to obey?**  - That is, “Which laws will be enough for me to receive eternal life?”
    * 


**as you love yourself**  - That is, “as much as you love yourself” or, “to the same degree that you love yourself.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__28-01|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/28-the-rich-young-ruler|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__28-03|>>]]**


===== What Else Must I Do? [28-03] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-28-03.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=c01f19?nolink&640x360}}


But the young man said, “I have **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/obey|obeyed]]** all these **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/gods-law|laws]]****ever since I was a boy**. **What do I still need to do**  in order to live forever?” **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** looked at him and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/love|loved]] him**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**ever since I was a boy**  – Another way to say this would be, “from the time I was a child until now.”
    * 


**What do I still need to do?**  - That is, “What else do I need to do” or, “What do I need to do in addition to these?”
    * 


**loved him**  - Jesus had compassion on him. Choose a word for love that is consistent with the kind of love God has for people.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__28-02|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/28-the-rich-young-ruler|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__28-04|>>]]**


===== Sell Everything [28-04] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-28-04.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=793e43?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** answered, “If **you**  want to be **perfect**, then go and sell **everything you own**  and give the money to the poor, and you will have **treasure in [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/heaven|heaven]]**. Then come and follow me.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**you**  - If your language has different words for “you” depending on the number of people intended, use the singular form. Jesus was addressing this command to this one man.
    * 


**perfect**  - That is, “completely righteous.”
    * 


**everything you own**  - That is, “all of your possessions.”
    * 


**treasure**  - This could also be translated as, “riches” or, “great wealth.”
    * 


**in heaven**  - This could also be translated as, “located in heaven when you arrive there.” This treasure will exist “there and then,” as opposed to the wealth that Jesus asked the young man to give up “here and now.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__28-03|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/28-the-rich-young-ruler|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__28-05|>>]]**


===== Not Willing to Obey [28-05] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-28-05.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=c64ef0?nolink&640x360}}


When the young man **heard what [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]] said**, he became very sad, because he was very rich and did not want to give away all the things he possessed. He turned and went away from Jesus.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**heard what Jesus said**  – That is, “heard Jesus tell him to give away what he owned.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__28-04|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/28-the-rich-young-ruler|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__28-06|>>]]**


===== The Camel and the Needle [28-06] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-28-06.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=7e61bf?nolink&640x360}}


Then **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** said to his **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/disciple|disciples]]**, “It is extremely hard for rich people to **enter into the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/kingdom-of-god|kingdom of God]]**! Yes, it is easier for a **camel**  to go through the **eye of a needle**  than for a rich man to enter the kingdom of God.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**enter the kingdom of God**  - This can also be translated as, “become a citizen in God's kingdom.”
    * 


**camel**  - Camels are very large animals that are often used to carry heavy loads. If camels are not known in your language area, a phrase such as, “very large animal” or, “beast of burden” could be used. If you choose to substitute the name of some other large animal, make sure that the animal would have been known by the people Jesus was talking to, such as, “ox” or, “donkey.”
    * 


**eye of a needle**  - This refers to the tiny hole in the end of a sewing needle. The idea of something as large as a camel going through the eye of a needle is intended to represent something that is impossible.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__28-05|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/28-the-rich-young-ruler|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__28-07|>>]]**


===== Who Can Be Saved? [28-07] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-28-07.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=1a02ff?nolink&640x360}}


When the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/disciple|disciples]]** heard what Jesus said, they were **shocked**  and said, “Then **who can be [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/save|saved]]**?”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**shocked**  - That is, “greatly astonished.”
    * 


**who can be saved**  - This could also be translated as, “If even rich people cannot be saved, how can anyone else be saved?” Many people believed that being rich was a sign of God's favor.
    * 


**saved**  - Here it refers to being saved from God's judgment and condemnation for sin and being allowed to be a citizen in God's kingdom.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__28-06|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/28-the-rich-young-ruler|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__28-08|>>]]**


===== All Things Are Possible [28-08] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-28-08.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=01a0ec?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** looked at the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/disciple|disciples]]** and said, “**With people this is impossible**, but **with [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]], all things are possible**.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**With people this is impossible**  - That is, “It is not possible for people to do this” or, “Mere humans cannot save themselves.”
    * 


**with God, all things are possible**  - This could also be translated as, “God is able to do anything, even save a rich person” or, “God is able to do impossible things, so he can save even a rich person.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__28-07|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/28-the-rich-young-ruler|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__28-09|>>]]**


===== What Is Our Reward? [28-09] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-28-09.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=bf37f6?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/peter|Peter]]** said to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]**, “We have **left everything**  and followed you. **What will be our reward?**”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**left everything**  - That is, “left everything behind” or, “given up everything we owned.”
    * 


**What will be our reward?**  - Another way to say this is, “What reward will we receive” or, “How will we be rewarded?” or, “What will God give us as a reward?” It may also be necessary to add, “because we have done this?”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__28-08|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/28-the-rich-young-ruler|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__28-10|>>]]**


===== The First and the Last [28-10] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-28-10.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=4eac41?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** answered, “Everyone who **has left**  houses, brothers, sisters, father, mother, children, or property **for my sake**, will receive **100 times more**  and will also receive **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/eternal-life|eternal life]]**. But **many who are first will be last**, and **many who are last will be first**.”


//A Bible story from: Matthew 19:16-30; Mark 10:17-31; Luke 18:18-30//


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**has left**  – That is, “has left behind” or, “has given up” or, “has counted as less important than God.”
    * 


**for my sake**  - This may also be translated as, “because of me” or, “on my account.”
    * 


**100 times more**  - That is, “very much more than he had before.”
    * 


**many who are first will be last**  - That is, “many people who are important now, will not be important then.”
    * 


**many who are last will be first**  - That is, “many people who are considered to not be very important on earth will be considered very important in heaven” or, “Many people who are considered now to be of little value on earth will be highly valued in heaven.”
    * 


//A Bible story from//  - These references may be slightly different in some Bible translations.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__28-09|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/28-the-rich-young-ruler|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__29-01|>>]]**


===== How Many Times? [29-01] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-29-01.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=cd43f0?nolink&640x360}}


**One day**, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/peter|Peter]]** asked **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]**, “**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/lord|Master]]**, how many times should I **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/forgive|forgive]]****my brother**  when he **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sin|sins]] against me**? As many as seven times?” Jesus said, “**Not seven times, but seventy times seven!**” **By this, Jesus meant**  that we should always forgive. Then Jesus told the following story.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**One day**  - This phrase introduces an event that happened in the past, but does not state the specific time. Many languages have a similar way to begin telling a true story.
    * 


**my brother**  - This term sometimes included people who were not actually siblings, but who shared another very strong connection such as religion, ethnic background, etc.
    * 


**sins against me**  - This could also be translated as, “does something wrong against me.”
    * 


**Not seven times, but seventy times seven!**  - This could be translated as, “You should not forgive only seven times, rather you should forgive seventy times seven times.” Jesus was not talking about an exact number. He was saying that we should forgive people every time they sin against us.
    * 


**By this, Jesus meant**  – That is, “When Jesus said this he meant.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__28-10|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/29-the-story-of-the-unmerciful-servant|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__29-02|>>]]**


===== The Huge Debt [29-02] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-29-02.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=d57274?nolink&640x360}}


Jesus said, “**The [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/kingdom-of-god|kingdom of God]] is like****a [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/king|king]] who**wanted to **settle accounts with his [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/servant|servants]]**. One of his servants owed a huge debt worth 200,000 years’ wages.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**The kingdom of God is like**  - Another way to say this would be, “God's rule over people is like” or, “The way God rules people can be compared to.”
    * 


**is like a king who**  - This could be translated as, “is like the kingdom of a king who” or, “can be compared with the rule of a king who.”
    * 


**settle accounts with his servants**  - That is, “collect the debts his servants owed him” or, “collect the money his servants had borrowed from him.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__29-01|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/29-the-story-of-the-unmerciful-servant|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__29-03|>>]]**


===== Not Able to Repay [29-03] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-29-03.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=94e987?nolink&640x360}}


“Since the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/servant|servant]]** could not **pay the debt**, the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/king|king]]** said, ‘Sell this man and his family as **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/servant|slaves]]****to make payment on his debt**.’”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


(Jesus continues the story.)


    * 


**pay the debt**  - That is, “pay back the money he owed to the king.”
    * 


**to make payment on his debt**  - This could be translated as, “and use the money received from selling them to pay part of what he owes me.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__29-02|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/29-the-story-of-the-unmerciful-servant|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__29-04|>>]]**


===== The Debt Is Canceled [29-04] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-29-04.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=f07fa4?nolink&640x360}}


“The **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/servant|servant]]****fell on his knees**  **before the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/king|king]]** and said, ‘Please be patient with me, and I will pay the full amount that I owe you.’ The king **felt pity**  for the servant, so he **canceled all of his debt**  and let him go.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


(Jesus continues the story.)


    * 


**fell on his knees**  - That is, “quickly knelt down on the ground.” This was a way to show his humility and his desire for the king to help him. Make sure it doesn't sound like he fell down accidentally.
    * 


**before the king**  - This means, “in front of the king.”
    * 


**felt pity**  - That is, “felt compassion for” or, “felt sorry for.” The king knew that the servant and his family would suffer greatly if they were sold into slavery.
    * 


**canceled all of his debt**  - This can be translated as, “said that the servant did not need to pay back any of the money that he owed the king.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__29-03|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/29-the-story-of-the-unmerciful-servant|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__29-05|>>]]**


===== The Small Debt [29-05] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-29-05.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=c82961?nolink&640x360}}


“But when the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/servant|servant]]** went out from the king, he found a **fellow servant**  who owed him a debt worth four months’ wages. The servant grabbed his fellow servant and said, ‘Pay me the money that you owe me!’”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


(Jesus continues the story.)


    * 


**fellow servant**  - This refers to another man who was also a servant of the king.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__29-04|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/29-the-story-of-the-unmerciful-servant|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__29-06|>>]]**


===== To Prison [29-06] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-29-06.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=2191f4?nolink&640x360}}


“The **fellow [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/servant|servant]]****fell on his knees**  and said, ‘Please be patient with me, and I will pay the full amount that I owe you.’ But instead, the servant **threw his fellow servant into prison**  until he could pay the debt.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


(Jesus continues the story.)


    * 


**fellow servant**  - Translate this phrase in the same way as in **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__29-05|[29-05]]]**.
    * 


**fell on his knees**  - This phrase has the same meaning as in **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__29-04|[29-04]]]**.
    * 


**threw his fellow servant into prison**  - This could also be translated as, “had the man put into prison.” The word “threw” is figurative and means it was done in a forceful way.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__29-05|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/29-the-story-of-the-unmerciful-servant|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__29-07|>>]]**


===== The King Heard [29-07] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-29-07.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=55c5d8?nolink&640x360}}


“Some other **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/servant|servants]]** saw **what had happened**  and **were greatly disturbed**. They went to the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/king|king]]** and told him **everything**.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


(Jesus continues the story.)


    * 


**what had happened**  - That is, “that the servant had refused to cancel the other servant's debt and had put him into prison.”
    * 


**were greatly disturbed**  - That is, “deeply grieved” or, “very distressed.”
    * 


**everything**–That is, “they told the king what the servant had done to his fellow servant.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__29-06|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/29-the-story-of-the-unmerciful-servant|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__29-08|>>]]**


===== The Wicked Servant [29-08] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-29-08.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=8c7b70?nolink&640x360}}


“The **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/king|king]]****called the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/servant|servant]]** and said, ‘You wicked servant! I **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/forgive|forgave]]** your debt because you **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/beg|begged]] me**. **You should have done the same**.’ The king was so angry that he **threw**  the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/evil|wicked]]** servant into prison until he could pay back all of his debt.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


(Jesus continues the story.)


    * 


**called the servant**  - That is, “commanded the servant to come to him” or, “ordered his guards to bring the servant to him.”
    * 


**begged me**  – This could be translated as, “pleaded with me” or, “urgently asked me to be merciful.”
    * 


**You should have done the same**  - That is, “You should have forgiven the man who owed you, just as I forgave you.”
    * 


**threw**  - That is, “commanded his guards to put.” Consider how “threw” was translated in frame **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__29-06|[29-06]]]**.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__29-07|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/29-the-story-of-the-unmerciful-servant|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__29-09|>>]]**


===== Forgive Your Brother [29-09] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-29-09.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=06492a?nolink&640x360}}


**Then [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]] said**, “**This**  is what **my [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god-father|heavenly Father]]** will do to every one of you if you do not **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/forgive|forgive]]****your brother**  **from your heart**.”


//A Bible story from: Matthew 18:21-35//


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**Then Jesus said**  – Some languages may add, “to his disciples.”
    * 


**This**  - “This” refers back to the way the king punished the unforgiving servant in **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__29-08|[29-08]]]**.
    * 


**my heavenly Father**  - That is, “my Father in heaven.” Jesus is expressing his unique, personal relationship to God the Father.
    * 


**your brother**  - See how you translated this in **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__29-01|[29-01]]]**.
    * 


**from your heart**  - That is, “with sincerity” or, “truly” or, “genuinely” or, “honestly.”
    * 


//A Bible story from//  - These references may be slightly different in some Bible translations.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__29-08|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/29-the-story-of-the-unmerciful-servant|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__30-01|>>]]**


===== A Quiet Place [30-01] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-30-01.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=b6e8fb?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** sent his **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/apostle|apostles]]** to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/preach|preach]]** and to teach people in many different villages. When they returned to where Jesus was, they told him what they had done. Then Jesus invited them to go with him to a **quiet place**  across the lake to rest for a while. So, they got into a boat and went to the other side of the lake.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**quiet place**  - This refers to a place with few people where they could be by themselves.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__29-09|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/30-jesus-feeds-five-thousand-people|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__30-02|>>]]**


===== The Crowd Followed Jesus [30-02] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-30-02.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=52b9da?nolink&640x360}}


But there were many people who saw **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** and the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/disciple|disciples]]** leave in the boat to cross the lake. These people ran along the shore of the lake to get to the other side ahead of them. So when Jesus and the disciples **arrived**, a large group of people was already there, waiting for them.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**arrived**  - That is, “got to the other side of the lake” or, “got there.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__30-01|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/30-jesus-feeds-five-thousand-people|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__30-03|>>]]**


===== Jesus Taught and Healed People [30-03] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-30-03.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=dd0a54?nolink&640x360}}


The crowd had over 5,000 men in it, **not counting the women and children**. **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** felt great compassion towards the people. **To Jesus**, these people were **like [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sheep|sheep]] without a [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/shepherd|shepherd]]**. So he taught them and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/heal|healed]]** the people among them who were sick.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**not counting the women and children**  - That is, “not counting the women and children who were with them” or, “and there were also women and children in addition to the men.” Another way to translate this could also be, “in addition, there were many women and children.”
    * 


**To Jesus**  – That is, “Jesus knew that” or, “Jesus understood that.”
    * 


**like sheep without a shepherd**  - This could be translated as, “vulnerable and lost, just like sheep are when they have no shepherd to take care of them.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__30-02|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/30-jesus-feeds-five-thousand-people|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__30-04|>>]]**


===== The People Were Hungry [30-04] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-30-04.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=5686c5?nolink&640x360}}


**Late in the day**, the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/disciple|disciples]]** told **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]**, “It is late and there are no towns nearby. **Send the people away**  so they can go get something to eat.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**Late in the day**  - This could also be translated as, “When it was almost evening.”
    * 


**Send the people away**  - This could be translated as, “Please tell the people to go to a town” or, “Shouldn't you tell the people to go somewhere?” or, “Let the people go to a town.” Make sure it sounds like a polite request, not an order.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__30-03|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/30-jesus-feeds-five-thousand-people|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__30-05|>>]]**


===== Five Loaves and Two Fish [30-05] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-30-05.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=95d536?nolink&640x360}}


But **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** said to the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/disciple|disciples]]**, “You give them something to eat!” They responded, “**How can we do that?**  We only have five loaves of bread and two small fish.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**How can we do that?**  – This could be translated as, “We cannot do that!” or, “It is impossible to do that!” The disciples were not asking an actual question. Rather, they were strongly expressing that they did not think this was possible.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__30-04|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/30-jesus-feeds-five-thousand-people|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__30-06|>>]]**


===== Preparation for the Meal [30-06] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-30-06.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=0e5518?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** told his **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/disciple|disciples]]** to tell the people in the crowd to sit down on the grass, in groups of fifty people each.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


//(There are no notes for this frame.)// 
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__30-05|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/30-jesus-feeds-five-thousand-people|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__30-07|>>]]**


===== Jesus Blessed the Food [30-07] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-30-07.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=daf782?nolink&640x360}}


Then **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** took the five loaves of bread and the two fish, looked up to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/heaven|heaven]]**, and thanked **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** for the food.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


//(There are no notes for this frame.)// 
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__30-06|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/30-jesus-feeds-five-thousand-people|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__30-08|>>]]**


===== Everyone Ate [30-08] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-30-08.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=5626cb?nolink&640x360}}


Then **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]****broke the bread and the fish**  into pieces. He gave the pieces to his **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/disciple|disciples]]** to give to the people. The disciples kept passing out the food, and **it never ran out**! All the people ate and **were satisfied**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**broke the bread and the fish**  - That is, “tore the bread and the fish.”
    * 


**it never ran out**  – Another way to say this would be, “there was always more left.”
    * 


**were satisfied**  – That is, “were no longer hungry” or, “were not hungry any more.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__30-07|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/30-jesus-feeds-five-thousand-people|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__30-09|>>]]**


===== More than Enough [30-09] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-30-09.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=ff2f1f?nolink&640x360}}


After that, the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/disciple|disciples]]** collected the food that had not been eaten and it was enough to fill twelve baskets! All the food came from the five loaves of bread and two fish.


//A Bible story from: Matthew 14:13-21; Mark 6:31-44; Luke 9:10-17; John 6:5-15//


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


//A Bible story from//  - These references may be slightly different in some Bible translations.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__30-08|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/30-jesus-feeds-five-thousand-people|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__31-01|>>]]**


===== Jesus Prayed Alone [31-01] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-31-01.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=135b26?nolink&640x360}}


Then **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** told the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/disciple|disciples]]** to get into the boat and sail to the other side of the lake while **he dismissed the crowd**. After Jesus had sent the crowd away, he went up on a **mountainside**  to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/pray|pray]]**. Jesus was there all alone, and he prayed until late at night.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**he dismissed the crowd**  - This is another way of saying, “he sent the crowd on their way” or, “he told the crowd of people to go back to their homes.”
    * 


**mountainside**  - That is, “the side of a mountain.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__30-09|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/31-jesus-walks-on-water|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__31-02|>>]]**


===== The Storm [31-02] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-31-02.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=e85f3d?nolink&640x360}}


**Meanwhile**, the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/disciple|disciples]]** were **rowing their boat**, but by late in the night they had only traveled as far as the middle of the lake. They were rowing with **great difficulty**  because the wind was blowing hard against them.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**Meanwhile**  - That is, “while Jesus was praying on the mountainside.”
    * 


**rowing their boat**  - The boat had a sail, but it would not have worked when the wind was against them.
    * 


**great difficulty**  - That is, “much difficulty” or, “a lot of difficulty.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__31-01|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/31-jesus-walks-on-water|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__31-03|>>]]**


===== Jesus Walked on the Water [31-03] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-31-03.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=a0f062?nolink&640x360}}


Then **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** finished praying and went to the disciples. He walked on top of the water across the lake toward their boat!


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


//(There are no notes for this frame.)// 
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__31-02|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/31-jesus-walks-on-water|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__31-04|>>]]**


===== The Disciples Were Afraid [31-04] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-31-04.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=b82c7e?nolink&640x360}}


The **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/disciple|disciples]]** were very afraid when they saw **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]**, because they thought they were seeing **a ghost**. Jesus knew that they were afraid, so he called out to them and said, “**Do not be afraid**. **It is I!**”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**a ghost**  - That is, “a spirit.” They thought Jesus was a spirit, since normally a human being cannot walk on water.
    * 


**Do not be afraid**  – For some languages it may be more natural to say here, “Stop being afraid.”
    * 


**it is I!**  - For some, it might be more natural to translate this as, “It is me, Jesus.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__31-03|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/31-jesus-walks-on-water|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__31-05|>>]]**


===== Jesus Called Peter [31-05] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-31-05.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=2a5a6e?nolink&640x360}}


Then **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/peter|Peter]]** said to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]**, “**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/lord|Master]]**, **if it is you**, command me to come to you on the water.” Jesus told Peter, “**Come!**”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**if it is you**  - That is, “if it is really you, and not a ghost.”
    * 


**Come!**  - That is, “Come here” or, “Come to me” or, “Come, walk to me.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__31-04|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/31-jesus-walks-on-water|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__31-06|>>]]**


===== Peter Walked on the Water [31-06] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-31-06.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=ba8386?nolink&640x360}}


So, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/peter|Peter]]** got out of the boat and started walking to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** on the surface of the water. But after walking a short distance, he **turned his eyes away from**  Jesus and began to look at the waves and to feel the strong wind.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**turned his eyes away from**  - This expression means, “looked away from.” It could also be translated as, “stopped looking at.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__31-05|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/31-jesus-walks-on-water|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__31-07|>>]]**


===== Peter Sank [31-07] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-31-07.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=7aa1e7?nolink&640x360}}


Then **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/peter|Peter]]** became afraid and began to sink in the water. He cried out, “**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/lord|Master]]**, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/save|save]]** me!” **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** reached out right away and grabbed him. Then he said to Peter, “**You man of little [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/faith|faith]]**, **why did you doubt**?”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**You man of little faith**  - This may also be translated as, “You have so little faith in me!” or, “You do not trust me very much!”
    * 


**why did you doubt?**  - That is, “You should not have doubted me!” or, “You should have trusted me completely.” This isn't a real question, but a way in this language to make a strong point. In many languages, it works better to express this as a statement.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__31-06|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/31-jesus-walks-on-water|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__31-08|>>]]**


===== The Son of God [31-08] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-31-08.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=50a5c3?nolink&640x360}}


**When [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/peter|Peter]] and [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]] got into the boat, the wind**immediately stopped blowing and the water became calm. The **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/disciple|disciples]]** were amazed. They **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/worship|worshiped]]** Jesus, saying to him, “**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/true|Truly]], you are the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god-son|Son of God]]**.”


//A Bible story from: Matthew 14:22-33; Mark 6:45-52; John 6:16-21//


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**When Peter and Jesus got into the boat, the wind**  – It may be better to say, “Peter and Jesus got into the boat, and then the wind.”
    * 


**worshiped Jesus**  – This could be translated as, “bowed down and worshiped Jesus.” This word has the idea of physically bowing down in front of someone out of respect and reverence.
    * 


**Truly you are the Son of God**  – Other ways to say this would be, “You really are the Son of God” or, “It really is true that you are the Son of God.”
    * 


//A Bible story from//  - These references may be slightly different in some Bible translations.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__31-07|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/31-jesus-walks-on-water|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__32-01|>>]]**


===== The Country of the Gerasenes [32-01] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-32-01.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=b0eb5c?nolink&640x360}}


**One day**, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** and his **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/disciple|disciples]]** went in a boat across the lake to the region where **the Gerasene people**  lived.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**One day**  - This phrase introduces an event that happened in the past, but does not state the specific time. Many languages have a similar way to begin telling a true story.
    * 


**the Gerasene people**  - The Gerasenes lived in an area along the eastern shore of the Sea of Galilee. They are descendants of the Jews, but we know few details about them.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__31-08|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/32-jesus-heals-a-demon-possessed-man|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__32-02|>>]]**


===== A Man with Evil Spirits [32-02] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-32-02.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=886325?nolink&640x360}}


When they reached the other side of the lake, **a [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/demon-possessed|demon-possessed]] man****came running up to**  **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**a demon-possessed man**  - That is, “a man who had demons in him” or, “a man who was controlled by evil spirits.”
    * 


**came running up to**  - That is, “ran to” or, “ran and stopped in front of.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__32-01|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/32-jesus-heals-a-demon-possessed-man|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__32-03|>>]]**


===== Breaking the Chains [32-03] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-32-03.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=46d64b?nolink&640x360}}


This man was so strong that nobody could control him. People had even **fastened**  his arms and legs with chains, but he **kept breaking them**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**fastened his arms and legs**  - That is, “restrained” or, “bound.”
    * 


**kept breaking them**  - Some languages may need to say, “kept breaking the chains.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__32-02|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/32-jesus-heals-a-demon-possessed-man|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__32-04|>>]]**


===== Living among the Tombs [32-04] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-32-04.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=d4379d?nolink&640x360}}


The man lived **among the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/tomb|tombs]]** in the area. This man would scream all day and all night. He did not wear clothes and cut himself repeatedly with stones.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**among the tombs**  - That is “near the tombs” or, “around the tombs.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__32-03|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/32-jesus-heals-a-demon-possessed-man|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__32-05|>>]]**


===== Jesus Commanded the Demons [32-05] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-32-05.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=8882d0?nolink&640x360}}


When the man came to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]**, he **fell on his knees**  in front of him. Jesus said to the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/demon|demon]]**, “Come out of this man!”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**fell on his knees**  - That is, “quickly knelt down on the ground.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__32-04|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/32-jesus-heals-a-demon-possessed-man|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__32-06|>>]]**


===== My Name Is Legion [32-06] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-32-06.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=4b78d1?nolink&640x360}}


The **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/demon-possessed|man with the demon]]****cried out**  in a loud voice, “**What do you want with me**, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]**, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god-son|Son]]** of **the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|Most High God]]**? Please do not torture me!” Then Jesus asked the demon, “What is your name?” **He replied**, “My name is **Legion**, because **we are many**.” (A “legion” was a group of several thousand soldiers in the Roman army.)


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**cried out**  – That is, “shouted” or, “exclaimed.”
    * 


**What do you want with me**  - This expression means, “What are you going to do to me?”
    * 


**the Most High God**  - That is, “the Supreme God” or, “the Most Sovereign God” or, “the Most Powerful God.” The meaning of “high” here refers to God's greatness. It does not refer to altitude or being tall.
    * 


**Legion**  - This was the name of the group of demons, but it also describes that the evil spirits were very numerous. Use the name if the note that follows will make the meaning clear in your language. If not, you may need to translate the word as something like, “Army” or, “Crowd” or, “Thousands.”
    * 


**we are many**  - we are many - That is, “there are many of us” or, “we are many demons.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__32-05|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/32-jesus-heals-a-demon-possessed-man|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__32-07|>>]]**


===== The Herd of Pigs [32-07] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-32-07.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=349460?nolink&640x360}}


The **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/demon|demons]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/beg|begged]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]**, “Please **do not send us**  out of this region!” There was a herd of pigs feeding on a nearby hill. So, the demons begged Jesus, “**Please send us**  into the pigs **instead**!” Jesus said, “**Go!**”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**do not send us**  – That is, “do not make us go.”
    * 


**Please send us**  – That is, “Please let us go.”
    * 


**instead**  - That is, “instead of making us go away.”
    * 


**Go!**  – This could be translated as, “Go into the pigs!” or, “You may go into the pigs!”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__32-06|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/32-jesus-heals-a-demon-possessed-man|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__32-08|>>]]**


===== The Pigs Drowned [32-08] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-32-08.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=462008?nolink&640x360}}


The **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/demon|demons]]** came out of the man and entered the pigs. The pigs ran down a steep bank into the lake and drowned. There were about 2,000 pigs in the **herd**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**herd**  - That is, “herd of pigs” or, “group of pigs.” Many languages have specific names for groups of animals, such as “flock of sheep,” “herd of cattle,” “pack of dogs,” and “school of fish.” Use a word that can appropriately be used for a large group of pigs.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__32-07|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/32-jesus-heals-a-demon-possessed-man|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__32-09|>>]]**


===== The Man Was Healed [32-09] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-32-09.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=31f07d?nolink&640x360}}


When the people who took care of the pigs saw **what happened**, they ran into the town and told everyone that they met what **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** had done. The people from the town came and saw the man **who used to have the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/demon|demons]]**. He was sitting calmly, wearing clothes, and acting like a normal person.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**what happened**  - That is, “how Jesus sent the demons out of the man and into the pigs.”
    * 


**who used to have the demons**  – That is, “in whom the demons had lived” or, “who had been controlled by the evil spirits.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__32-08|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/32-jesus-heals-a-demon-possessed-man|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__32-10|>>]]**


===== Jesus Left [32-10] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-32-10.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=57c759?nolink&640x360}}


The **people**  were very **afraid**  and asked **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** to leave. So Jesus got into the boat and **prepared**  to leave. The man who used to have the demons **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/beg|begged]] to go along with Jesus**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**people**  – Some languages may prefer to say, “people from that region” or, “the Gerasene people.”
    * 


**afraid**  – It may be better to say, “afraid because of what Jesus had done.”
    * 


**prepared**  – That is, “was getting ready.”
    * 


**begged to go along with Jesus**  - That is, “begged Jesus to let him go with him” or, “earnestly asked Jesus if he could go with him.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__32-09|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/32-jesus-heals-a-demon-possessed-man|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__32-11|>>]]**


===== Go Home [32-11] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-32-11.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=32af3d?nolink&640x360}}


But **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** said to him, “No, I want you to go home and tell your friends and family about everything that **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** has done for you and **how he has had [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/mercy|mercy]] on you**.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**how he has had mercy on you**  - This can be translated as, “how he has shown mercy to you” or, “that he has been merciful to you.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__32-10|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/32-jesus-heals-a-demon-possessed-man|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__32-12|>>]]**


===== The Testimony of the Man [32-12] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-32-12.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=0bf404?nolink&640x360}}


So the man went away and told everyone about what **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** had done for him. Everyone who **heard his story**  **was filled with wonder and amazement**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**heard his story**  – That is, “heard the man tell what had happened to him.”
    * 


**was filled with wonder and amazement**  - The words “amazement” and “wonder” are similar in meaning. They are used together to emphasize how amazed the people were. This could be translated as, “completely astonished about what he told them.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__32-11|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/32-jesus-heals-a-demon-possessed-man|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__32-13|>>]]**


===== The Sick Woman [32-13] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-32-13.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=c6b16f?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** returned to the other side of the lake. After he arrived there, a large crowd gathered around him and **pressed in on him**. In the crowd was a woman who had suffered from a bleeding problem for twelve years. She had paid all of her money to doctors so they would **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/heal|heal]]** her, but **she only got worse**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**pressed in on him**  - That is, “pushed tightly against him” or, “crowded in tightly around him.”
    * 


**she only got worse**  - That is, “her condition only got worse” or, ” her health got worse instead of better” or, “instead she became more sick.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__32-12|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/32-jesus-heals-a-demon-possessed-man|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__32-14|>>]]**


===== The Woman Was Healed [32-14] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-32-14.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=70ad86?nolink&640x360}}


She had heard that **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** had **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/heal|healed]]** many sick people and thought, “**I'm sure that if I can just touch Jesus’ clothes, then I will be healed, too!**” So she came up behind Jesus and touched his clothes. As soon as she touched them, the bleeding stopped!


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


//(There are no notes for this frame.)// 
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__32-13|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/32-jesus-heals-a-demon-possessed-man|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__32-15|>>]]**


===== Who Touched Me? [32-15] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-32-15.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=d8a991?nolink&640x360}}


Immediately, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** realized that **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/power|power]] had gone out from him**. So he turned around and asked, “Who touched me?” The **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/disciple|disciples]]** replied, “There are many people crowding around you and bumping into you. **Why did you ask, ‘Who touched me?’**”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**power had gone out from him**  - This may be translated as, “healing power had flowed from him into someone else” or, “his power had healed someone.” Jesus did not lose any power because of this.
    * 


**Why did you ask, ‘Who touched me?’**  - In some languages it may be better to use an indirect quote here such as, “Why did you ask who was touching you?” or, “Why you are wondering who touched you?”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__32-14|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/32-jesus-heals-a-demon-possessed-man|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__32-16|>>]]**


===== Healed by Faith [32-16] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-32-16.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=9a148d?nolink&640x360}}


The woman **fell on her knees**  **before [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]**, **shaking and very afraid**. Then she told him what she had done, and that she had been healed. Jesus said to her, “**Your [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/faith|faith]] has [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/heal|healed]] you**. Go in **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/peace|peace]]**.”


//A Bible story from: Matthew 8:28-34; 9:20-22; Mark 5:1-20; 5:24b-34; Luke 8:26-39; 8:42b-48//


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**fell on her knees**  – That is, “quickly knelt down.”
    * 


**before Jesus**  – That is, “in front of Jesus.”
    * 


**shaking and very afraid**  - That is, “shaking with fear” or, “trembling because she was afraid.”
    * 


**Your faith has healed you.**  - This could also be translated as, “You have been healed because of your faith.”
    * 


**Go in peace.**  - People spoke this traditional blessing when they left each other. Other languages may say something similar such as, “Go well”, “Go with God” or, “Peace.” Other ways of translating it could be, “May you have peace as you go” or, “Go and know that all is well between us.”
    * 


//A Bible story from//  - These references may be slightly different in some Bible translations.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__32-15|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/32-jesus-heals-a-demon-possessed-man|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__33-01|>>]]**


===== Jesus Taught the Crowds [33-01] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-33-01.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=d07345?nolink&640x360}}


**One day**, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** was teaching a very large crowd of people near the shore of the lake. So many people came to hear him that Jesus got into a boat at the edge of the water in order to have enough space to speak to them. He sat in the boat and taught the people.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**One day**  - This phrase introduces an event that happened in the past, but does not state the specific time. Many languages have a similar way to begin telling a true story.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__32-16|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/33-the-story-of-the-farmer|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__33-02|>>]]**


===== The Seed on the Path [33-02] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-33-02.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=f16e64?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** told this story. “A farmer went out to plant **some seed**. As he was **spreading the seeds by hand**, some seeds happened to fall on the path, and the birds came and ate all of those seeds.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**spreading the seeds by hand**  - That is, “throwing the seeds on the soil” or, “covering all of his crop soil with seeds.” This is the way that farmers in the ancient Middle East typically planted grain-bearing crops.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__33-01|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/33-the-story-of-the-farmer|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__33-03|>>]]**


===== The Seed on the Rocks [33-03] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-33-03.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=a7bcfc?nolink&640x360}}


“Other seeds fell on **rocky ground**, where there was very little soil. The seeds in the rocky ground sprouted quickly, but their roots were not able to go deep into the soil. When the sun came up and it got hot, the plants withered and died.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


(Jesus continues the story.)


    * 


**rocky ground**  - That is, “ground that was full of rocks.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__33-02|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/33-the-story-of-the-farmer|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__33-04|>>]]**


===== The Seed in the Thorns [33-04] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-33-04.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=56b634?nolink&640x360}}


“Still other seeds fell among thorn bushes. Those seeds began to grow, but **the thorns**  **choked them out**. So the plants that grew from the seeds in the **thorny ground**  did not produce any grain.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


(Jesus continues the story.)


    * 


**the thorns**  – That is, “the thorn plants” or, “the thorn bushes.”
    * 


**choked them out**  - This can also be translated as, “overshadowed them” or, “crowded them out.”
    * 


**thorny ground**  - That is, “ground that was covered with thorny bushes.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__33-03|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/33-the-story-of-the-farmer|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__33-05|>>]]**


===== The Seed in Good Soil [33-05] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-33-05.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=16c6f5?nolink&640x360}}


“Other seeds fell into **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/good|good]] soil**. These seeds grew up and produced 30, 60, or even 100 times as much grain as the seed that had been planted. **He who has ears, let him hear!**”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


(Jesus continues the story.)


    * 


**good soil**  – That is, “fertile soil” or, “soil that was good for growing plants.”
    * 


**He who has ears, let him hear!**  - This saying means, “Everyone who hears what I am saying should listen to me carefully” or, “If anyone hears what I have said, he should pay attention to what I mean.” This can also be translated as a command. “Since you have ears to hear, listen carefully to what I am saying.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__33-04|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/33-the-story-of-the-farmer|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__33-06|>>]]**


===== The Seed Is the Word [33-06] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-33-06.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=5f5272?nolink&640x360}}


**This story confused the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/disciple|disciples]]**. So **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** explained, “The seed is the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/word-of-god|word of God]]**. The path **is a person**  who hears God’s word, but does not understand it, and the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/satan|devil]]****takes the word away from him**.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**This story confused the disciples.**  - That is, “The disciples did not understand this story.”
    * 


**is a person**  - This comparison can also be translated as, “is like a person” or, “represents a person” or, “refers to a person” or, “is speaking about a person.”
    * 


**takes the word away from him**  - This may also be translated as, “takes God's word away, causing him to forget it” or, “steals the word from his heart so he won't believe it and be saved.” You may also add the following: “just as birds eat up the seeds that fall on a path.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__33-05|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/33-the-story-of-the-farmer|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__33-07|>>]]**


===== Persecution and Hardship [33-07] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-33-07.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=dc6271?nolink&640x360}}


“The **rocky ground**  **is a person**  who hears **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/word-of-god|God’s word]]** and **accepts it with [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/joy|joy]]**. But when he experiences hardship or **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/persecute|persecution]]**, he **falls away**.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


(Jesus continues to explain the story.)


    * 


**rocky ground**  - See how you translated this term in **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__33-03|[33-03]]]**.
    * 


**is a person**  - See how you translated this comparison in **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__33-06|[33-06]]]**.
    * 


**accepts it with joy**  - That is, “believes it joyfully” or, “joyfully agrees that it is true.”
    * 


**falls away**  - That is, “no longer follows God or obeys him” or, “stops following or obeying God.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__33-06|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/33-the-story-of-the-farmer|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__33-08|>>]]**


===== The Desire for Riches [33-08] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-33-08.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=0f8f9d?nolink&640x360}}


“The **thorny ground**  **is a person**  who hears **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/word-of-god|God’s word]]**, but as time passes, the **cares**, **riches**, and **pleasures of life**  **choke out**  his **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/love|love]]** for **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]**. As a result, the teaching he heard **does not produce fruit**.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


(Jesus continues to explain the story.)


    * 


**thorny ground**  - See how you translated this term in **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__33-04|[33-04]]]**.
    * 


**is a person**  - See how you translated this comparison in **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__33-06|[33-06]]]**.
    * 


**cares**  - That is, “concerns” or, “needs” or, “problems.”
    * 


**riches**  - That is, “desire for wealth.”
    * 


**pleasures of life**  - This could also be translated as, “doing things to get pleasure” or, “focusing on things that give pleasure.”
    * 


**choke out**  - That is, “squelch” or, “destroy” or, “overcome.” This phrase could also be translated as, “cause him to stop loving God.”
    * 


**does not produce fruit**  - That is, “does not produce spiritual fruit” or “does not behave in a way that shows God's Spirit is working in him.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__33-07|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/33-the-story-of-the-farmer|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__33-09|>>]]**


===== Spiritual Fruit [33-09] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-33-09.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=64eda4?nolink&640x360}}


“But the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/good|good]] soil****is a person**  who hears the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/word-of-god|word of God]]**, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/believe|believes]]** it, and **produces fruit**.”


//A Bible story from: Matthew 13:1-8, 18-23; Mark 4:1-8, 13-20; Luke 8:4-15//


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


(Jesus continues to explain the story.)


    * 


**good soil**  - See how you translated this term in **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__33-05|[33-05]]]**.
    * 


**is a person**  - See how you translated this comparison in **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__33-06|[33-06]]]**.
    * 


**produce fruit**  - See how you translated this phrase in **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__33-08|[33-08]]]**.
    * 


//A Bible story from//  - These references may be slightly different in some Bible translations.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__33-08|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/33-the-story-of-the-farmer|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__34-01|>>]]**


===== The Mustard Seed [34-01] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-34-01.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=8b3983?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** told many other **stories**  about the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/kingdom-of-god|kingdom of God]]**. For example, he said, “The kingdom of God is like a **mustard seed**  that someone planted in his field. You know that the mustard seed is **the smallest seed of all**.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**stories**  - Jesus used these stories to teach truths about God's kingdom. It is not clear if the events actually happened or not. If your language has a term that includes both fictional and real stories, you should use it here.
    * 


**mustard seed**  - This probably refers to the seed of the black mustard plant, which has tiny seeds that rapidly grow into very large plants. If there is a word for this plant in your language, you should use it. If not, you may need to substitute the name of another plant which has the same characteristics.
    * 


**the smallest seed of all**  - That is, “the smallest of all the seeds that people plant.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__33-09|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/34-jesus-teaches-other-stories|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__34-02|>>]]**


===== The Large Tree [34-02] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-34-02.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=e14023?nolink&640x360}}


“But when the **mustard seed**  **grows**, it becomes the largest of all of the **garden plants**, big enough that even the birds come and **rest in**  its branches.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


(Jesus continues the story.)


    * 


**mustard seed**  - See how you translated this term in **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__34-01|[34-01]]]**.
    * 


**grows**  – You may want to add, “into a mature plant.”
    * 


**garden plants**  – This can also be translated as, “plants that would be planted in a garden.”
    * 


**rest in**  - This may also be translated as, “sit on” or, “perch on.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__34-01|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/34-jesus-teaches-other-stories|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__34-03|>>]]**


===== The Yeast [34-03] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-34-03.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=1df05e?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** told another **story**, “The **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/kingdom-of-god|kingdom of God]]** is like **yeast**  that a woman mixes into some **bread dough**  until **it spreads throughout the dough**.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    *
