**story**  - See how you translated this term in **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__34-01|[34-01]]]**.
    * 


**yeast**  - This can also be translated as, “leaven” or, “the little bit of leaven.” It is added to bread dough to make it rise. A little bit of yeast can be mixed into a large amount of dough and make the whole batch of dough rise.
    * 


**bread dough**  - This is a mixture of flour and liquid that can be shaped and baked into bread. If you do not have words for dough or flour, you can borrow a word for flour or call it “ground-up grain.”
    * 


**it spreads throughout the dough**  - That is, “every part of the dough has yeast in it” or, “the yeast grows throughout all the dough.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__34-02|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/34-jesus-teaches-other-stories|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__34-04|>>]]**


===== The Treasure in the Field [34-04] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-34-04.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=5c6d2a?nolink&640x360}}


“The **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/kingdom-of-god|kingdom of God]]** is also like **treasure**  that someone hid in a field. Another man found the treasure and then **buried it again**. He was so **filled with [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/joy|joy]]** that he went and sold everything he had and used the money to **buy that field**.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


(Jesus told another story.)


    * 


**treasure**  - That is, “something that is very valuable.”
    * 


**buried it again**  - It is also possible to add, “so that no one else would find it.”
    * 


**filled with joy**  - Another way to say this is, “very happy” or, “excited.”
    * 


**buy that field**  - Some people may want to add, “so that the treasure would be his.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__34-03|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/34-jesus-teaches-other-stories|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__34-05|>>]]**


===== The Perfect Pearl [34-05] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-34-05.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=09be81?nolink&640x360}}


“The **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/kingdom-of-god|kingdom of God]]** is also like a **perfect pearl of great value**. When a **pearl merchant**  found it, he sold all that he had and used the money to buy it.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


(Jesus continues with another story about the kingdom of God.)


    * 


**perfect pearl**  – That is, “a pearl without any defects.”
    * 


**pearl**  - If pearls are unknown, this can be translated as, “beautiful stone” or, “beautiful stone-like thing.”
    * 


**of great value**  – That is, “that was very valuable” or, “that was worth a lot of money.”
    * 


**pearl merchant**  - That is, “pearl dealer” or, “pearl trader.” This refers to a person whose business is buying and selling pearls.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__34-04|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/34-jesus-teaches-other-stories|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__34-06|>>]]**


===== Two Men at the Temple [34-06] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-34-06.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=c38fca?nolink&640x360}}


Then **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** told a **story**  to some people who **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/trust|trusted]] in their own good deeds**and **despised other people**. He said, “Two men went to the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/temple|Temple]]** to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/pray|pray]]**. One of them was a **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/tax-collector|tax collector]]**, and the other was a **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jewish-leaders|religious leader]]**.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**story**  - See how you translated this term in **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__34-01|[34-01]]]**.
    * 


**trusted in their own good deeds**  - That is, “believed that their good deeds made them righteous” or, “were proud of how perfectly they kept God's law” or, “believed that their good deeds caused God to be completely pleased with them.”
    * 


**despised other people**  - That is, “considered other people to be inferior to them” or, “looked down on other people.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__34-05|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/34-jesus-teaches-other-stories|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__34-07|>>]]**


===== The Religious Leader's Prayer [34-07] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-34-07.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=9bf416?nolink&640x360}}


“**The [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jewish-leaders|religious leader]] prayed like this**, ‘Thank you, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]**, that **I am not a [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sin|sinner]] like**other men—such as robbers, **unjust men**, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/adultery|adulterers]]**, or even like that **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/tax-collector|tax collector]]**.’”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


(Jesus continues the story.)


    * 


**The religious leader prayed like this**  - Another way to say this would be, “This is how the religious leader prayed” or, “The religious leader prayed in this way.”
    * 


**I am not a sinner like**  - That is, “I am not sinful like” or, “I am righteous, not like.”
    * 


**unjust men**  - That is, “men who are not righteous” or, “people who do evil things” or, “law breakers.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__34-06|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/34-jesus-teaches-other-stories|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__34-08|>>]]**


===== I Am Good [34-08] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-34-08.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=873eb1?nolink&640x360}}


“‘For example, **I [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/fast|fast]]** two times every week and I give you **ten percent**  of all the money and goods that I receive.’”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


(Jesus continues to tell of the religious leader's prayer.)


    * 


**I fast**  - The religious ruler believed that doing this would earn favor with God.
    * 


**ten percent**  - That is, “one-tenth.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__34-07|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/34-jesus-teaches-other-stories|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__34-09|>>]]**


===== The Tax Collector's Prayer [34-09] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-34-09.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=8f97e3?nolink&640x360}}


“But the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/tax-collector|tax collector]]****stood far away**  from the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jewish-leaders|religious leader]]**, and **did not even look up to [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/heaven|heaven]]**. Instead, **he pounded on his chest with his fist**  and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/pray|prayed]]**, ‘**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]**, please be **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/mercy|merciful]]** to me because I am a **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sin|sinner]]**.’”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


(Jesus continues the story.)


    * 


**stood far away **  - This can also be translated as, “stood at a distance” or, “stayed separate.”
    * 


**did not even look up to heaven**  - The word “even” indicates that people normally looked up to heaven when praying to God, but that this man did not because he was so ashamed of his sin.
    * 


**he pounded on his chest with his fist**  - This could also be translated as, “because of his grief, he hit his chest with his fist” or, “he pounded his chest in sorrow.” If people would find this hard to understand because they beat their chest for other reasons, you could translate this as, “he showed his despair.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__34-08|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/34-jesus-teaches-other-stories|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__34-10|>>]]**


===== The Proud Will Be Humbled [34-10] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-34-10.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=b45c22?nolink&640x360}}


Then **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** said, “I tell you the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/true|truth]]**, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** heard the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/tax-collector|tax collector's]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/pray|prayer]]** and **declared him to be [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/righteous|righteous]]**. But he did not like the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jewish-leaders|religious leader's]]** prayer. God **will [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/humble|humble]]** everyone who is **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/proud|proud]]**, and he will lift up whoever **humbles himself**.”


//A Bible story from: Matthew 13:31-33, 44-46; Mark 4:30-32; Luke 13:18-21; 18:9-14//


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**declared him to be righteous**  - That is, “considered him to be a righteous person.” Even though the tax collector was a sinner, God was merciful to him because of his humility and repentance.
    * 


**will humble**  - This could also be translated as, “will give a lower status to” or, “will cause to not be important.” It could be translated figuratively as, “will bring down.”
    * 


**will lift up**  - That is, “will give a higher position to” or, “will honor.”
    * 


**humbles himself**  - That is, “chooses to behave in a humble way” or, “has a humble attitude about himself.”
    * 


//A Bible story from//  - These references may be slightly different in some Bible translations.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__34-09|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/34-jesus-teaches-other-stories|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__35-01|>>]]**


===== Jesus Taught Sinners [35-01] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-35-01.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=93c1c5?nolink&640x360}}


**One day**, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** was teaching many **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/tax-collector|tax collectors]]** and other **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sin|sinners]]** who had gathered to hear him.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**One day**  - This phrase introduces an event that happened in the past, but does not state the specific time. Many languages have a similar way to begin telling a true story.
    * 


**tax collectors**  – Tax collectors were considered to be the worst of sinners because often they stole money from people by collecting a higher tax than the government required.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__34-10|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/35-the-story-of-the-compassionate-father|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__35-02|>>]]**


===== The Religious Leaders Grumbled [35-02] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-35-02.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=857d40?nolink&640x360}}


Some **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jewish-leaders|religious leaders]]** who were also there saw **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** treating these **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sin|sinners]]** as friends, and they began to criticize him to each other. So Jesus told them this **story**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**story**  - Jesus used this story to teach truths about God's kingdom. It is not clear if the events actually happened or not. If your language has a term that includes both fictional and real stories, you should use it here.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__35-01|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/35-the-story-of-the-compassionate-father|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__35-03|>>]]**


===== The Two Sons [35-03] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-35-03.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=07e7ca?nolink&640x360}}


“There was a man who had two **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/son|sons]]**. The younger son told his father, ‘Father, I want **my [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/inherit|inheritance]]** now!’ So the father divided his **property**  between his two sons.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


(Jesus tells the story.)


    * 


**my inheritance**  – This could be translated as, “the part of your wealth that will be rightfully mine when you die.”
    * 


**property**  – That is, “wealth” or, “possessions.” This property would probably have included land, animals, and money.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__35-02|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/35-the-story-of-the-compassionate-father|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__35-04|>>]]**


===== The Younger Son [35-04] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-35-04.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=d152a3?nolink&640x360}}


“Soon the younger son gathered all that he had and went far away and **wasted his money**  in **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sin|sinful]] living**.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


(Jesus continues the story.)


    * 


**wasted his money**  - That is, “spent all his money without getting anything of value in exchange.” In some languages it can be translated as, “threw his money away” or, “ate all his money.”
    * 


**sinful living**  - That is, “doing sinful things.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__35-03|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/35-the-story-of-the-compassionate-father|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__35-05|>>]]**


===== The Famine [35-05] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-35-05.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=08dd66?nolink&640x360}}


“After that, **a severe famine happened**  in the land where the younger son was, and he had **no money to buy food**. So he took the only job he could find, **feeding pigs**. He was so miserable and hungry that he wanted to eat the pigs’ food.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


(Jesus continues the story.)


    * 


**a severe famine happened**  - That is, “there was very little food.” In some languages this might be translated as, “there was a severe famine.”
    * 


**no money to buy food**  - Because of the famine, food was very expensive, and he had already spent all of his money.
    * 


**job**  - This refers to work that he would do for someone else in exchange for money. If this is not clear, this sentence could start with, “So in order to earn some money, he took the only job.”
    * 


**feeding pigs**  - That is, “giving food to pigs.” This would have been considered as one of the lowest jobs in society at this time. If your language has a certain word for low status jobs, use that word.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__35-04|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/35-the-story-of-the-compassionate-father|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__35-06|>>]]**


===== The Son Repented [35-06] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-35-06.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=e065a8?nolink&640x360}}


“Finally, the younger son said to himself, ‘**What am I doing?**  All my father’s **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/servant|servants]]** have plenty to eat, and yet here I am starving. I will go back to my father and ask to be one of his servants.’”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


(Jesus continues the story.)


    * 


**What am I doing?**  - That is, “Why am I living like this?” or, ” I should not be living like this!” or, “It doesn't make sense for me to live like this.” The son isn't really asking a question, so some languages will have to translate this as a statement.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__35-05|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/35-the-story-of-the-compassionate-father|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__35-07|>>]]**


===== The Father's Welcome [35-07] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-35-07.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=3d17f7?nolink&640x360}}


“So the younger **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/son|son]]** started back towards his father's home. When he was **still far away**, his father saw him and **felt compassion**  for him. He ran to his son and hugged him and kissed him.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


(Jesus continues the story.)


    * 


**still far away**  – This can also be translated as, “within sight of his father's home, but still a distance away.” The son was getting close to his father's house but was still far enough away that most people in the house would not have seen him. Make sure it does not sound like he was still in a different country.
    * 


**felt compassion**  - That is, “felt deep love and pity.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__35-06|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/35-the-story-of-the-compassionate-father|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__35-08|>>]]**


===== I Have Sinned [35-08] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-35-08.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=aff356?nolink&640x360}}


“The **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/son|son]]** said, ‘Father, I have **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sin|sinned]] against [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]] and against you**. **I am not worthy**  to be your son.’”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


(Jesus continues the story.)


    * 


**sinned against God and against you**  - This could be translated as, “sinned against God, and I have also sinned against you.”
    * 


**I am not worthy**  – It is also possible to say, “So I am not worthy” or, “As a result, I am not worthy.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__35-07|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/35-the-story-of-the-compassionate-father|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__35-09|>>]]**


===== Prepare the Feast [35-09] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-35-09.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=b9267e?nolink&640x360}}


“But his father told one of his **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/servant|servants]]**, ‘Go quickly and bring the best clothes and put them on my **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/son|son]]**! Put a ring on his finger and put sandals on his feet. Then kill **the best calf**  so we can have a feast and celebrate, because **my son was [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/death|dead]], but now he is [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/life|alive]]!****He was lost, but now he is found!**’”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


(Jesus continues the story.)


    * 


**the best calf**  – This could also be translated as, “the fattest calf.” This was the calf that had been fattened so that when cooked it would taste the best.
    * 


**My son was dead, but now he is alive!**  - That is, “This is like my son was dead and is alive again!” or, “I grieved as if my son had died, but now I rejoice because it is as if he has come back to life!” The father is using this expression to show how happy he is that his son has come home.
    * 


**He was lost, but now he is is found!**  - That is, “This is like I had lost him but now I have found him.” This expression also shows how happy the father is about having his son at home again.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__35-08|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/35-the-story-of-the-compassionate-father|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__35-10|>>]]**


===== The Older Brother [35-10] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-35-10.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=dd036f?nolink&640x360}}


“So the people began to celebrate. **Before long**, the older son came home from working in the field. He heard the music and dancing and wondered what was happening.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


(Jesus continues the story.)


    * 


**Before long**  - This can also be translated as, “Soon” or, “After a little while.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__35-09|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/35-the-story-of-the-compassionate-father|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__35-11|>>]]**


===== The Brother Is Angry [35-11] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-35-11.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=f3febc?nolink&640x360}}


“When the older **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/son|son]]** found out that they were celebrating because his brother had come home, he was very angry and would not go into the house. His father came out and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/beg|begged]]** him to come and celebrate with them, but he refused.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


(Jesus continues the story.)


**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__35-10|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/35-the-story-of-the-compassionate-father|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__35-12|>>]]**


===== Working for Nothing [35-12] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-35-12.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=ad4c6f?nolink&640x360}}


“The older son said to his father, ‘All these years I have worked **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/faithful|faithfully]]** for you! I never **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/disobey|disobeyed]]** you, and still you did not even give me **one small goat**  so I could celebrate with my friends. But when **this son of yours**  who **consumed your money**  in **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sin|sinful]]** behavior came home, you **killed the best calf**  for him!’”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


(Jesus continues the story.)


    * 


**one small goat**  - A small goat would have fed fewer people than the best calf, and would not be valued as much. The older brother is complaining that his father was treating the sinful younger son better than him.
    * 


**this son of yours**  - This expression shows that the older son was angry. It shows his rejection of his younger brother and his disapproval of his father for welcoming back this wayward son. Other languages may also have an indirect way of communicating these things.
    * 


**consumed your money**  - That is, “squandered the money that you gave him” or, “devoured your wealth.” If possible, use an expression that shows the brother's anger.
    * 


**killed the best calf**  - That is, “killed the best calf to eat at a feast.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__35-11|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/35-the-story-of-the-compassionate-father|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__35-13|>>]]**


===== We Must Celebrate [35-13] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-35-13.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=2dd210?nolink&640x360}}


“The father answered, ‘My **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/son|son]]**, you are always with me, and everything I have is yours. But **it is right for us**  to celebrate, because **your brother was [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/death|dead]], but now is [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/life|alive]]**. **He was lost, but now is found!**’”


//A Bible story from: Luke 15:11-32//


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


(Jesus continues the story.)


    * 


**it is right for us**  - That is, “it is the right thing for us to do” or, “it is proper for us.”
    * 


**your brother**  - The father refers to his younger son as, “your brother” to remind the older son of his relationship to the younger son and of how he should love his younger brother.
    * 


**was dead, but now is alive**  - See how you translated this in **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__35-09|[35-09]]]**.
    * 


**He was lost, but now is found!**  - See how you translated this in **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__35-09|[35-09]]]**.
    * 


//A Bible story from//  - These references may be slightly different in some Bible translations.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__35-12|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/35-the-story-of-the-compassionate-father|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__36-01|>>]]**


===== To the Mountain [36-01] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-36-01.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=3be526?nolink&640x360}}


**One day**, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** took three of his **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/disciple|disciples]]**, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/peter|Peter]]**, **James**, and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/john|John]]** with him. (The disciple named John was not the same person who **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/baptize|baptized]]** Jesus.) They went up on a high mountain by themselves to pray.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**One day**  - This phrase introduces an event that happened in the past, but does not state the specific time. Many languages have a similar way to begin telling a true story.
    * 


**James**  - This is a different James than the one who wrote the Book of James in the Bible. To make this clear, some languages may need to use two slightly different names or to spell them differently.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__35-13|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/36-the-transfiguration|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__36-02|>>]]**


===== Jesus Was Changed [36-02] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-36-02.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=d11101?nolink&640x360}}


As **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** was praying, his face became as bright as the sun and his clothes became as white as light, **whiter**  than anyone on earth could make them.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**whiter **  - That is, “more white.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__36-01|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/36-the-transfiguration|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__36-03|>>]]**


===== Moses and Elijah [36-03] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-36-03.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=2828df?nolink&640x360}}


Then **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/moses|Moses]]** and the prophet **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/elijah|Elijah]]****appeared**. These men had lived on the earth hundreds of years before this. They talked with **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** about **his [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/death|death]], which would soon happen****in [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jerusalem|Jerusalem]]**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**appeared**  – It is also possible to say, “appeared out of nowhere.” They suddenly were there.
    * 


**his death, which would soon happen**  - This could be translated as, “how he would soon die” or, “how he would soon be killed.”
    * 


**in Jerusalem**  – Some languages may prefer to say, “in the city of Jerusalem.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__36-02|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/36-the-transfiguration|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__36-04|>>]]**


===== Peter's Comments [36-04] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-36-04.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=b2a435?nolink&640x360}}


As **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/moses|Moses]]** and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/elijah|Elijah]]** were talking with **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]**, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/peter|Peter]]** said to Jesus, “It is **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/good|good]]** for us to be here. Let us make three **shelters**, one for you, one for Moses, and one for Elijah.” Peter **did not know what he was saying**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**shelters**  - This can also be translated as, “lean-tos” or, “garden huts” or, “tents.” It refers to small, individual, temporary shelters, like the Jews made from tree branches during an annual Jewish holiday.
    * 


**did not know what he was saying**  - That is, “was speaking without understanding what was happening” or, “spoke without thinking clearly because he was so excited.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__36-03|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/36-the-transfiguration|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__36-05|>>]]**


===== This Is My Son [36-05] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-36-05.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=132d5f?nolink&640x360}}


As **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/peter|Peter]]** was talking, a bright cloud came down and surrounded them and **a voice from the cloud said**, “This is my **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god-son|Son]]** whom I **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/love|love]]**. I am pleased with him. **Listen to him**.” The three **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/disciple|disciples]]** were **terrified**  and **fell on the ground**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**a voice from the cloud said**  – This can also be translated as, “a voice spoke from the cloud saying” or, “God spoke from the cloud and said.”
    * 


**Listen to him**  – This could be translated as, “He is the one you must listen to.”
    * 


**terrified**–That is, “extremely scared.”
    * 


**fell on the ground**  – That is, “quickly bowed to the ground” or, “immediately got down on the ground.” Make sure the translation of “fell” does not sound like an accident. They probably did this intentionally out of awe and fear.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__36-04|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/36-the-transfiguration|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__36-06|>>]]**


===== Alone with Jesus [36-06] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-36-06.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=a9ebb5?nolink&640x360}}


Then **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]] touched them**and said, “**Do not be afraid**. **Get up**.” When they looked around, **the only one still there was Jesus**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**touched them**  – That is, “put his hand on them.” Some languages may prefer to specify where he touched them. If so, this could be translated as, “he touched them on the shoulder” or, “he put his hand on each one's shoulder.”
    * 


**Do not be afraid**  – This could also be translated as, “Stop being afraid.”
    * 


**Get up**  - This could also be translated as, “Stand up” or, “Please get up.” Make sure that it sounds like Jesus spoke this with kindness.
    * 


**the only one still there was Jesus**  - It is also possible to add, “Moses and Elijah had left.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__36-05|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/36-the-transfiguration|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__36-07|>>]]**


===== Keep the Secret [36-07] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-36-07.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=5b6eec?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** and the three **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/disciple|disciples]]** went back down the mountain. Then Jesus said to them, “Do not tell anyone yet about what happened here. I will soon **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/death|die]]** and then come back to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/life|life]]**. After that, you may tell people.”


//A Bible story from: Matthew 17:1-9; Mark 9:2-8; Luke 9:28-36//


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


//A Bible story from//  - These references may be slightly different in some Bible translations.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__36-06|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/36-the-transfiguration|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__37-01|>>]]**


===== Lazarus Was Sick [37-01] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-37-01.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=aa8e3b?nolink&640x360}}


**One day**, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** received a message that **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/lazarus|Lazarus]]** was very sick. Lazarus and his two sisters, **Mary**  and Martha, were close friends of Jesus. When Jesus heard this news, he said, “**This sickness will not end in [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/death|death]]**, but **it is for the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/glory|glory]] of [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]**.” Jesus **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/love|loved]]** his friends, **but he waited where he was for two days**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**One day**  - This phrase introduces an event that happened in the past, but does not state the specific time. Many languages have a similar way to begin telling a true story.
    * 


**Mary**  - Jesus' mother was also named Mary. This was a different woman.
    * 


**this sickness will not end in death**  - This can also be translated as, “the final result of this sickness will not be death” or, “Lazarus is sick, but death is not the final result of this sickness.” Jesus' disciples probably thought this meant that Lazarus would not die. But Jesus knew that, although Lazarus would die from his sickness, he would live in the end.
    * 


**it is for the glory of God**  - That is, “this will cause people to praise God for how great he is.”
    * 


**but he waited where he was for two days**  - This could be translated as, “but he stayed where he was for two days, even though they wanted him to go and heal Lazarus.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__36-07|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/37-jesus-raises-lazarus-from-the-dead|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__37-02|>>]]**


===== Back to Judea [37-02] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-37-02.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=380467?nolink&640x360}}


After the two days had passed, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** said to his **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/disciple|disciples]]**, “Let’s go back to **Judea**.” “But **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/teacher|Teacher]]**,” the disciples answered, “Just a short time ago the people there wanted to kill you!” Jesus said, “Our friend **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/lazarus|Lazarus]]****has fallen asleep, and I must wake him**.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**Judea**  - This refers to the southern section of Israel, which was settled by the tribe of Judah. Some languages will prefer to say, “the region of Judea.”
    * 


**has fallen asleep, and I must wake him.**  - Translate this phrase with the normal words for “asleep” and “wake” in your language. Although Jesus was using these words with a different meaning, the disciples did not understand that yet.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__37-01|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/37-jesus-raises-lazarus-from-the-dead|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__37-03|>>]]**


===== Lazarus Was Dead [37-03] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-37-03.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=9542bb?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus']]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/disciple|disciples]]** replied, “**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/lord|Master]]**, if **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/lazarus|Lazarus]]** is sleeping, then **he will get better**.” Then Jesus told them plainly, “**Lazarus is [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/death|dead]]**. **I am glad**  that I was not there, so that you may **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/believe|believe]]** in me.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**he will get better**  - The disciples intended this in the sense of, “there is no reason for us to go to him now, since he will get well.”
    * 


**I am glad**  - This could be translated as, “I am happy” or, “It is good that.” It does not mean he was happy that Lazarus died, but rather that he was happy that God was going to show how great he is.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__37-02|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/37-jesus-raises-lazarus-from-the-dead|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__37-04|>>]]**


===== Martha Met Jesus [37-04] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-37-04.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=4010c5?nolink&640x360}}


When **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** arrived at **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/lazarus|Lazarus']]** hometown, Lazarus had already been **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/death|dead]]** for four days. **Martha**  **went out to meet Jesus**  and said, “**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/lord|Master]]**, if only you had been here, **my brother would not have died**. But I **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/believe|believe]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]****will give you whatever you ask from him**.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**Martha**  - Martha was the sister of Lazarus and Mary. See **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__37-01|[37-01]]]**.
    * 


**went out to meet Jesus**  – That is, “went to meet Jesus as he was coming into the town.”
    * 


**my brother would not have died.**  - That is, “you would have healed my brother and he would not have died” or, “you could have prevented my brother from dying.”
    * 


**will give you whatever you ask from him**  – That is, “will do whatever you ask him to do.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__37-03|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/37-jesus-raises-lazarus-from-the-dead|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__37-05|>>]]**


===== I Am the Resurrection [37-05] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-37-05.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=8f30e8?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** replied, “**I am the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/resurrection|Resurrection]] and the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/life|Life]]**. Whoever **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/believe|believes]]** in me **will live, even though he [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/death|dies]]**. Everyone who believes in me **will never die**. Do you believe this?” **Martha**  answered, “Yes, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/lord|Master]]**! I believe you are the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/messiah|Messiah]]**, the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god-son|Son of God]]**.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**I am the Resurrection and the Life**  - This is one of several very powerful “I am” statements in which Jesus says something about his essential nature. In this one, Jesus indicated that he is the “provider” or, “source” of resurrection and life. If possible, translate this phrase in a way that makes it clear that this is his essential nature. This can also be translated as, “I am the one who resurrects people and causes them to live.”
    * 


**will live, even though he dies.**  - That is, “will live forever, even if he dies.” The English word, “he” does not only refer to men. Women who believe in Jesus will also live forever.
    * 


**Martha**  - Martha was the sister of Lazarus and Mary. See **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__37-01|[37-01]]]**.
    * 


**will never die**  - This can also be translated as, “will live forever.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__37-04|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/37-jesus-raises-lazarus-from-the-dead|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__37-06|>>]]**


===== Mary Met Jesus [37-06] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-37-06.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=458f92?nolink&640x360}}


Then **Mary**  arrived. She **fell at the feet of [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** and said, “**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/lord|Master]]**, if only you had been here, **my brother would not have [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/death|died]]**.” Jesus asked them, “Where have you put **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/lazarus|Lazarus]]**?” They told him, “In the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/tomb|tomb]]**. Come and see.” Then Jesus wept.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**Mary**  - This was the same woman as in **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__37-01|[37-01]]]**, not the mother of Jesus.
    * 


**fell at the feet of Jesus**  - That is, “knelt down at Jesus' feet” as a sign of respect.
    * 


**my brother would not have died.**  - That is, “you could have kept my brother from dying” or, “you could have prevented my brother's death” or, “my brother would still be alive.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__37-05|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/37-jesus-raises-lazarus-from-the-dead|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__37-07|>>]]**


===== Open the Tomb [37-07] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-37-07.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=5a9957?nolink&640x360}}


The **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/tomb|tomb]]** was a cave with a stone rolled in front of its opening. When **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** arrived at the tomb, **he told them**, “**Roll the stone away**.” But **Martha**  said, “**He has been [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/death|dead]] for four days**. There will be a bad smell.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**he told them**  - That is, “he told the men there.” He was probably not telling Mary and Martha to roll the stone away.
    * 


**Roll the stone away**  - Some languages may prefer to say, “Roll the stone away from the opening of the tomb.”
    * 


**Martha**  - Martha was the sister of Lazarus and Mary. See **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__37-01|[37-01]]]**.
    * 


**He has been dead for four days**  - This could also be translated as, “He died four days ago and his body is lying there.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__37-06|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/37-jesus-raises-lazarus-from-the-dead|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__37-08|>>]]**


===== Rolling the Stone Away [37-08] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-37-08.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=20ca71?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** responded, “**Did I not tell you**  that you would **see [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God's]] [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/glory|glory]]** if you **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/believe|believe]]** in me?” So they **rolled the stone away**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**Did I not tell you?**  - That is, “Remember that I told you.” Jesus is not asking this question in order to get an answer, so some languages should translate this as a command.
    * 


**see God's glory**  - That is, “see the glory of God displayed” or, “see God show how great he is.”
    * 


**rolled the stone away**  - Some languages should say, “rolled the stone away from the opening of the tomb.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__37-07|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/37-jesus-raises-lazarus-from-the-dead|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__37-09|>>]]**


===== Jesus' Prayer [37-09] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-37-09.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=c08bd3?nolink&640x360}}


Then **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** looked up to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/heaven|heaven]]** and said, “**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god-father|Father]]**, thank you for **hearing me**. I know you always listen to me, but I say this for the sake of all these people standing here, so that they will **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/believe|believe]]** you sent me.” Then Jesus shouted, “**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/lazarus|Lazarus]]**, **come out**!”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**hearing me**  – That is, “listening to me.” It may be helpful to add, “as I pray to you” or, “when I talk to you.”
    * 


**come out**  - Some languages may prefer to say, “come out of the tomb.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__37-08|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/37-jesus-raises-lazarus-from-the-dead|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__37-10|>>]]**


===== Lazarus Was Alive Again [37-10] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-37-10.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=da33c4?nolink&640x360}}


So **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/lazarus|Lazarus]] came out!** He was still wrapped in **grave clothes**. **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** told them, “Help him take off those grave clothes and release him!” Many of the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jew|Jews]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/believe|believed]]** in Jesus **because of this [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/miracle|miracle]]**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**Lazarus came out!**  - Some languages should say, “Lazarus came out of the tomb!”
    * 


**grave clothes**  - That is, “burial clothes.” This can also be translated as, “burial bandages” or, “strips of cloth.”
    * 


**because of this miracle**  – That is, “because God had done this amazing miracle” or, “because Jesus had made Lazarus come alive again.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__37-09|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/37-jesus-raises-lazarus-from-the-dead|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__37-11|>>]]**


===== The Leaders Were Jealous [37-11] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-37-11.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=2fc72e?nolink&640x360}}


But the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jewish-leaders|religious leaders]]** of the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jew|Jews]]** were **jealous**, so they **gathered together**  to plan how they could kill **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/lazarus|Lazarus]]**.


//A Bible story from: John 11:1-46//


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**jealous**  - That is, “jealous of Jesus' power and popularity” or, “jealous that so many Jews were believing in Jesus.”
    * 


**gathered together**  - That is, “met together” or, “joined together.” This was a not a casual meeting, but a meeting for a specific purpose–to plan how to kill Jesus.
    * 


//A Bible story from//  - These references may be slightly different in some Bible translations.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__37-10|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/37-jesus-raises-lazarus-from-the-dead|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__38-01|>>]]**


===== The Passover [38-01] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-38-01.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=1c6dac?nolink&640x360}}


Every year, the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jew|Jews]]** celebrated the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/passover|Passover]]**. This was a celebration of how **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** had **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/save|saved]]** their ancestors from **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/servant|slavery]]** in **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/egypt|Egypt]]****many centuries earlier**. About three years after **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** first began **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/preach|preaching]]** and teaching publicly, Jesus told his **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/disciple|disciples]]** that he wanted to celebrate this Passover with them in **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jerusalem|Jerusalem]]**, and that he would be killed there.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**many centuries earlier**  - That is, “hundreds of years earlier” or, “a very long time before.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__37-11|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/38-jesus-is-betrayed|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__38-02|>>]]**


===== Judas Made a Deal [38-02] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-38-02.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=14a51d?nolink&640x360}}


One of **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus']]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/disciple|disciples]]** was a man named **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/judas|Judas]]**. Judas was **in charge of the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/apostle|apostles']] moneybag**, but he **loved money**  and often stole money out of the bag. After Jesus and the disciples arrived in **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jerusalem|Jerusalem]]**, Judas went to the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jewish-leaders|Jewish leaders]]** and offered to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/betray|betray]]** Jesus to them in exchange for money. He knew that the Jewish leaders denied that Jesus was the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/messiah|Messiah]]** and that they were plotting to kill him.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**in charge of the apostles’ moneybag**  - That is, “responsible to hold the apostles' money” or, “responsible to hold the bag that had the disciples' money in it and to distribute funds from it.”
    * 


**loved money**  – That is, “highly valued money” or, “wanted money.” Some languages would not use the same word that can be used for “loved people.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__38-01|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/38-jesus-is-betrayed|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__38-03|>>]]**


===== Thirty Pieces of Silver [38-03] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-38-03.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=975f9f?nolink&640x360}}


The **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jewish-leaders|Jewish leaders]]**, led by the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/priest-high|high priest]]**, paid **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/judas|Judas]]****thirty silver coins**  to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/betray|betray]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]**. This happened just as the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/prophet|prophets]]** had predicted. Judas agreed, took the money, and went away. He began looking for an opportunity to help them arrest Jesus.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**thirty silver coins**  - Each of these coins were worth about four days' wages.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__38-02|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/38-jesus-is-betrayed|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__38-04|>>]]**


===== This Is My Body [38-04] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-38-04.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=c05870?nolink&640x360}}


In Jerusalem, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]****celebrated**  the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/passover|Passover]]** with his **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/disciple|disciples]]**. During the Passover meal, Jesus **took some bread**  and **broke it**. He said, “Take and eat this. **This is my body**, which is **given for you.**  **Do this to remember me.**” In this way, Jesus said that his body would be **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sacrifice|sacrificed]]** for them.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**celebrated**  – That is, “was celebrating.”
    * 


**took some bread**  – This could be translated as, “picked up a piece of bread” or, “picked up a flat loaf of bread.”
    * 


**broke it**  – Some languages should say, “tore it in pieces” or, “tore it in half” or, “tore off part of it.”
    * 


**given for you**  - This can also be translated as, “which I give for you.”
    * 


**Do this to remember me**  - That is, “Do this as a way to remind yourselves of what I am doing for you.” Jesus was referring to his death, which would happen soon.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__38-03|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/38-jesus-is-betrayed|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__38-05|>>]]**


===== This Is My Blood [38-05] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-38-05.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=96abff?nolink&640x360}}


Then **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** picked up a cup and said, “**Drink this.**  **It is my [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/blood|blood]] of the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/covenant-new|New Covenant]]** that **is poured out**  **for the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/forgive|forgiveness]] of [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sin|sins]]**. Do this to **remember me**  every time you drink it.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**a cup**  – That is, “a cup of wine” or, “a cup full of a drink made from grapes.”
    * 


**Drink this**  - That is, “Drink what is in this cup” or, “Drink from this cup.” The drink in the cup was made from grapes so that it had a deep red color.
    * 


**blood of the New Covenant**  – This could be translated as, “blood that makes the New Covenant possible” or, “blood that is the basis for the New Covenant.”
    * 


**is poured out**  - This could be translated as, “will run out of my body” or, “I will bleed out.”
    * 


**for the forgiveness of sins**  - That is, “so that God can completely forgive people for all of their sins.”
    * 


**remember me**  - That is, “celebrate me” or, “commemorate me.” It could also be translated as, “especially focus on me” or, “remind you of me.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__38-04|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/38-jesus-is-betrayed|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__38-06|>>]]**


===== The Betrayer [38-06] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-38-06.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=5c2981?nolink&640x360}}


Then **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** said to the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/disciple|disciples]]**, “One of you will **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/betray|betray]]** me.” The disciples were shocked, and asked who would do such a thing. Jesus said, “The person to whom I give this piece of bread **is the betrayer**.” Then he gave the bread to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/judas|Judas]]**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**give this piece of bread**  – That is, “hand this piece of bread.”
    * 


**is the betrayer**  - This could also be translated as, “will betray me” or, “is the one who will betray me.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__38-05|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/38-jesus-is-betrayed|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__38-07|>>]]**


===== Satan Entered Judas [38-07] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-38-07.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=6610ea?nolink&640x360}}


After **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/judas|Judas]]** took the bread, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/satan|Satan]] entered into him**. **Judas left and went**  to help the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jew|Jewish]]** leaders arrest Jesus. **It was nighttime.**


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**Satan entered into him.**  - That is, “Satan went into him” or, “Satan took control of him.”
    * 


**Judas left and went**  - Some languages may prefer to say, “Judas left the meal and went” or, “Judas left the room and went outside.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__38-06|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/38-jesus-is-betrayed|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__38-08|>>]]**


===== You Will Be Scattered [38-08] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-38-08.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=51bbba?nolink&640x360}}


After the meal, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** and his **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/disciple|disciples]]** walked to the **Mount of Olives**. Jesus said, “You will all **abandon me**  tonight. **It is written**, ‘**I will strike the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/shepherd|shepherd]]** and **all the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sheep|sheep]] will be scattered**.’”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**Mount of Olives**  - This is the name of a hill covered with olive trees, just outside the walls of the city of Jerusalem. It can also be translated as, “Olive Tree Hill.”
    * 


**abandon me**  – That is, “desert me” or, “leave me.”
    * 


**It is written**  - That is, “It is written in God's word” or, “It is written in the scriptures” or, “One of God's prophets wrote.” It is also possible to say, “What is written will happen” or, “It will be like what is written.” This prophecy refers to Jesus' death and his followers running away.
    * 


**I will strike**  - That is, “I will kill.”
    * 


**the shepherd and all the sheep**  - Do not use Jesus' name in this quote because the prophet who first wrote it would not have known the shepherd's name. Also, do not refer to the sheep being the disciples. It is best to use words that mean “shepherd” and “sheep” in your translation.
    * 


**will be scattered**  - That is, “will go away in different directions.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__38-07|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/38-jesus-is-betrayed|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__38-09|>>]]**


===== Jesus Prayed for Peter [38-09] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-38-09.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=090f93?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/peter|Peter]]** replied, “Even if all the others **abandon you**, I will not!” Then **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** said to Peter, “**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/satan|Satan]]** wants **to have all of you**, but I have **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/pray|prayed]]** for you, Peter, **that your [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/faith|faith]] will not fail**. Even so, tonight, **before the rooster crows**, you will deny that you even know me three times.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**abandon you**  – Check to see how you translated this in **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__38-08|[38-08]]]**.
    * 


**to have all of you**  - That is, “to completely control you” or, “to get you to serve him completely.” The word “you” is plural in this phrase. All of the words “you” and “your” that follow are singular.
    * 


**that your faith will not fail**  - That is, “that you will not stop believing in me.”
    * 


**before the rooster crows**  - Roosters normally crow at the first light of the new day. If that is not clear, it may be helpful to say, “Before the rooster crows at dawn tomorrow” or, “before the rooster crows tomorrow morning.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__38-08|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/38-jesus-is-betrayed|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__38-10|>>]]**


===== Peter's Promise [38-10] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-38-10.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=64c296?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/peter|Peter]]** then said to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]**, “Even if I must **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/death|die]]**, I will never **deny you**!” All the other **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/disciple|disciples]]** said the same thing.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**deny you**  - That is, “deny that I know you” or, “deny that I am your disciple” or, “disown you.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__38-09|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/38-jesus-is-betrayed|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__38-11|>>]]**


===== At Gethsemane [38-11] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-38-11.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=74dff9?nolink&640x360}}


Then **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** went with his **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/disciple|disciples]]** to **a place called Gethsemane**. Jesus told his disciples to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/pray|pray]]** that they would not **enter into [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/tempt|temptation]]**. Then Jesus went to pray **by himself**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**a place called Gethsemane**  - This could be translated as, “a nearby place called Gethsemane” or, “a place called Gethsemane at the foot of the Mount of Olives.”
    * 


**enter into temptation**  - That is, “would not sin when they were tempted” or, “would not give in to the temptation they were about to experience.”
    * 


**by himself**  – This could be translated as, “alone.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__38-10|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/38-jesus-is-betrayed|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__38-12|>>]]**


===== Your Will Be Done [38-12] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-38-12.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=c878ef?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/pray|prayed]]** three times, “**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god-father|My Father]]**, if it is possible, please let me not have to **drink this cup of [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/suffer|suffering]]**. But if there is no other way for people’s **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sin|sins]]** to be **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/forgive|forgiven]]**, then **let your will be done**.” Jesus was very troubled and **his sweat was like drops of [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/blood|blood]]**. **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** sent an **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/angel|angel]]** to strengthen him.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**drink this cup of suffering**  - That is, “go through this suffering” or, “suffer what is about to happen” or, “endure this suffering.”
    * 


**let your will be done**  - This expression means, “do what you have planned” or, “do what needs to be done.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__38-11|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/38-jesus-is-betrayed|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__38-13|>>]]**


===== The Disciples Slept [38-13] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-38-13.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=7abafb?nolink&640x360}}


**After each time of [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/pray|prayer]]**, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** came back to his **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/disciple|disciples]]**, but they were asleep. When he returned the third time, Jesus said, “Wake up! My **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/betray|betrayer]]** is here.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**After each time of prayer**  - That is, “Every time Jesus prayed that prayer.” This refers to the three times he prayed, as mentioned in **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__38-12|[38-12]]]**.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__38-12|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/38-jesus-is-betrayed|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__38-14|>>]]**


===== Judas Betrayed Jesus [38-14] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-38-14.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=5f4b1e?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/judas|Judas]]** came with the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jewish-leaders|Jewish leaders]]**, soldiers, and a large crowd. They were carrying swords and clubs. Judas **came to**  **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** and said, “**Greetings**, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/teacher|Teacher]]**,” and kissed him. This was **the sign**  for the Jewish leaders to know whom to arrest. Then Jesus said, “Judas, **do you [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/betray|betray]] me with a kiss**?”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**came to**  - Some languages may prefer to say, “went to.”
    * 


**Greetings**  - This can also be translated as, “Hello” or, “Peace” or, “Good evening.”
    * 


**the sign**  - That is, “the signal.”
    * 


**do you betray me with a kiss?**  - That is, “are you really going to betray me with a kiss?” Jesus is not looking for an answer to this question. So some languages would translate it as a statement, such as, “you are betraying me by kissing me!” or, “you make your betrayal even worse by kissing me!”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__38-13|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/38-jesus-is-betrayed|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__38-15|>>]]**


===== Peter Fought for Jesus [38-15] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-38-15.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=acf18e?nolink&640x360}}


**As the soldiers arrested [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]**, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/peter|Peter]]****pulled out his sword**  and cut off the ear of a **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/servant|servant]]** of the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/priest-high|high priest]]**. Jesus said, “Put the sword away! I could ask the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god-father|Father]]** for an army of **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/angel|angels]]** to defend me. But **I must [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/obey|obey]] my Father**.” Then Jesus **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/heal|healed]]** the man’s ear. After Jesus was arrested, all the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/disciple|disciples]]** ran away.


//A Bible story from: Matthew 26:14-56; Mark 14:10-50; Luke 22:1-53; John 12:6; 18:1-11//


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**As the soldiers arrested Jesus**  - That is, “While the soldiers were arresting Jesus.”
    * 


**pulled out his sword**  - That is, “pulled out his sword from the place where he was carrying it.”
    * 


**I must obey my Father**  - That is, “I won't do that because I must obey my Father's will and allow myself to be arrested.”
    * 


//A Bible story from//  - These references may be slightly different in some Bible translations.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__38-14|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/38-jesus-is-betrayed|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__39-01|>>]]**


===== The House of the High Priest [39-01] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-39-01.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=d9a6f4?nolink&640x360}}


It was now **the middle of the night**. The soldiers led **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** to the house of the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/priest-high|high priest]]** in order for the high priest **to question him**. **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/peter|Peter]]** followed far behind them. When Jesus was taken into the house, Peter stayed outside and warmed himself by a fire.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**the middle of the night**  - This expression means, “halfway through the night” or, “very late at night.”
    * 


**to question him**  – That is, “to ask Jesus questions to try to find something they could accuse Jesus of doing wrong.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__38-15|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/39-jesus-is-put-on-trial|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__39-02|>>]]**


===== The False Witnesses [39-02] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-39-02.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=26ba6c?nolink&640x360}}


Inside the house, the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jewish-leaders|Jewish leaders]]****put [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]] on trial**. They brought many false **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/witness|witnesses]]** who **lied about him**. However, **their statements did not agree with each other**, so the Jewish leaders could not prove **he was [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/guilt|guilty]] of anything**. Jesus did not say anything.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**put Jesus on trial**  – This could be translated as, “had a formal meeting to accuse Jesus of doing something wrong.” Usually a trial is done to find out if someone is innocent or guilty of a certain crime. In this case, the leaders were determined to make Jesus seem guilty.
    * 


**lied about him**  - That is, “told lies about him” or, “falsely accused him of doing something wrong.”
    * 


**their statements did not agree with each other**  - This could be translated as, “they said things about Jesus that were very different from each other” or, “the witnesses said things about Jesus that contradicted each other.”
    * 


**he was guilty of anything**  – That is, “that he had done anything wrong.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__39-01|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/39-jesus-is-put-on-trial|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__39-03|>>]]**


===== Are You the Son of God? [39-03] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-39-03.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=1d2e71?nolink&640x360}}


Finally, the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/priest-high|high priest]]** looked directly at **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** and said, “Tell us, are you the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/messiah|Messiah]]**, the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god-son|Son of the living God]]**?”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**Finally**  - That is, “After they were unable to find any evidence against him” or, “After they were unable to prove that he was guilty.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__39-02|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/39-jesus-is-put-on-trial|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__39-04|>>]]**


===== I Am the Son of God [39-04] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-39-04.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=642951?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** said, “**I am**, and you will see me **seated with [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]] and coming from [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/heaven|heaven]]**.” The **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/priest-high|high priest]]****tore his clothes in anger**  and shouted to the other **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jewish-leaders|religious leaders]]**, “We do not need any more **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/witness|witnesses]]**! You have heard him say that he is the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god-son|Son of God]]**. **What is your [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/judge|judgment]]**?”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**I am**  - That is, “I am as you said” or, “I am the Messiah and the Son of God.” “I am” is also the name of God (See **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__09-14|[09-14]]]**). By saying simply, “I am” Jesus was also saying that he is God. If possible, translate this so that people will see a similarity between Jesus' answer and the name of God.
    * 


**seated with God**  - This could be translated as, “reigning with God.” Because God is the ruler over all, people talk about him as sitting on a throne in heaven. By saying that he would be seated with God, Jesus claimed that he had authority to rule with the Father.
    * 


**seated with God and coming from heaven**  – This could be translated as, “sitting beside God and then coming from heaven.”
    *
