**tore his clothes in anger**  - The Jews would tear their clothes to show grief or anger. If tearing the clothes means something else in your language, you may want to substitute a phrase such as, “he was extremely angry.”
    * 


**What is your judgment?**  - That is, “What is your decision?” or, “Tell us what have you decided: Is he innocent or guilty?” The chief priest wanted the religious leaders to condemn Jesus for claiming to be equal with God.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__39-03|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/39-jesus-is-put-on-trial|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__39-05|>>]]**


===== They Mocked Jesus [39-05] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-39-05.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=20f35e?nolink&640x360}}


The **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jewish-leaders|Jewish leaders]]** all answered the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/priest-high|high priest]]**, “He deserves to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/death|die]]**!” Then **they blindfolded [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]**, **spit on him**, hit him, and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/mock|mocked]]** him.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**they blindfolded Jesus**  - That is. “they covered Jesus' eyes so that he could not see.”
    * 


**spit on him**  - This could also be translated as, “spit on him to insult him” or, “spit on him in order to say that he was worthless.” This was a way of showing contempt for someone.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__39-04|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/39-jesus-is-put-on-trial|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__39-06|>>]]**


===== Peter and the Servant Girl [39-06] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-39-06.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=094915?nolink&640x360}}


As **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/peter|Peter]]** was waiting outside the house, a **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/servant|servant girl]]** saw him and said to him, “You also were with **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]**!” Peter **denied it**. Later, another girl said the same thing, and **Peter denied it again**. Finally, the people said, “We know that you were with Jesus because you both **are from [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/galilee|Galilee]]**.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**denied it**  - This can be translated as, “said that it was not true” or, “said that he was not with Jesus” or, “said, 'No. That is not true.'”
    * 


**Peter denied it again**  – This could be translated as, “Peter denied knowing Jesus a second time” or, “again Peter said he had not been with Jesus.”
    * 


**are from Galilee**  - This could also be translated as, “are Galileans.” The people could tell from the way Jesus and Peter talked that they came from the region of Galilee.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__39-05|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/39-jesus-is-put-on-trial|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__39-07|>>]]**


===== Peter Denied Jesus [39-07] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-39-07.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=422bda?nolink&640x360}}


Then **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/peter|Peter]] vowed**, saying, “**May [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]] [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/curse|curse]] me if I know this man**!” Immediately, **a rooster crowed**, and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** turned around and looked at Peter.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**vowed**  - That is, “said emphatically” or, “said very strongly.”
    * 


**May God curse me if I know this man**  - This is a curse that means, “May God cause harm to me if what you say is true” or, “May God punish me if I am lying to you!” In this way Peter was saying very strongly that he did not know Jesus. He also referred to Jesus as, “this man” to make it sound like he did not know him.
    * 


**a rooster crowed**  - “Crowing” is the loud sound that a rooster makes. Compare how you translated this in **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__38-09|[38-09]]]**.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__39-06|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/39-jesus-is-put-on-trial|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__39-08|>>]]**


===== Judas Killed Himself [39-08] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-39-08.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=40b728?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/peter|Peter]]** went away and **cried bitterly**. Meanwhile, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/judas|Judas]]**, **the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/betray|betrayer]]**, saw that the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jewish-leaders|Jewish leaders]]****had condemned [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]] to die**. Judas became full of sorrow and went away and killed himself.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**cried bitterly**  - That is, “cried, feeling deep sorrow” or, “cried, feeling deep regret.”
    * 


**the betrayer**  – That is, “who had betrayed Jesus” or, “who had helped the leaders arrest Jesus.”
    * 


**had condemned Jesus to die**  - That is, “had said that Jesus was guilty and must die.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__39-07|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/39-jesus-is-put-on-trial|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__39-09|>>]]**


===== Jesus and Pilate [39-09] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-39-09.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=15b199?nolink&640x360}}


Early the next morning, the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jewish-leaders|Jewish leaders]]** brought **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/pilate|Pilate]]**, the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/rome|Roman]] governor**. They hoped that Pilate would condemn Jesus as guilty and **sentence him to be killed**. Pilate asked Jesus, “Are you the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/king-of-jews|king of the Jews]]**?”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**Roman governor**  - That is, “Roman government official.” The Roman government had appointed Pilate to govern the region of Judea in Israel.
    * 


**sentence him to be killed**  - As governor, Pilate had the authority to condemn Jesus to death and to give approval for his crucifixion, or to set him free. The Jewish religious leaders did not have the authority to have someone killed.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__39-08|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/39-jesus-is-put-on-trial|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__39-10|>>]]**


===== What Is Truth? [39-10] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-39-10.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=5e7961?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** answered, “**You have said so**, but **my [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/kingdom-of-god|kingdom]] is not an earthly [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/kingdom|kingdom]]**. If it were, **my [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/servant|servants]] would fight for me**. I have come to earth to tell the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/true|truth]]** about **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]**. Everyone who **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/love|loves]]** the truth **listens to me**.” **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/pilate|Pilate]]** said, “**What is truth?**”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**You have said so**  - That is, “You have spoken correctly.”
    * 


**my kingdom is not an earthly kingdom**  - That is, “my kingdom is not like earthly kingdoms.”
    * 


**my servants would fight for me**  - That is, “my disciples would fight to protect me” so that I could establish my kingdom.
    * 


**listens to me**  – This could be translated as, “hears my teaching and obeys me.” It includes not just hearing Jesus' words, but also doing what he says.
    * 


**What is truth?**  - that is, “Can anyone know what is true?”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__39-09|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/39-jesus-is-put-on-trial|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__39-11|>>]]**


===== He Is Not Guilty [39-11] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-39-11.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=3f6650?nolink&640x360}}


After speaking with **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]**, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/pilate|Pilate]]** went out to the crowd and said, “**I find no [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/guilt|guilt]] in this man**.” But the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jewish-leaders|Jewish leaders]]** and the crowd shouted, “**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/crucify|Crucify]]** him!” Pilate replied, “**He is not guilty**.” But they shouted even louder. Then Pilate said a third time, “He is not guilty!”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**I find no guilt in this man**  - That is, “I do not find this man to be guilty” or, “I have examined this man, and I do not see that he has done anything wrong.”
    * 


**He is not guilty**  - That is, “He has done nothing wrong!”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__39-10|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/39-jesus-is-put-on-trial|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__39-12|>>]]**


===== The King of the Jews [39-12] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-39-12.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=b69690?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/pilate|Pilate]]** became afraid that the crowd would begin to **riot**, so he ordered his soldiers to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/crucify|crucify]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]**. The **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/rome|Roman]]** soldiers whipped Jesus and put **a royal robe**  and a **crown made of thorns**  on him. Then they **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/mock|mocked]]** him by saying, “**Look**, **the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/king-of-jews|King of the Jews]]**!”


//A Bible story from: Matthew 26:57-27:26; Mark 14:53-15:15; Luke 22:54-23:25; John 18:12-19:16//


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**riot**  - That is, “start doing violent things in their anger.”
    * 


**a royal robe**  - That is, “a robe like a king's robe.” This robe had a bright color, so it looked like the kind of robe that a king would wear.
    * 


**crown made of thorns**  - This means that they tied thorn branches into a circle to look like a crown. A crown is an ornament that a king wears on his head to show his authority. But the crown that they put on Jesus' head had sharp, dangerous thorns on it.
    * 


**Look**  – That is, “Look at” or, ”Here is.”
    * 


**the King of the Jews**  – Since the soldiers were mocking Jesus, this could be translated as, “the so-called King of the Jews.”
    * 


//A Bible story from//  - These references may be slightly different in some Bible translations.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__39-11|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/39-jesus-is-put-on-trial|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__40-01|>>]]**


===== Jesus Carried His Cross [40-01] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-40-01.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=f01d70?nolink&640x360}}


After the soldiers **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/mock|mocked]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]**, they **led him away**  **to [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/crucify|crucify]] him**. They made him carry the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/cross|cross]]** on which he would die.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**led him away**  – That is, “forced him to go with them.” This could also be translated as, “took him away.”
    * 


**to crucify him**  - That is, “to kill him on a cross.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__39-12|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/40-jesus-is-crucified|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__40-02|>>]]**


===== Jesus Was Nailed to the Cross [40-02] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-40-02.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=686aef?nolink&640x360}}


The soldiers brought **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** to a place called “**the Skull**” and nailed his arms and feet to the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/cross|cross]]**. But Jesus said, “**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god-father|Father]]**, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/forgive|forgive]] them, because they do not know what they are doing**.” **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/pilate|Pilate]]** commanded that they write, “**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/king-of-jews|King of the Jews]]**” on a sign and put it on the cross above Jesus’ head.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**the Skull**  - A hill near Jerusalem with a white, rocky top that was shaped somewhat like the top of a skull.
    * 


**forgive them, because they do not know what they are doing**  - That is, “they do not understand the meaning of what they are doing, so please forgive them.” The soldiers thought Jesus was only a criminal who deserved to die. They did not understand that he was the Son of God.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__40-01|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/40-jesus-is-crucified|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__40-03|>>]]**


===== Gambling for His Clothes [40-03] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-40-03.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=0ac7af?nolink&640x360}}


The soldiers **gambled for [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus']] clothing**. When they did this, **they [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/fulfill|fulfilled]] a [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/prophet|prophecy]] that said**, “They divided my garments among them, and gambled for my clothing.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**gambled for Jesus' clothing**  - That is, “played a game of chance to win Jesus' clothes.” We do not know how they did this, but in some cultures it could be translated as, “tossed stones on the ground to win Jesus' clothing” or, “chose sticks to decide who could take Jesus' clothes.”
    * 


**they fulfilled a prophecy that said**  - That is, “they did what the scriptures had long ago predicted would happen to the Messiah” or, “they did what a prophet wrote long ago.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__40-02|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/40-jesus-is-crucified|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__40-04|>>]]**


===== The Two Robbers [40-04] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-40-04.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=a86619?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** was **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/crucify|crucified]]** between **two robbers**. One of them **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/mock|mocked]]** Jesus, but the other said, “Do you have no fear of **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]**? **We are [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/guilt|guilty]], but this man is [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/innocent|innocent]]**.” Then he said to Jesus, “**Please remember me**  **in your [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/kingdom-of-god|kingdom]]**.” Jesus answered him, “Today, you will be with me in **Paradise**.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**two robbers**  - This could also be translated as, “two bandits.” This refers to criminals who used force or violence to steal things.
    * 


**Do you have no fear of God?**  - The robber does not expect an answer to this question; it is a way that some languages use to make a strong statement. If your language does not use questions in this way, then translate this as, “You should fear God!”
    * 


**We are guilty but this man is innocent**  – This could be translated as, “You and I have done evil things and deserve to die, but this man, Jesus, has done nothing wrong and does not deserve to die.” “We” here includes both robbers, but does not include Jesus.
    * 


**this man**  - This phrase refers to Jesus.
    * 


**Please remember me**  - That is, “Please accept me” or, “Please welcome me” or, “Please allow me to be with you.” “Remember” here does not mean to recall something after forgetting it. Translate this in a way that communicates a humble request.
    * 


**in your kingdom**  – That is, “when you establish your kingdom” or, “when you are ruling as king.”
    * 


**Paradise**  - This is another name for “heaven.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__40-03|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/40-jesus-is-crucified|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__40-05|>>]]**


===== Come Down from the Cross [40-05] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-40-05.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=0db1b7?nolink&640x360}}


The **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jewish-leaders|Jewish leaders]]** and the other people in the crowd **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/mock|mocked]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]**. They said to him, “If you are the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god-son|Son of God]]**, come down from the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/cross|cross]]** and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/save|save]]** yourself! Then we will **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/believe|believe]]** you.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**believe you**  – That is, “believe in you” or, “believe that you are the Messiah.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__40-04|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/40-jesus-is-crucified|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__40-06|>>]]**


===== The Darkness [40-06] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-40-06.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=5fd2e5?nolink&640x360}}


Then the sky over the whole region became completely dark, even though it was the middle of the day. It stayed dark from noon until 3:00 in the afternoon.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


//(There are no notes in this frame.)// 
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__40-05|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/40-jesus-is-crucified|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__40-07|>>]]**


===== Jesus Died [40-07] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-40-07.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=d31315?nolink&640x360}}


Then **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** cried out, “**It is finished!**  **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god-father|Father]]**, I give my **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/spirit|spirit]]****into your hands**.” Then he **bowed his head**  and **gave up his spirit**. When he **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/death|died]]**, there was an earthquake and the **large curtain**  that separated the people from the presence of **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** in the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/temple|Temple]]** was torn in two, from the top to the bottom.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**It is finished!**  - This could also be translated as, “It is completed” or, “I have finished it” or, “I have completed the work.” This means that Jesus' work of salvation was complete.
    * 


**into your hands**  - That is, “into your care.”
    * 


**bowed his head**  – That is, “lowered his head.”
    * 


**gave up his spirit**  - That is, “gave up his spirit to God” or, “released his spirit to God and died.”
    * 


**large curtain**  - This was a large, strong fabric hung in the temple. It was like a wall separating one room from another. It can also be translated as “thick curtain” or, “hanging fabric” or, “screen.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__40-06|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/40-jesus-is-crucified|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__40-08|>>]]**


===== The Soldier's Testimony [40-08] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-40-08.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=964198?nolink&640x360}}


**Through his [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/death|death]]**, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]****opened a way**  for people to **come to [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]**. When the soldier guarding Jesus saw everything that had happened, he said, “Certainly, this man was **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/innocent|innocent]]**. He was the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god-son|Son of God]]**.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**Through his death**  - That is, “By means of his death” or, “By dying.”
    * 


**opened a way**  - That is, “made it possible.”
    * 


**come to God**  - That is, “come near to God” or, “go near to God” or, “approach God” or, “know God personally.” The tearing of the curtain showed that the barrier between God and people had been removed.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__40-07|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/40-jesus-is-crucified|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__40-09|>>]]**


===== The Burial of Jesus [40-09] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-40-09.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=8d2e9f?nolink&640x360}}


Then **Joseph**  and Nicodemus, two **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jewish-leaders|Jewish leaders]]** who **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/believe|believed]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** was the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/messiah|Messiah]]**, **asked [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/pilate|Pilate]] for Jesus’ body**. They wrapped his body in cloth and placed it in a **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/tomb|tomb]]** cut out of rock. Then they rolled a large stone in front of the tomb to block the opening.


//A Bible story from: Matthew 27:27-61; Mark 15:16-47; Luke 23:26-56; John 19:17-42//


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**Joseph**  - This was not Mary's husband. It was another man named Joseph.
    * 


**asked Pilate for Jesus' body**  – That is, “asked Pilate to permit them to take Jesus' body down from the cross.”
    * 


//A Bible story from//  - These references may be slightly different in some Bible translations.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__40-08|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/40-jesus-is-crucified|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__41-01|>>]]**


===== Guards for the Tomb [41-01] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-41-01.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=4a2ec6?nolink&640x360}}


After the soldiers **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/crucify|crucified]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]**, **the unbelieving [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jewish-leaders|Jewish leaders]]** said to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/pilate|Pilate]]**, “**That liar, Jesus, said**  he would **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/raise|rise]] from the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/death|dead]]** after three days. Someone must guard the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/tomb|tomb]]** to make sure that his **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/disciple|disciples]]** do not steal the body and then say he has risen from the dead.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**the unbelieving Jewish leaders**  - That is, “the Jewish leaders who did not believe in Jesus.”
    * 


**That liar, Jesus, said**  – This could also be translated as, “That man, Jesus, lied and said.” They refused to believe that Jesus told the truth about being the Son of God.
    * 


**rise from the dead**  - That is, “come back to life” or, “become alive again.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__40-09|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/41-god-raises-jesus-from-the-dead|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__41-02|>>]]**


===== The Tomb Was Sealed [41-02] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-41-02.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=bffe22?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/pilate|Pilate]]** said, “Take some soldiers and make the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/tomb|tomb]]** as secure as you can.” So **they placed a seal on the stone**  at the entrance of the tomb and put the soldiers there to make sure no one could steal the body.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**they placed**  - That is, “the religious leaders and the soldiers placed.”
    * 


**a seal on the stone**  - They put a soft material like clay or wax between the stone and the tomb and marked it with an official seal. If anyone moved the stone, the material would break and show that someone had entered the tomb. This could also be translated as, “a mark on the stone to forbid people from moving it.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__41-01|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/41-god-raises-jesus-from-the-dead|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__41-03|>>]]**


===== The Women [41-03] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-41-03.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=d5c20b?nolink&640x360}}


The day after **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** was buried was a **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sabbath|Sabbath]]** day, and **the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jew|Jews]] were not permitted**to go to a **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/tomb|tomb]]** on that day. So very early on the morning after the Sabbath day, several women prepared to go to Jesus’ **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/tomb|tomb]]** to put more **burial spices**  on his body.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**the Jews were not permitted**  – The Sabbath day rules did not permit a Jew to walk very far or to do any other kind of work.
    * 


**burial spices**  - This refers to sweet-smelling spices that were placed on a dead body to cover the bad smell. This can also be translated as, “sweet-smelling spices” or, “sweet-smelling oils” or, “sweet-smelling plants.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__41-02|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/41-god-raises-jesus-from-the-dead|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__41-04|>>]]**


===== The Angel Appeared [41-04] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-41-04.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=18422b?nolink&640x360}}


Suddenly, there was a **great earthquake**. An **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/angel|angel]]****that shone as bright as lightning**  appeared from **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/heaven|heaven]]**. He rolled away the stone that was covering the entrance to the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/tomb|tomb]]** and sat on it. The soldiers guarding the tomb were terrified and **fell to the ground like [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/death|dead]] men**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**great earthquake**  – This could also be translated as, “violent earthquake” or, “forceful shaking of the ground.” Some languages may prefer to reword this as, “the ground began to shake violently.”
    * 


**that shone as bright as lightning**  - That is, “whose appearance was as bright as lightning.”
    * 


**fell to the ground like dead men**  - They were not dead, but they did not move, just like dead men do not move. They probably had fainted from fright. To make this clear, this could be translated as, “suddenly fell to the ground and did not move.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__41-03|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/41-god-raises-jesus-from-the-dead|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__41-05|>>]]**


===== Jesus Is Risen [41-05] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-41-05.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=a6b138?nolink&640x360}}


When the women arrived at the tomb, the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/angel|angel]]** told them, “**Do not be afraid**. **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** is not here. **He has [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/raise|risen]] from the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/death|dead]]**, just like he said he would! Look in the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/tomb|tomb]]** and see.” The women looked into the tomb and saw where Jesus' body had been laid. His body was not there!


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**Do not be afraid**  - That is, “Stop being afraid.” An angel shining like lightning was a frightening sight!
    * 


**He has risen from the dead**  – This could be translated as, “He has come back to life.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__41-04|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/41-god-raises-jesus-from-the-dead|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__41-06|>>]]**


===== Tell the Disciples [41-06] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-41-06.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=665c3c?nolink&640x360}}


Then the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/angel|angel]]** told the women, “Go and tell the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/disciple|disciples]]**, '**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** has **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/raise|risen]]** from the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/death|dead]]** and **he will go to [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/galilee|Galilee]] ahead of you**.'”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**he will go to Galilee ahead of you **- That is, “he will meet you in Galilee” or, “he will be in Galilee when you get there.” “You” here is plural, including the apostles and other disciples.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__41-05|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/41-god-raises-jesus-from-the-dead|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__41-07|>>]]**


===== The Joyful News [41-07] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-41-07.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=8a2158?nolink&640x360}}


The women were **full of fear and great [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/joy|joy]]**. They ran to tell the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/disciple|disciples]]** the **good news**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**full of fear and great joy**  – That is, “experiencing emotions of fear and also great joy.”
    * 


**good news**  - This can also be translated as, “the good news that Jesus was alive again.” This good news refers to the fact that Jesus had risen from the dead.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__41-06|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/41-god-raises-jesus-from-the-dead|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__41-08|>>]]**


===== Jesus Appeared to the Women [41-08] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-41-08.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=3eb0f5?nolink&640x360}}


As the women were on their way to tell the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/disciple|disciples]]** the good news, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** appeared to them, and they **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/worship|worshiped]]** him. Jesus said, “Do not be afraid. Go and tell my disciples to go to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/galilee|Galilee]]**. They **will see me**  there.”


//A Bible story from: Matthew 27:62-28:15; Mark 16:1-11; Luke 24:1-12; John 20:1-18//


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**will see me**  - That is, “will meet me” or, “can meet with me.”
    * 


//A Bible story from//  - These references may be slightly different in some Bible translations.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__41-07|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/41-god-raises-jesus-from-the-dead|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__42-01|>>]]**


===== The Two Disciples [42-01] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-42-01.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=2f0ae1?nolink&640x360}}


On the day that **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** was **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/raise|raised]]** from the dead, two of his **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/disciple|disciples]]** were going to a nearby town. As they walked, they talked about what had happened to Jesus. They had hoped that he was the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/messiah|Messiah]]**, but then he was killed. Now the women said he was **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/life|alive]]** again. They did not know what to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/believe|believe]]**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


//(There are no notes for this frame.)// 
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__41-08|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/42-jesus-returns-to-heaven|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__42-02|>>]]**


===== Jesus Walked with the Disciples [42-02] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-42-02.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=3294b2?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** approached them and started walking with them, but they **did not recognize him**. He asked what they were talking about, and they told him about **all the remarkable things that had happened**  concerning Jesus during the previous few days. They thought they were talking to a visitor who did not know what had happened in **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jerusalem|Jerusalem]]**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**did not recognize him**  - That is, “did not know that it was Jesus.”
    * 


**all the remarkable things that had happened**  - This refers to the teaching and miracles of Jesus, his death, and the reports of his resurrection.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__42-01|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/42-jesus-returns-to-heaven|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__42-03|>>]]**


===== Jesus Explained the Prophets [42-03] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-42-03.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=70ad77?nolink&640x360}}


Then **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** explained to them what **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/word-of-god|God’s word]]** said about the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/messiah|Messiah]]**. He reminded them that the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/prophet|prophets]]** said the Messiah would **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/suffer|suffer]]** and be killed, but would **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/raise|rise]]** again **on the third day**. When they arrived at the town where the two men planned to stay, **it was almost evening**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**on the third day**  - Some languages may prefer to say, “on the third day after his death.”
    * 


**it was almost evening**  - This can also be translated as, “the day was ending” or, “the sun was going down” or, “it was starting to get dark.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__42-02|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/42-jesus-returns-to-heaven|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__42-04|>>]]**


===== Breaking the Bread [42-04] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-42-04.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=93a654?nolink&640x360}}


The two men invited **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** to stay with them, so he did. When they were ready to eat the evening meal, Jesus picked up a loaf of bread, thanked **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** for it, and then broke it. Suddenly, they recognized that he was Jesus. But at that moment, **he disappeared from their sight**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**he disappeared from their sight**  - This could also be translated as, “he was gone” or, “he was no longer there.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__42-03|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/42-jesus-returns-to-heaven|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__42-05|>>]]**


===== Jesus Is Alive [42-05] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-42-05.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=0d2643?nolink&640x360}}


The two men said to each other, “That was **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]**! That is why **our hearts were burning**  when he explained **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/word-of-god|God’s word]]** to us!” Immediately, they went back to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jerusalem|Jerusalem]]**. When they arrived, they told the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/disciple|disciples]]**, “Jesus is **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/life|alive]]**! We have seen him!”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**our hearts were burning**  - That is, “we were getting excited” or, “we were beginning to hope” or, “we felt joy.” Some languages have ways of expressing it such as, “our hearts were stirred” or, “our hearts were warmed.” If you use an expression that refers to the heart burning, make sure it does not indicate that they were upset or angry.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__42-04|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/42-jesus-returns-to-heaven|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__42-06|>>]]**


===== Jesus Appeared to the Disciples [42-06] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-42-06.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=1adf98?nolink&640x360}}


As the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/disciple|disciples]]** were talking, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** suddenly appeared in the room with them and said, “**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/peace|Peace]] to you**!” The **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/disciple|disciples]]** thought he was a **ghost**, but Jesus said, “Why are you afraid and **doubting**? Look at my hands and feet. Ghosts do not have bodies like I do.” **To prove**  that he was not a ghost, he asked for something to eat. They gave him a piece of cooked fish, and he ate it.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**Peace to you**  - This may also be translated as, “May you have peace” or, “Be at peace.”
    * 


**ghost**  - This refers to the spirit of a dead person.
    * 


**doubting**  – That is, “doubting that I am alive and here with you.”
    * 


**To prove**  - That is, “to demonstrate to them.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__42-05|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/42-jesus-returns-to-heaven|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__42-07|>>]]**


===== Jesus Opened their Minds [42-07] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-42-07.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=d04c2a?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** said, “I told you that everything written about me in **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/word-of-god|God’s word]]** must be **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/fulfill|fulfilled]]**.” Then he **opened their minds so that they could understand**  God’s word. He said, “It was written long ago that the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/messiah|Messiah]]** would **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/suffer|suffer]]**, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/death|die]]**, and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/raise|rise]]** from the dead **on the third day**.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**must be fulfilled**  - This can be translated as, “must happen.”
    * 


**opened their minds so that they could understand**  - This could also be translated as, “caused them to be able to understand” or, “made them able to comprehend.”
    * 


**on the third day**  - That is, “after three days” or, “three days later.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__42-06|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/42-jesus-returns-to-heaven|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__42-08|>>]]**


===== You Are Witnesses [42-08] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-42-08.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=e4b617?nolink&640x360}}


“It was also written in the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/word-of-god|scriptures]]** that my **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/disciple|disciples]]** will **proclaim**  that everyone should **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/repent|repent]]** in order to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/receive|receive]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/forgive|forgiveness]]** for their **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sin|sins]]**. **They will do this starting in [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jerusalem|Jerusalem]]**, and then go to all **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/people-group|people groups]]** everywhere. **You are [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/witness|witnesses]] of these things**.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**proclaim**  - That is, “announce” or, “preach.”
    * 


**They will do this starting in Jerusalem**  - That is, “They will begin doing this in Jerusalem” or, “They will begin to proclaim these things in Jerusalem.”
    * 


**You are witnesses of these things**  - That is, “You have seen these things happen” or, “You will tell other people the things that you have seen happen.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__42-07|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/42-jesus-returns-to-heaven|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__42-09|>>]]**


===== Jesus Taught for Forty Days [42-09] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-42-09.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=d5add1?nolink&640x360}}


During the next forty days, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** appeared to his **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/disciple|disciples]]** many times. Once, he even appeared to more than 500 people at the same time! He proved to his disciples in many ways that he was **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/life|alive]]**, and he taught them about the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/kingdom-of-god|kingdom of God]]**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


//(There are no notes for this frame.)// 
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__42-08|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/42-jesus-returns-to-heaven|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__42-10|>>]]**


===== Make Disciples [42-10] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-42-10.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=0518b8?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** said to his **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/disciple|disciples]]**, “**All authority in [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/heaven|heaven]] and on earth has been given to me**. So go, **make disciples of all [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/people-group|people groups]]** by **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/baptize|baptizing]]** them **in the name of**  the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god-father|Father]]**, the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god-son|Son]]**, and the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/holy-spirit|Holy Spirit]]**, and by teaching them to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/obey|obey]]** everything I have commanded you. Remember, I will be with you always.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**All authority in heaven and on earth has been given to me**  - This can also be translated as, “God has given me all authority in heaven and on earth” or, “God has given me complete authority over everyone in heaven and on earth” or, “I have all authority in heaven an on earth.”
    * 


**make disciples of all people groups**  - That is, “help people from every people group become my disciples.”
    * 


**in the name of**  - This phrase means both, “by the authority of” and, “under the authority of.” Consider translating the word “name” literally if it will be understood in this way in your language. This phrase can also be repeated as in, “in the name of the Father, in the name of the Son, and in the name of the Holy Spirit.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__42-09|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/42-jesus-returns-to-heaven|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__42-11|>>]]**


===== Jesus Went to Heaven [42-11] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-42-11.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=9ffdb8?nolink&640x360}}


Forty days after **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** rose from the dead, he told his **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/disciple|disciples]]**, “Stay in **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jerusalem|Jerusalem]]** until my **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god-father|Father]]** gives you **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/power|power]]** when the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/holy-spirit|Holy Spirit]]****comes on you**.” Then Jesus went up to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/heaven|heaven]]**, and **a cloud hid him from their sight**. Jesus sat down **at the right hand of [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** to rule **over all things**.


//A Bible story from: Matthew 28:16-20; Mark 16:12-20; Luke 24:13-53; John 20:19-23; Acts 1:1-11//


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**comes on you**  - That is, “comes down upon you” or, “comes onto you.”
    * 


**a cloud hid him from their sight**  - This could also be translated as, “he disappeared into a cloud.”
    * 


**at the right hand of God**  - This could also be translated as, “at the right side of God.”
    * 


**over all things**  - That is, “over everything.”
    * 


//A Bible story from//  - These references may be slightly different in some Bible translations.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__42-10|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/42-jesus-returns-to-heaven|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__43-01|>>]]**


===== The Disciples in Jerusalem [43-01] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-43-01.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=f92200?nolink&640x360}}


After **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]] returned to [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/heaven|heaven]]**, the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/disciple|disciples]]****stayed in [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jerusalem|Jerusalem]]** as Jesus had commanded them to do. The **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/believer|believers]]** there constantly gathered together to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/pray|pray]]**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**returned to heaven**  - That is, “went back to heaven.”
    * 


**stayed in Jerusalem**  – That is, “stayed in Jerusalem for awhile.” They didn't stay there permanently.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__42-11|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/43-the-church-begins|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__43-02|>>]]**


===== The Feast of Pentecost [43-02] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-43-02.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=9b3573?nolink&640x360}}


Every year, 50 days after the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/passover|Passover]]**, the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jew|Jews]]** celebrated an important day called **Pentecost**. Pentecost was a time when the Jews **celebrated the harvest**. Jews came from all over the world to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jerusalem|Jerusalem]]** to celebrate Pentecost together. **This year**, the time for Pentecost came about a week after **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** had gone back to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/heaven|heaven]]**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**Pentecost**  - “Pentecost” means “fiftieth (day).” You could use the word “Pentecost” in your translation and let the text explain the meaning. Or you could use a term that means, “50th day.”
    * 


**celebrated the harvest**  - The Jews would thank God for the harvest by bringing offerings and celebrate by having special meals.
    * 


**This year**  - That is, “In the year that Jesus died.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__43-01|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/43-the-church-begins|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__43-03|>>]]**


===== Speaking Other Languages [43-03] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-43-03.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=aef7da?nolink&640x360}}


While the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/believer|believers]]** were all together, suddenly the house where they were was filled with **a sound like a strong wind**. Then something that looked like flames of fire appeared over the heads of all the believers. They were all **filled with the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/holy-spirit|Holy Spirit]]** and they began to speak **in other languages**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**a sound like a strong wind**  - That is, “a noise that a strong wind makes” or, “the sound that the wind makes when it blows hard.”
    * 


**filled with the Holy Spirit**  - That is, “given ability by the Holy Spirit” or, “given power by the Holy Spirit.”
    * 


**in other languages**  - This could be translated as, “in languages other than their own language” or, “in foreign languages” or, “as people from other places speak.” The believers did not know these languages until the Holy Spirit gave them the power to speak them. Make sure the word used to translate “languages” refers to languages people actually speak and understand.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__43-02|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/43-the-church-begins|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__43-04|>>]]**


===== The Crowd Gathered [43-04] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-43-04.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=9c1ef4?nolink&640x360}}


When the people in **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jerusalem|Jerusalem]]** heard the noise, **a crowd**  came to see what was happening. When the people heard the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/believer|believers]]** proclaiming **the wonderful works of [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]**, they were astonished that they were hearing these things in their own native languages.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**a crowd**  – This could be translated as, “a crowd of people” or, “a large group of people.”
    * 


**the wonderful works of God**  - This could be translated as, “the amazing things that God had done.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__43-03|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/43-the-church-begins|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__43-05|>>]]**


===== God's Spirit Was Poured Out [43-05] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-43-05.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=70113b?nolink&640x360}}


Some of the people **accused the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/disciple|disciples]] of being drunk**. But **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/peter|Peter]]** stood up and said to them, “Listen to me! These people are not drunk! This **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/fulfill|fulfills]]** the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/prophet|prophecy]]** made by the prophet **Joel**  in which God said, ‘In **the last days**, I will **pour out my [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/holy-spirit|Spirit]]**.’”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**accused the disciples of being drunk**  - This could also be translated as, “said that the disciples were drunk.”
    * 


**Joel**  - Joel was a prophet in Israel who lived hundreds of years before this happened.
    * 


**the last days**  - This refers to, “the final days before the end of the world.”
    * 


**pour out my Spirit**  - This can be understood in the sense of, “give my Spirit generously to people” or, “cause my Spirit to completely empower people.”
    * 


**my Spirit**  - That is, “my Holy Spirit.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__43-04|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/43-the-church-begins|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__43-06|>>]]**


===== You Crucified Jesus [43-06] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-43-06.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=d5203d?nolink&640x360}}


“**Men of [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israel]]**, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** was a man who did many mighty **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/miracle|signs and wonders]]** by the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/power|power]]** of **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]**, as you have seen and already know. But **you [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/crucify|crucified]] him!**”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


(Peter continues preaching to the crowd.)


    * 


**Men of Israel**  – For some languages it is better to say, “People of Israel” for it to be clear that this included men and women. This could also be translated as, “My fellow people of Israel” or, “My fellow Jews” to make it clear that Peter was also a Jew and belonged to the “people of Israel.”
    * 


**you crucified him!**  - This could also be translated as, “you caused him to be crucified” or, “because of you, he was crucified.” The Jews did not actually nail Jesus to the cross. However, the Jewish leaders caused him to be condemned and many of the people in the crowd had shouted for him to be crucified.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__43-05|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/43-the-church-begins|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__43-07|>>]]**


===== God Raised Jesus [43-07] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-43-07.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=bff0bf?nolink&640x360}}


“Although **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** died, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/raise|raised]]** him from the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/death|dead]]**. **This [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/fulfill|fulfills]] the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/prophet|prophecy]] which says**, ‘**You will not let your**  **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/messiah|Holy One]]****rot in the grave**.’ We are **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/witness|witnesses]]** to the fact that God **raised Jesus to [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/life|life]] again**.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


(Peter continues preaching to the crowd.)


    * 


**This fulfills the prophecy which says**  – Another way to translate this would be, “This caused to come true what one of the prophets said long ago.”
    * 


**You will not let your**  - “You” and “your” refer to God the Father. To make that clear, this could be translated as, “You, God, will not let your.” Some languages may have a special way of addressing someone, such as, “You, O God.”
    * 


**rot in the grave**  - That is, “decay in the tomb” or, “decompose in the grave.” This refers to the fact that Jesus did not remain in the tomb very long and is another way of saying that he did not stay dead, but rather came back to life again.
    * 


**raised Jesus to life again**  - That is, “made Jesus alive again.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__43-06|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/43-the-church-begins|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__43-08|>>]]**


===== The Holy Spirit [43-08] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-43-08.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=adb024?nolink&640x360}}


“**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]] is now exalted**to **the right hand of**  **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god-father|God the Father]]**. And Jesus has sent the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/holy-spirit|Holy Spirit]]** just as he **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/promise|promised]]** he would do. The Holy Spirit is **causing**  the things that you are now seeing and hearing.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


(Peter continues preaching to the crowd.)


    * 


**Jesus is now exalted**  - This could also be translated as, “Jesus is now lifted up” or, “Jesus is now raised up” or, “God has exalted Jesus.”
    * 


**the right hand of**  - This could also be translated as, “the most important position with” or, “the place of highest honor next to.”
    * 


**causing**  - That is, “enabling the believers to do” or, “giving these people the power to do.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__43-07|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/43-the-church-begins|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__43-09|>>]]**


===== Jesus Is the Messiah [43-09] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-43-09.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=0befee?nolink&640x360}}


“You **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/crucify|crucified]]** this man, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]**. **But know for certain that**  **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** has caused Jesus to become both **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/lord|Lord]]** and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/messiah|Messiah]]**!”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


(Peter continues preaching to the crowd.)


    * 


**But know for certain that**  – This could also be translated as, “But you can know that it is true that” or, “But you can be sure that.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__43-08|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/43-the-church-begins|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__43-10|>>]]**


===== What Should We Do? [43-10] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-43-10.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=86a705?nolink&640x360}}


The people listening to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/peter|Peter]]** were **deeply moved by**  the things that he said. So they asked Peter and the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/disciple|disciples]]**, “**Brothers**, what should we do?”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**deeply moved by**  - That is, “very troubled by” or, “felt very sad when they heard.” To be “moved” is to feel strong emotions.
    * 


**Brothers**  - This was a normal way for a Jew to address fellow Jews. It could also be translated as, “Friends.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__43-09|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/43-the-church-begins|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__43-11|>>]]**


===== Repent and Be Baptized [43-11] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-43-11.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=e09473?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/peter|Peter]]** answered them, “Every one of you should **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/repent|repent]]** and be **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/baptize|baptized]]****in the name of**  **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]] [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/messiah|Christ]]** so that **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** will **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/forgive|forgive]]** your **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sin|sins]]**. Then he will also give you the **gift of the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/holy-spirit|Holy Spirit]]**.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**in the name of**  - This phrase means both, “by the authority of” and, “under the authority of.” Consider translating the word “name” literally if it will be understood in this way in your language.
    * 


**Christ**  – This is the same meaning as “Messiah.” It could be translated as “Anointed One” or, “Chosen One.” Instead of translating the meaning, some translators may choose to keep the word “Christ” and spell it using the sounds in their own language.
    * 


**Jesus Christ**  – Since “Christ” is a title here, some translators may choose to change the order and say, “Christ Jesus.” Both orders are used in the Bible.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__43-10|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/43-the-church-begins|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__43-12|>>]]**


===== 3000 Believe [43-12] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-43-12.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=6f2eb6?nolink&640x360}}


About 3,000 people **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/believe|believed]]** what **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/peter|Peter]]** said and became **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/disciple|disciples]]** of **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]**. They were **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/baptize|baptized]]** and became part of the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/church|church]]** at **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jerusalem|Jerusalem]]**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


//(There are no notes for this frame.)// 
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__43-11|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/43-the-church-begins|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__43-13|>>]]**


===== The Disciples Met Together [43-13] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-43-13.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=73da5c?nolink&640x360}}


The **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/disciple|disciples]]** continually listened to the teaching of the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/apostle|apostles]]**, spent time together, ate together, and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/pray|prayed]]** with each other. They enjoyed **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/praise|praising]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** together and they shared everything they had with each other. Everyone **thought well of them**. Every day, more people became **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/believer|believers]]**.


//A Bible story from: Acts 2//


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**thought well of them**  - That is, “had a positive opinion of them.”
    * 


//A Bible story from//  - These references may be slightly different in some Bible translations.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__43-12|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/43-the-church-begins|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__44-01|>>]]**


===== The Crippled Man [44-01] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-44-01.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=ff2d0c?nolink&640x360}}


**One day**, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/peter|Peter]]** and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/john|John]]** were going to the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/temple|Temple]]**. As they approached the Temple gate, they saw **a crippled man**  who was **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/beg|begging]]** for money.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**One day**  - This phrase introduces an event that happened in the past, but does not state the specific time. Many languages have a similar way to begin telling a true story.
    * 


**a crippled man**  - This could also be translated as, “a lame man.” This refers to a man who did not have full use of his legs, and could not stand or walk.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__43-13|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/44-peter-and-john-heal-a-beggar|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__44-02|>>]]**


===== Get Up and Walk [44-02] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-44-02.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=418772?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/peter|Peter]]** looked at the lame man and said, “I do not have any money to give you. But I will give you what I do have. **In the name of [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]**, **get up**  and walk!”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**In the name of Jesus**  - “Name” here stands for the authority and power of the person. Therefore, this expression here means, “by the authority of Jesus.”
    * 


**get up**  - That is, “stand up.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__44-01|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/44-peter-and-john-heal-a-beggar|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__44-03|>>]]**


===== The Crippled Man Was Healed [44-03] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-44-03.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=64836b?nolink&640x360}}


Immediately, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/heal|healed]]** the lame man, and he began to walk and jump around, and to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/praise|praise]]** God. The people in the **courtyard of the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/temple|Temple]]** were amazed.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**courtyard of the Temple**  - Only priests could enter the Temple, but ordinary Jews were allowed to come into this area that surrounded the Temple.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__44-02|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/44-peter-and-john-heal-a-beggar|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__44-04|>>]]**


===== The Power of Jesus [44-04] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-44-04.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=340a87?nolink&640x360}}


A crowd of people quickly came to see the man who was **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/heal|healed]]**. **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/peter|Peter]]** said to them, “Why are you amazed that this man is healed? We did not heal him through our own power or goodness. Rather, it is the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/power|power]]** of **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** and the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/faith|faith]]** that Jesus gives that healed this man.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


//(There are no notes for this frame.)// 
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__44-03|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/44-peter-and-john-heal-a-beggar|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__44-05|>>]]**


===== Peter Preached [44-05] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-44-05.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=b90af1?nolink&640x360}}


“You are the ones who told the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/rome|Roman]]** governor to kill **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]**. You killed the **author of [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/life|life]]**, but **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/raise|raised]]** him from the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/death|dead]]**. Although you did not understand what you were doing, God used **your actions**  to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/fulfill|fulfill]]** the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/prophet|prophecies]]** that the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/messiah|Messiah]]** would **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/suffer|suffer]]** and die. So now, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/repent|repent]]** and **turn to God**  so that **your [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sin|sins]] will be washed away**.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


(Peter continues to preach to the crowd.)


    * 


**author of life**  - That is, “the one who created life” or, “the one who gives us life” or, “the one who causes people to live.” This refers to Jesus.
    * 


**your actions **  - This can also be translated as, “the things you did.” This refers to their asking Pilate to kill Jesus.
    * 


**turn to God**  - That is, “decide to obey God.”
    * 


**your sin will be washed away**  - This could be translated as, “God will wash away your sins” or, “God will take away your sins and make you clean.” This is talking about God purifying people in their spirit by completely removing their sins. It does not mean physical washing.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__44-04|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/44-peter-and-john-heal-a-beggar|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__44-06|>>]]**


===== Peter and John Were Arrested [44-06] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-44-06.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=5d776b?nolink&640x360}}


The leaders of the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/temple|Temple]]** were very upset by what **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/peter|Peter]]** and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/john|John]]** were saying. So they arrested them and put them into prison. But many of the people **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/believe|believed]]****Peter's message**, and the **number of men**  who believed in Jesus grew to about 5,000.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**Peter's message**  - That is, “the message that Peter had preached to them.”
    * 


**number of men**  - This was in addition to the woman and children who believed.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__44-05|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/44-peter-and-john-heal-a-beggar|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__44-07|>>]]**


===== Before the Jewish Leaders [44-07] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-44-07.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=4cf19c?nolink&640x360}}


The next day, the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jewish-leaders|Jewish leaders]]** brought **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/peter|Peter]]** and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/john|John]]** to the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/priest-high|high priest]]** and the other religious leaders. They asked Peter and John, “By what **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/power|power]]** did you heal this crippled man?”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


//(There are no notes for this frame.)// 
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__44-06|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/44-peter-and-john-heal-a-beggar|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__44-08|>>]]**


===== No Other Way but Jesus [44-08] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-44-08.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=54d477?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/peter|Peter]]** answered them, “This man stands before you **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/heal|healed]]** by the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/power|power]]** of **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/messiah|Messiah]]**. You **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/crucify|crucified]]** Jesus, but **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/raise|raised]]** him to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/life|life]]** again! You **rejected him**, **but there is no other way to be [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/save|saved]] except through the power of Jesus**!”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**healed**  - That is, “well” or, “whole” or, “strong.”
    * 


**rejected him**  - That is, “refused to accept him” or, “refused to believe in Jesus” or, “refused to believe that Jesus is the Savior.”
    * 


**but there is no other way to be saved except through the power of Jesus**  – This could also be translated as, “but the only way to be saved is through the power of Jesus” or, “but only Jesus can save us, by his power.”
    * 


**to be saved**  - This can also be translated as, “to be saved from our sins” or, “that we can be saved from our sins.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__44-07|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/44-peter-and-john-heal-a-beggar|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__44-09|>>]]**


===== The Disciples Were Released [44-09] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-44-09.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=fbba5f?nolink&640x360}}


The **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jewish-leaders|leaders]]****were shocked**  that **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/peter|Peter]]** and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/john|John]]** spoke so boldly because they could see that these men were **ordinary**  men **who were uneducated**. But **then they remembered**  that these men **had been with [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]**. **After they threatened**  Peter and John, they **let them go**.


//A Bible story from: Acts 3:1-4:22//


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**were shocked**  - That is, “were very surprised” or, “were amazed.”
    * 


**ordinary**  - That is, “common” or, “lower-class.” Peter and John were simple fishermen.
    * 


**who were uneducated**  - That is, “who did not have a formal education.” This could also be translated as, “who had not gone to religious school.”
    * 


**then they remembered**  - This could also be translated as, “But then they thought about the fact that.”
    *
