**had been with Jesus**  - This could also be translated as, “had spend time with Jesus” or, “had been taught by Jesus.”
    * 


**After they threatened**  - The leaders said that they would punish Peter and John if they continued to teach people about Jesus.
    * 


**let them go**  - That is, “allowed them to leave.”
    * 


//A Bible story from//  - These references may be slightly different in some Bible translations.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__44-08|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/44-peter-and-john-heal-a-beggar|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__45-01|>>]]**


===== The Miracles of Stephen [45-01] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-45-01.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=fa8395?nolink&640x360}}


One of the leaders in **the early [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/church|Church]]** was a man named Stephen. He **had a good reputation**  and **was full of the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/holy-spirit|Holy Spirit]] and of [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/wise|wisdom]]**. Stephen did many **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/miracle|miracles]]** and **reasoned persuasively that**  people should **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/believe|believe]]** in **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**the early Church**  - That is, “the Church when it first began.”
    * 


**had a good reputation**  - This could be translated as, “was thought well of by the people.” Some languages might translate this as, “had a good name.”
    * 


**was full of the Holy Spirit and of wisdom**  - This could also be translated as, “had power and ability from the Holy Spirit and had much wisdom” or, “was full of the Holy Spirit and was very wise.”
    * 


**reasoned persuasively that**  - That is, “gave convincing reasons why.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__44-09|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/45-philip-and-the-ethiopian-official|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__45-02|>>]]**


===== Stephen's Arrest [45-02] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-45-02.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=c3603a?nolink&640x360}}


**One day**, when Stephen was teaching about **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]**, some **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jew|Jews]]** who did not believe in Jesus began to argue with Stephen. They became very angry and lied about Stephen to the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jewish-leaders|religious leaders]]**. They said, “We heard him speak **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/evil|evil]]** things about **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/moses|Moses]]** and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]**!” So the religious leaders arrested Stephen and brought him to the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/priest-high|high priest]]** and the other leaders of the Jews, where more false **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/witness|witnesses]]** lied about Stephen.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**One day**  - This phrase introduces an event that happened in the past, but does not state the specific time. Many languages have a similar way to begin telling a true story.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__45-01|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/45-philip-and-the-ethiopian-official|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__45-03|>>]]**


===== You Killed the Messiah [45-03] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-45-03.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=983d9c?nolink&640x360}}


The **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/priest-high|high priest]]** asked Stephen, “**Are these things [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/true|true]]**?” Stephen replied by reminding them of many of the great things **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** had done from the time of **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/abraham|Abraham]]** to the time of **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]**, and how God's people continually **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/disobey|disobeyed]]** him. Then he said, “You stubborn and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/rebel|rebellious]]** people **always reject the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/holy-spirit|Holy Spirit]]**, just as **your ancestors**  always rejected God and killed his **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/prophet|prophets]]**. But you did something worse than they did! You killed the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/messiah|Messiah]]**!”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**Are these things true?**  - That is, “Are these accusations against you true?” or, “Are the things these people are saying about you true?” or, “Is it true that you said evil things about Moses and God?”
    * 


**always reject the Holy Spirit**  - That is, “never obey the Holy Spirit” or, “always refuse to listen to the Holy Spirit.”
    * 


**your ancestors**  - This could be translated as, “your ancestors, the Israelites.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__45-02|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/45-philip-and-the-ethiopian-official|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__45-04|>>]]**


===== Stephen Was Stoned [45-04] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-45-04.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=2eeaf0?nolink&640x360}}


When the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jewish-leaders|religious leaders]]** heard this, they were so angry that they **covered their ears**  and **yelled loudly**. They dragged Stephen out of the city and threw stones at him in order to kill him.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**covered their ears**  - This could also be translated as, “They put their hands over their ears.” This was to show that they did not want to hear what Stephen said.
    * 


**yelled loudly**  - They were yelling in anger. Translate this in a way that communicates that they were very upset.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__45-03|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/45-philip-and-the-ethiopian-official|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__45-05|>>]]**


===== Stephen's Prayer [45-05] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-45-05.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=95f186?nolink&640x360}}


**As Stephen was dying**, he **cried out**, “**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]**, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/receive|receive]]** my **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/spirit|spirit]]**.” Then he fell to his knees and cried out again, “**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/lord|Master]]**, **do not count this [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sin|sin]] against them**.” Then he **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/death|died]]**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**As Stephen was dying**  - That is, “Just before Stephen died.”
    * 


**cried out**  – That is, “called out in a loud voice” or, “said very loudly.”
    * 


**do no count this sin against them**  - That is, “do not consider them guilty of the sin of killing me.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__45-04|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/45-philip-and-the-ethiopian-official|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__45-06|>>]]**


===== The People Attacked the Believers [45-06] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-45-06.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=116b63?nolink&640x360}}


A young man named **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/paul|Saul]]** agreed with the people who killed Stephen and **guarded their robes**  while they threw stones at him. That day, many people in **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jerusalem|Jerusalem]]** started **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/persecute|persecuting]]** the followers of **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]**, so the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/believer|believers]]** fled to other places. **But in spite of this**, they **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/preach|preached]]** about Jesus everywhere they went.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**guarded their robes**  - This could be translated as, “watched over their coats.” He was probably making sure they didn't get stolen or damaged.
    * 


**But in spite of this**  – The Jewish leaders thought they could stop the spread of Jesus' teaching by persecuting his followers. Instead, this caused them to scatter and spread the message even more widely.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__45-05|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/45-philip-and-the-ethiopian-official|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__45-07|>>]]**


===== Philip on the Desert Road [45-07] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-45-07.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=ff1b53?nolink&640x360}}


A **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/disciple|disciple]]** of **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus']]** named Philip was one of the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/believer|believers]]** who fled from **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jerusalem|Jerusalem]]** during the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/persecute|persecution]]**. He went to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/samaria|Samaria]]** where he **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/preach|preached]]** about Jesus and many people were **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/save|saved]]**. Then **one day**, an **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/angel|angel]]** from **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** told Philip to go to a certain road in the desert. As he walked along the road, Philip saw an important official from **Ethiopia**  riding in his **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/chariot|chariot]]**. The **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/holy-spirit|Holy Spirit]]** told Philip to go and talk to this man.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**one day**  - This phrase introduces an event that happened in the past, but does not state the specific time. Many languages have a similar way to begin telling a true story.
    * 


**Ethiopia**  - Ethiopia is a country in Eastern Africa.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__45-06|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/45-philip-and-the-ethiopian-official|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__45-08|>>]]**


===== The Ethiopian Read Isaiah [45-08] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-45-08.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=45b89e?nolink&640x360}}


When Philip **approached the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/chariot|chariot]]**, he heard the **Ethiopian**  reading from what the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/isaiah|prophet Isaiah]]** wrote. The man read, “They led him like a **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/lamb|lamb]]** to be killed, and **as a lamb is silent**, he did not say a word. They treated him unfairly and did not respect him. **They took his [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/life|life]] away from him**.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**Ethiopian**  - That is, a person from the country of Ethiopia. See note on **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__45-07|[45-07]]]**.
    * 


**approached the chariot**  - That is, “got close to the chariot” or, “came near to the chariot.”
    * 


**as a lamb is silent**  - This could also be translated as, “like a lamb that is silent even when it is about to be killed.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__45-07|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/45-philip-and-the-ethiopian-official|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__45-09|>>]]**


===== Philip Met the Ethiopian [45-09] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-45-09.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=f32a68?nolink&640x360}}


Philip asked the Ethiopian, “Do you understand what you are reading?” The Ethiopian replied, “No. I cannot understand it unless someone explains it to me. Please come and sit next to me. **Was [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/isaiah|Isaiah]] writing about**himself or someone else?”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**Was Isaiah writing about**  - This can also be translated as, “Was Isaiah referring to.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__45-08|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/45-philip-and-the-ethiopian-official|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__45-10|>>]]**


===== Philip Preached about Jesus [45-10] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-45-10.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=4db741?nolink&640x360}}


Philip explained to the Ethiopian man that **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/isaiah|Isaiah]]** was writing about **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]**. Philip also used other **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/word-of-god|scriptures]]** to tell him the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/good-news|good news]]** about Jesus.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


//(There are no notes for this frame.)// 
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__45-09|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/45-philip-and-the-ethiopian-official|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__45-11|>>]]**


===== Here Is Water [45-11] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-45-11.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=534a03?nolink&640x360}}


As Philip and the Ethiopian traveled, they came to **some water**. The Ethiopian said, “Look! There is some water! **May I be [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/baptize|baptized]]**?” And he told the driver to stop the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/chariot|chariot]]**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**some water**  - Use a term that means a larger body of water such as a pond, lake, or stream.
    * 


**May I be baptized?**  - This could also be translated as, “Is there any reason that I cannot be baptized?”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__45-10|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/45-philip-and-the-ethiopian-official|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__45-12|>>]]**


===== Philip Baptized the Ethiopian [45-12] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-45-12.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=6098db?nolink&640x360}}


So they went down into the water, and Philip **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/baptize|baptized]]** the Ethiopian. After they came up out of the water, the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/holy-spirit|Holy Spirit]]** suddenly **carried Philip away**  to another place where he continued telling people about **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**carried Philip away**  - That is, “took Philip away” or, “snatched Philip away.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__45-11|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/45-philip-and-the-ethiopian-official|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__45-13|>>]]**


===== The Ethiopian Went Home [45-13] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-45-13.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=db597b?nolink&640x360}}


The Ethiopian continued traveling toward his home, happy that he knew **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]**.


//A Bible story from: Acts 6:8-8:5; 8:26-40//


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


//A Bible story from//  - These references may be slightly different in some Bible translations.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__45-12|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/45-philip-and-the-ethiopian-official|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__46-01|>>]]**


===== Saul Arrested the Believers [46-01] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-46-01.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=06d01a?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/paul|Saul]]** was the young man who **guarded the robes of the men who killed Stephen**. He did not **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/believe|believe]]** in **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]**, and so he **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/persecute|persecuted]]** the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/believer|believers]]**. He went **from house to house**  in **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jerusalem|Jerusalem]]** to arrest both men and women and to put them in prison. The **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/priest-high|high priest]]** gave Saul permission to go to the city of **Damascus**  to arrest Christians there and to bring them back to Jerusalem.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**guarded the robes of the men who killed Stephen**  - See **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__45-06|[45-06]]]**.
    * 


**from house to house**  - That is, “into many houses.”
    * 


**Damascus**  - Damascus is now the capital of the country of Syria. During Saul's time, it was a city belonging to the Roman Empire. Most of the people there were not Jewish, but there were some Jews and also some Christians living there.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__45-13|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/46-paul-becomes-a-christian|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__46-02|>>]]**


===== Saul Saw Jesus [46-02] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-46-02.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=6c20aa?nolink&640x360}}


While **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/paul|Saul]]** was **on his way**  to Damascus, a bright light from heaven shone all around him, and he fell to the ground. Saul heard someone say, “Saul! Saul! Why do you **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/persecute|persecute]]** me?” Saul asked, “Who are you, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/lord|Master]]**?” Jesus replied to him, “I am Jesus. You are persecuting me!”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**on his way**  - That is, “on his journey.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__46-01|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/46-paul-becomes-a-christian|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__46-03|>>]]**


===== Saul Became Blind [46-03] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-46-03.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=582a11?nolink&640x360}}


When **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/paul|Saul]]** got up, he could not see. His friends had to lead him into Damascus. Saul did not eat or drink anything for three days.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


//(There are no notes for this frame.)// 
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__46-02|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/46-paul-becomes-a-christian|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__46-04|>>]]**


===== God Sent Ananias to Saul [46-04] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-46-04.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=14a682?nolink&640x360}}


There was a **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/disciple|disciple]]** in Damascus named Ananias. **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** said to him, “Go to the house where **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/paul|Saul]]** is staying. Place your hands on him so that he can see again.” **But Ananias said**, “**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/lord|Master]]**, I have heard how this man has **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/persecute|persecuted]]** the believers.” **God answered him**, “Go! I have chosen him **to declare my name**  to the Jews and to people from other people groups. He will **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/suffer|suffer]]** many things **for my name**.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**But Ananias said**  – If it is not clear why the word “But” is used here, this could be translated as, “But Ananias was afraid, so he said.”
    * 


**God answered him**  – This could be translated as, “To reassure Ananias, God said” to make clear why God said this.
    * 


**to declare my name**  - That is, “to teach about me” or, “to make me known.”
    * 


**for my name**  - That is, “for me” or, “because of me” or, “because he serves me” or, “because he teaches others about me.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__46-03|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/46-paul-becomes-a-christian|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__46-05|>>]]**


===== Ananias Baptized Saul [46-05] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-46-05.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=ade53c?nolink&640x360}}


So Ananias went to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/paul|Saul]]**, placed his hands on him, and said, “**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]**, who appeared to you on your way **here**, sent me to you so that you can **regain your sight**  and be filled with the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/holy-spirit|Holy Spirit]]**.” Saul immediately was able to see again, and Ananias **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/baptize|baptized]]** him. Then Saul ate some food and **his strength returned**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**here**  - That is, “to Damascus.”
    * 


**regain your sight**  - This could also be translated as, “be able to see again.”
    * 


**his strength returned**  - This could also be translated as, “he became strong again” or, “he felt better.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__46-04|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/46-paul-becomes-a-christian|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__46-06|>>]]**


===== Saul Preached about Jesus [46-06] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-46-06.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=cf3ea8?nolink&640x360}}


**Right away**, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/paul|Saul]]** began **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/preach|preaching]]** to the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jew|Jews]]** in Damascus, saying, “**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** is the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god-son|Son of God]]**!” The Jews were amazed that the man who had tried to destroy the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/believer|believers]]** now also believed in Jesus! Saul **reasoned with the Jews**, proving that Jesus was the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/messiah|Messiah]]**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**Right away**  - This can also be translated as, “Immediately” or, “Then.”
    * 


**reasoned with the Jews**  - This could also be translated as, “gave the Jews good reasons for believing in Jesus” or, “spoke persuasively with the Jews.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__46-05|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/46-paul-becomes-a-christian|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__46-07|>>]]**


===== Saul Escaped Damascus [46-07] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-46-07.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=f63d4b?nolink&640x360}}


After many days, the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jew|Jews]]** made a plan to kill **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/paul|Saul]]**. They sent people to watch for him at **the city gates**  in order to kill him. But Saul heard about the plan, and his friends helped him escape. One night they **lowered him over the city wall in a basket**. After Saul escaped from Damascus, he continued to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/preach|preach]]** about **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**the city gates**  - The gates were the only normal way into or out of the walled cities.
    * 


**lowered him over the city wall in a basket**  - Another way to say this would be, “helped him get into a large basket and lowered the basket with him in it over the city wall.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__46-06|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/46-paul-becomes-a-christian|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__46-08|>>]]**


===== Saul Went to Jerusalem [46-08] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-46-08.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=ab52bc?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/paul|Saul]] went to [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jerusalem|Jerusalem]]** to meet with the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/disciple|disciples]]**, but they were afraid of him. Then a **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/believer|believer]]** named **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/barnabas|Barnabas]]** took Saul to the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/apostle|apostles]]** and told them how Saul had **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/preach|preached]]** boldly in Damascus. After that, the disciples **accepted Saul**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**accepted Saul**  - That is, “believed that Saul also was a believer in Jesus.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__46-07|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/46-paul-becomes-a-christian|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__46-09|>>]]**


===== The Christians in Antioch [46-09] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-46-09.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=0276ce?nolink&640x360}}


Some believers who fled from the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/persecute|persecution]]** in **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jerusalem|Jerusalem]]** went far away to the **city of Antioch**  and preached about **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]**. Most of the people in Antioch were not **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jew|Jews]]**, but for the first time, very many of them also became believers. **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/barnabas|Barnabas]]** and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/paul|Saul]]** went there to teach these new believers more about Jesus and to **strengthen the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/church|church]]**. It was at Antioch that believers in Jesus were first called “**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/christian|Christians]]**.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**city of Antioch**  - This was an ancient city located in what is now the southernmost tip of the modern country of Turkey, near its border with Syria and close to the Mediterranean Sea. It was about 450 miles northwest of Jerusalem.
    * 


**strengthen the church**  - This could also be translated as, “help the church to grow strong spiritually” or, “help the believers in Jesus to grow strong in their faith” or, “help the people to believe more firmly in Jesus.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__46-08|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/46-paul-becomes-a-christian|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__46-10|>>]]**


===== Barnabas and Saul [46-10] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-46-10.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=339ba0?nolink&640x360}}


**One day**, while the Christians at Antioch were **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/fast|fasting]]** and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/pray|praying]]**, the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/holy-spirit|Holy Spirit]]** said to them, “**Set apart for me Barnabas and Saul to do the work I have called them to do**.” So **the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/church|church]]** in Antioch **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/pray|prayed]]** for **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/barnabas|Barnabas]]** and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/paul|Saul]]** and **placed their hands on them**. Then they **sent them out**  to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/preach|preach]]** the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/good-news|good news]]** about **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** in many other places. Barnabas and Saul taught people from different people groups, and many people **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/believe|believed]]** in Jesus.


//A Bible story from: Acts 8:3; 9:1-31; 11:19-26; 13:1-3//


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**One day**  - This phrase introduces an event that happened in the past, but does not state the specific time. Many languages have a similar way to begin telling a true story.
    * 


**Set apart for me …**  - This sentence could also be translated as, “Appoint Paul and Barnabas to do the special work I have chosen them to do.”
    * 


**the church**  – This could also be translated as, “the believers” or, “the Christians.”
    * 


**placed their hands on them**  - This could also be translated as, “blessed them with the power and authority of the Holy Spirit by putting their hands on them” or, “put their hands on them as a sign of their unity in the Spirit.” Some languages may have to say where they placed their hands. If so, you could say they placed their hands on their head, shoulder or back.
    * 


**sent them out **  - That is, “sent them away” or, “sent them on their journey.”
    * 


//A Bible story from//  - These references may be slightly different in some Bible translations.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__46-09|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/46-paul-becomes-a-christian|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__47-01|>>]]**


===== Paul and Silas in Philippi [47-01] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-47-01.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=cb4032?nolink&640x360}}


As Saul traveled throughout the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/rome|Roman Empire]]**, **he began to use his Roman name, ”[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/paul|Paul]].”**One day, Paul and his friend **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/silas|Silas]]** went to the town of **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/philippi|Philippi]]** to **proclaim**  the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/good-news|good news]]** about **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]**. They went to a place by the river outside the city where people gathered to pray. There they met a woman named Lydia who was a **merchant**. She **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/love|loved]]** and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/worship|worshiped]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**proclaim**  - That is, “teach” or, “preach.”
    * 


**merchant**  - This could also be translated as, “seller” or, “business owner.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__46-10|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/47-paul-and-silas-in-philippi|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__47-02|>>]]**


===== Lydia Was Baptized [47-02] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-47-02.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=3220c7?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]****opened Lydia's heart to understand**  the message about **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]**, and **she and her family were [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/baptize|baptized]]**. She invited **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/paul|Paul]]** and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/silas|Silas]]** to stay at her house, **so they stayed with her and her family**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**opened Lydia's heart**  - That is, “enabled Lydia.”
    * 


**to understand**  - That is, “to understand and believe.”
    * 


**she and her family were baptized**  - This can also be translated as, “they baptized Lydia and her family.”
    * 


**so they stayed with her and her family**  - This was the normal custom of the day for people to provide hospitality to visitors in their homes. There were no immoral motives in this arrangement.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__47-01|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/47-paul-and-silas-in-philippi|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__47-03|>>]]**


===== The Slave Girl [47-03] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-47-03.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=a67461?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/paul|Paul]]** and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/silas|Silas]]** often met with people at the place of **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/pray|prayer]]**. Every day as they walked there, a **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/servant|slave girl]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/demon-possessed|possessed by a demon]]** followed them. By means of this **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/demon|demon]]** she predicted the future for people, so she made a lot of money for **her [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/lord|masters]]****as a fortuneteller**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**her masters**  - In this case, this could also be translated as, “her owners.”
    * 


**as a fortuneteller**  - That is, “as someone who told people what would happen to them in the future.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__47-02|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/47-paul-and-silas-in-philippi|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__47-04|>>]]**


===== The Testimony of the Demon [47-04] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-47-04.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=738552?nolink&640x360}}


The **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/servant|slave girl]]** kept yelling as they walked, “These men are **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/servant|servants]]** of the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|Most High God]]**. They are telling you **the way to be [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/save|saved]]**!” She did this so often that **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/paul|Paul]]** became annoyed.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**the way to be saved**  - That is, “how you can be saved” or, “how God saves people” or, “God's plan for saving people.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__47-03|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/47-paul-and-silas-in-philippi|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__47-05|>>]]**


===== Paul Healed the Slave Girl [47-05] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-47-05.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=065e05?nolink&640x360}}


Finally **one day**  when the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/servant|slave girl]]** started yelling, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/paul|Paul]]****turned to her**  and said to the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/demon|demon]]** that was in her, “**In the name of [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]**, **come out of her**.” Right away the demon left her.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**one day**  - This phrase introduces an event that happened in the past, but does not state the specific time. Many languages have a similar way to begin telling a true story.
    * 


**turned to her**  – That is, “turned around and looked at her.”
    * 


**In the name of Jesus**  - That is, “by the authority of Jesus.” Because of Jesus' authority, Paul could command the demon to leave.
    * 


**come out of her**  - That is, “leave her” or, “go away from her.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__47-04|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/47-paul-and-silas-in-philippi|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__47-06|>>]]**


===== The People Were Angry [47-06] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-47-06.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=ebcb75?nolink&640x360}}


The men who owned the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/servant|slave girl]]** became very angry! They realized that **without the demon**, the slave girl could not tell people **the future**. **This meant that**  people would no longer pay her owners money so that she would tell them what would happen to them.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**without the demon**  - That is, “without the power from the demon” or, “now that she did not have the demon.”
    * 


**the future**  - That is, “what would happen to them in the future.”
    * 


**This meant that**  - This could also be translated as, “Because of this” or, “Therefore.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__47-05|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/47-paul-and-silas-in-philippi|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__47-07|>>]]**


===== Paul and Silas Were Arrested [47-07] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-47-07.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=8597a3?nolink&640x360}}


So the owners of the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/servant|slave girl]]** took **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/paul|Paul]]** and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/silas|Silas]]** to the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/rome|Roman authorities]]**, who beat them and **threw them**  into jail.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**threw them**  - That is, “put them.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__47-06|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/47-paul-and-silas-in-philippi|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__47-08|>>]]**


===== Paul and Silas in Prison [47-08] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-47-08.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=8707f0?nolink&640x360}}


They put **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/paul|Paul]]** and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/silas|Silas]]** in the most secure part of the prison and even locked up their feet. Yet **in the middle of the night**, they were **singing songs of [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/praise|praise]] to [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**in the middle of the night**  – This could be translated as, “very late at night” or, “very early in the morning.” This was when it was completely dark outside, when people would normally be asleep.
    * 


**singing songs of praise to God**  - This can also be translating as, “praising God by singing” or, “singing songs to praise God” or, “singing songs that gave praise to God.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__47-07|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/47-paul-and-silas-in-philippi|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__47-09|>>]]**


===== The Earthquake [47-09] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-47-09.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=b381ce?nolink&640x360}}


Suddenly, there was a violent earthquake! All the prison doors **flew open**, and the chains of all the prisoners **fell off**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**flew open**  - That is, “became unlocked and suddenly opened wide.”
    * 


**fell off**  - That is, “suddenly came off” or, “suddenly came apart so that the prisoners were released.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__47-08|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/47-paul-and-silas-in-philippi|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__47-10|>>]]**


===== The Jailer [47-10] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-47-10.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=20a9d9?nolink&640x360}}


**The jailer**  woke up, and when he saw that the prison doors were open, he was terrified! He thought all the prisoners had escaped, so he planned to kill himself. (He knew the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/rome|Roman authorities]]** would kill him if he allowed the prisoners to escape.) But **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/paul|Paul]]** saw him and yelled, “Stop! Do not hurt yourself. **We**  are all here.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**The jailer**  - That is, “the official in charge of the jail.”
    * 


**We**  - Some languages have a special form of the word “we” which does not include the person being talked to. Here the “we” does not include the jailer, only Paul and the rest of the prisoners.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__47-09|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/47-paul-and-silas-in-philippi|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__47-11|>>]]**


===== What Must I Do? [47-11] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-47-11.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=46293f?nolink&640x360}}


The jailer trembled as he came to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/paul|Paul]]** and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/silas|Silas]]** and asked, “What must I do **to be [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/save|saved]]**?” **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/paul|Paul]]** answered, “**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/believe|Believe]] in [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]], the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/lord|Master]]**, and **you and your family will be [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/save|saved]]**.” Then the jailer took Paul and Silas into his home and washed their wounds. Paul **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/preach|preached]]** the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/good-news|good news]]** about Jesus to everyone in his house.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**to be saved**  - This could also be translated as, “in order to be saved from my sins” or “so that God will save me from my sins.” The question refers to salvation from being punished by the God who caused the earthquake.
    * 


**Believe in Jesus, the Master**  - This is addressed to both the jailer and his family, who all then believed and were baptized. Some languages may use a form to indicate that Paul is speaking to the group.
    * 


**you and your family will be saved**  - This can also be translated as, “God will save you and your family from eternal punishment for your sins.” Make sure it is clear that the salvation referred to here is spiritual, not physical.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__47-10|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/47-paul-and-silas-in-philippi|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__47-12|>>]]**


===== The Jailer Was Baptized [47-12] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-47-12.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=684a5d?nolink&640x360}}


The jailer and his whole family **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/believe|believed]]** in **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** and were **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/baptize|baptized]]**. Then the jailer gave **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/paul|Paul]]** and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/silas|Silas]]** a meal and they **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/joy|rejoiced]]** together.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


//(There are no notes for this frame.)// 
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__47-11|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/47-paul-and-silas-in-philippi|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__47-13|>>]]**


===== The Good News Spreads [47-13] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-47-13.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=331ede?nolink&640x360}}


The next day **the leaders of the city**  released **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/paul|Paul]]** and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/silas|Silas]]** from prison and asked them to leave **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/philippi|Philippi]]**. Paul and Silas visited **Lydia**  and some other friends and then left the city. **The [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/good-news|good news]] about [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]] kept spreading**, and **the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/church|Church]] kept growing**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**the leaders of the city**  - This refers to, “the officials of the city” or, “the authorities of the city.”
    * 


**The good news about Jesus kept spreading**  - That is, “People in more and more places were hearing the good news about Jesus.”
    * 


**the Church kept growing**  - That is, “more and more people were becoming part of the Church” or, “more and more people were believing in Jesus.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__47-12|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/47-paul-and-silas-in-philippi|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__47-14|>>]]**


===== Letters to the Churches [47-14] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-47-14.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=773d78?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/paul|Paul]]** and other **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/christian|Christian]]** leaders traveled to many cities, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/preach|preaching]]** and teaching people the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/good-news|good news]]** about **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]**. They also wrote **many letters**  to encourage and teach the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/believer|believers]]** in the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/church|churches]]**. Some of these letters became books of the Bible.


//A Bible story from: Acts 16:11-40//


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


//A Bible story from//  - These references may be slightly different in some Bible translations.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__47-13|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/47-paul-and-silas-in-philippi|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__48-01|>>]]**


===== The Perfect Creation [48-01] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-48-01.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=93c833?nolink&640x360}}


When **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]] created the world**, everything was **perfect**. **There was no [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sin|sin]]**. **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/adam|Adam]]** and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/eve|Eve]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/love|loved]]** each other, and they loved God. **There was no sickness or [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/death|death]]**. This was the way God wanted the world to be.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**God created the world**  - That is, “God made the world out of nothing.”
    * 


**perfect**  - That is, “exactly as it should be” to accomplish all that God intended for it.
    * 


**There was no sin**  - For some languages it is not possible to express “sin” as a thing, rather it is an action. In those cases this could be translated as, “No one ever sinned” or, “People did not sin” or, “Nothing evil had happened.”
    * 


**There was no sickness or death**  - That is, “No one got sick and no one died” or, “They did not get sick or die.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__47-14|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/48-jesus-is-the-promised-messiah|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__48-02|>>]]**


===== Adam and Eve Sinned [48-02] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-48-02.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=467457?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/satan|Satan]]** spoke through the snake in **the garden**  in order to **deceive [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/eve|Eve]]**. Then she and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/adam|Adam]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sin|sinned]]** against **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]**. Because they sinned, everyone on earth gets sick and everyone **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/death|dies]]**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**the garden**  - This refers to the garden created by God where he placed the first man and woman.
    * 


**deceive Eve**  - That is, “lie to Eve.” Satan lied by leading Eve to doubt what God had said. By doing this, he tricked her into disobeying God.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__48-01|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/48-jesus-is-the-promised-messiah|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__48-03|>>]]**


===== Enemies of God [48-03] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-48-03.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=17d6f7?nolink&640x360}}


Because **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/adam|Adam]]** and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/eve|Eve]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sin|sinned]]**, something **even more terrible**  happened. They became enemies of **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]**. As a result, every person since then has been born with a sinful nature and is also an enemy of God. The relationship between God and people was broken by sin. But God had a plan to restore that relationship.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**even more terrible**  - That is, “much worse” or, “worse yet.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__48-02|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/48-jesus-is-the-promised-messiah|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__48-04|>>]]**


===== Jesus Will Crush Satan [48-04] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-48-04.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=7ff62f?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/promise|promised]]** that one of **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/eve|Eve's]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/descendant|descendants]]** would **crush [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/satan|Satan's]] head**, and Satan would **wound his heel**. This meant that Satan would kill the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/messiah|Messiah]]**, but God would **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/raise|raise]] him to [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/life|life]] again**, and then the Messiah will crush the power of Satan forever. Many years later, God revealed that **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** is the Messiah.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**crush Satan's head**  - This could also be translated as, “step on Satan's head and smash it down flat” or, “shatter Satan's head by stepping on it.” This is an image of a person stepping on the head of a snake. The head is completely crushed, and the snake is dead and therefore harmless.
    * 


**wound his heel**  - This is an image of a snake on the ground biting a person's foot. In this case, Satan would cause the Messiah to suffer, but would not destroy him.
    * 


**raise him to life again**  - That is, “make him alive again.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__48-03|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/48-jesus-is-the-promised-messiah|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__48-05|>>]]**


===== A Way of Salvation [48-05] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-48-05.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=e3fbe4?nolink&640x360}}


When **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** destroyed the whole earth by the flood, he provided the boat to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/save|save]]** the people who **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/believe|believed]]** in him. In the same way, everyone deserves to be **destroyed because of their [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sin|sins]]**, but God provided **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** to save everyone who believes in him.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**destroyed because of their sins**  - This could also be translated as, “everyone should be punished eternally by God because they have sinned.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__48-04|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/48-jesus-is-the-promised-messiah|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__48-06|>>]]**


===== The Great High Priest [48-06] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-48-06.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=9f880f?nolink&640x360}}


For hundreds of years, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/priest|priests]]** continually offered **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sacrifice|sacrifices]]** to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** for people to show the punishment that they deserved for their **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sin|sins]]**. But those sacrifices could not take away their sin. **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** is the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/priest-high|Great High Priest]]**. Unlike other priests, **he offered himself**  as the only sacrifice that could to take away the sin of all the people in the world. Jesus was the perfect high priest because he **took the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/punish|punishment]]** for every sin that anyone has ever committed.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**he offered himself**  - This could also be translated as, “Jesus allowed himself to be killed.”
    * 


**took the punishment**  - That is, “received the punishment in his own body.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__48-05|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/48-jesus-is-the-promised-messiah|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__48-07|>>]]**


===== God's People [48-07] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-48-07.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=bcbbd6?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** told **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/abraham|Abraham]]**, “**All the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/people-group|people groups]] of the earth**will be **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/bless|blessed]]** through you.” **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** was a **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/descendant|descendant]] ** of Abraham. All the people groups are blessed through him, because everyone who **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/believe|believes]]** in Jesus is **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/save|saved]]** from sin, and becomes **a [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/spirit|spiritual]] descendant of Abraham**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**all the people groups of the earth**  – This could also be translated as, “people from all different parts of the world.”
    * 


**a spiritual descendant of Abraham**  - That is, “spiritually related to Abraham, and one of God's people.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__48-06|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/48-jesus-is-the-promised-messiah|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__48-08|>>]]**


===== The Lamb of God [48-08] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-48-08.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=19ffc9?nolink&640x360}}


When **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** told **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/abraham|Abraham]]** to offer his **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/son|son]]**, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/isaac|Isaac]]**, as a **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sacrifice|sacrifice]]**, God provided a **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/lamb|lamb]]** for the sacrifice **instead of his son, Isaac**. We all **deserve to [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/death|die]]** for our **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sin|sins]]**! But God provided **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]**, the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/lamb|Lamb of God]]**, as a sacrifice **to die in our place**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**instead of his son, Isaac**  - This can also be translated as, “in the place of his son, Isaac” or, “in his son Isaac's place” or, “so that he would not have to offer his son Isaac as a sacrifice.”
    * 


**deserve to die**  - That is, “should die.”
    * 


**to die in our place**  - This can also be translated as, “to die in the place of each of us” or, “so that he would not have to kill us.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__48-07|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/48-jesus-is-the-promised-messiah|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__48-09|>>]]**


===== The Passover [48-09] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-48-09.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=68355c?nolink&640x360}}


When **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]****sent the last plague on [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/egypt|Egypt]]**, he told each **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israelite]]** family to kill **a perfect [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/lamb|lamb]]** and spread **its [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/blood|blood]]** on the tops and sides of their **door frames**. When God saw the blood, he **passed over**  their houses and did not kill their firstborn sons. This event is called the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/passover|Passover]]**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**sent the last plague on Egypt**  – That is, “caused the final disaster to come on Egypt.” This was the tenth plague when God caused the firstborn sons of the Egyptians to die.
    * 


**a perfect lamb**  - That is, “a lamb without any defect.”
    * 


**its blood**  - That is, “the lamb's blood.”
    * 


**door frames**  – If door frames are not known, this could be translated as, “doors.”
    * 


**passed over**  - This could also be translated as, “passed by” or, “went by.” You may want to connect how this is translated with how “Passover” is translated.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__48-08|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/48-jesus-is-the-promised-messiah|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__48-10|>>]]**


===== The Passover Lamb [48-10] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-48-10.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=65eae1?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** is **our [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/passover|Passover]] [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/lamb|Lamb]]**. He was perfect and **sinless**  and was killed at the time of the Passover celebration. When anyone **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/believe|believes]]** in Jesus, the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/blood|blood]]** of Jesus pays for that person’s **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sin|sin]]**, and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God's]] [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/punish|punishment]] passes over that person**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**our Passover Lamb**  - That is, “the Passover Lamb that was killed for us” or, “the lamb that was killed so that God would pass over us” or, “the lamb that was killed so that God would spare us.”
    * 


**sinless**  - This can also be translated as, “had never sinned.”
    * 


**God's punishment passes over that person**  - This statement means, “God does not punish that person.” Translate it using a phrase that shows its relationship to the words for “Passover” and the “Passover Lamb.” If the word “spare” is used in the name of the Passover, this could also be translated as, “God spares that person from punishment.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__48-09|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/48-jesus-is-the-promised-messiah|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__48-11|>>]]**


===== God's New Covenant [48-11] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-48-11.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=ad519d?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** made a **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/covenant|covenant]]** with **the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israelites]], who were his chosen people**. But God has now made a **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/covenant-new|New Covenant]]** that is available to everyone. Because of this New Covenant, anyone from any **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/people-group|people group]]** can become part of God’s people by **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/believe|believing]]** in Jesus.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**the Israelites, who were his chosen people**  - That is, “the Israelites, the people he had chosen” or, “his chosen people, the Israelites.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__48-10|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/48-jesus-is-the-promised-messiah|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__48-12|>>]]**


===== The Word of God [48-12] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-48-12.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=69fc66?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/moses|Moses]]** was **a great [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/prophet|prophet]]** who proclaimed the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/word-of-god|word of God]]**. But **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** is **the greatest prophet**  of all. He is the Word of God.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**a great prophet**  - That is, “a very important prophet.”
    * 


**the greatest prophet**  - That is, “the most important prophet.”
    * 


**He is the Word of God**  - That is, “He is called the Word of God” because he reveals God's character. The other prophets preached the message God gave them, but Jesus revealed God in his preaching and his actions.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__48-11|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/48-jesus-is-the-promised-messiah|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__48-13|>>]]**


===== A Descendent of David [48-13] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-48-13.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=f21163?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/promise|promised]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/david|King David]]** that the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/messiah|Messiah]]** would be one of his **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/descendant|descendants]]**. **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]**, the Messiah, was that special descendant of David.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


//(There are no notes for this frame.)// 
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__48-12|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/48-jesus-is-the-promised-messiah|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__48-14|>>]]**


===== King of the Universe [48-14] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-48-14.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=125d6b?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/david|David]]** was the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/king|king]]** of **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israel]]**, but **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** is **the king of the entire universe**! He will come again and rule his **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/kingdom-of-god|kingdom]]** with **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/justice|justice]]** and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/peace|peace]]**, forever.


//A Bible story from: Genesis 1-3, 6, 14, 22; Exodus 12, 20; 2 Samuel 7; Hebrew 3:1-6, 4:14-5:10, 7:1-8:13, 9:11-10:18; Revelation 21//


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**the king of the entire universe**  - That is, “the king over everyone and everything everywhere.”
    * 


//A Bible story from//  - These references may be slightly different in some Bible translations.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__48-13|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/48-jesus-is-the-promised-messiah|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__49-01|>>]]**


===== The Virgin Birth [49-01] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-49-01.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=7e3070?nolink&640x360}}


An angel told a **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/virgin|virgin]]** named **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/mary|Mary]]** that she would give birth to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god-son|God's Son]]**. So while she was still a virgin, she gave birth to a son and named him **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]**. Therefore, Jesus is both God and human.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


//(There are no notes for this frame.)// 
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__48-14|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/49-gods-new-covenant|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__49-02|>>]]**


===== The Miracles [49-02] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-49-02.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=c9fc62?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** did many **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/miracle|miracles]]** that prove he is **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]**. He walked on water, calmed storms, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/heal|healed]]** many sick people, **drove out [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/demon|demons]]**, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/raise|raised]] the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/death|dead]] to life**, and turned five loaves of bread and two small fish into enough food for over 5,000 people.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**drove out demons**  - That is, “made demons come out of people.”
    * 


**raised the dead to life**  - This could also be translated as, “caused dead people to become alive again.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__49-01|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/49-gods-new-covenant|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__49-03|>>]]**


===== Jesus the Teacher [49-03] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-49-03.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=c9dab5?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** was also **a great teacher**, and he spoke with authority because he is the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god-son|Son of God]]**. He taught that you need to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/love|love]]** other people **the same way**  you love yourself.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**a great teacher**  - That is, “a very important teacher” or, “an excellent teacher.”
    * 


**the same way **  - That is, “as much as” or, “the same amount that” or, “to the same degree that.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__49-02|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/49-gods-new-covenant|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__49-04|>>]]**


===== Love God Above All [49-04] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-49-04.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=9b1449?nolink&640x360}}


He also taught that you need to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/love|love]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** more than you love anything else, including **your wealth**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**your wealth**  - This could also be translated as, “your money” or, “your possessions.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__49-03|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/49-gods-new-covenant|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__49-05|>>]]**


===== The Value of Salvation [49-05] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-49-05.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=bc4cb8?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** said that the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/kingdom-of-god|kingdom of God]]** is more valuable than anything else in the world. The most important thing that you should seek is **to be [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/save|saved]] from your [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sin|sin]]** so that you can enter into God's kingdom.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**to be saved from your sin**  - That is, “to be saved from being punished for your sin” or, “that God would save you from your sin” or, “to receive salvation from your sin.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__49-04|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/49-gods-new-covenant|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__49-06|>>]]**


===== Not All Will Be Saved [49-06] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-33-02.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=f16e64?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** taught that some people will **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/receive|receive]]** him and be **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/save|saved]]**, but **others will not**. He said that some people are like good soil. They receive the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/good-news|good news]]** of Jesus and are saved. Other people are like the hard soil of a path, where the **seed of [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/word-of-god|God's word]]** does not enter and does not produce any harvest. Those people reject the message about Jesus and will not enter into **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/kingdom-of-god|his kingdom]]**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**others will not**  - That is, “other people will not receive him and therefore will not be saved.”
    * 


**seed of God's word**  - This can be translated as, “seed, which can be compared to God's word.” This phrase makes a comparison between seed and God's word.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__49-05|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/49-gods-new-covenant|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__49-07|>>]]**


===== God Loves Sinners [49-07] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-49-07.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=dc7169?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** taught that **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/love|loves]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sin|sinners]]** very much. He wants to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/forgive|forgive]]** you and to make you his child.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


//(There are no notes for this frame.)// 
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__49-06|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/49-gods-new-covenant|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__49-08|>>]]**


===== God Hates Sin [49-08] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-49-08.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=1bef47?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** also told us that **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** hates **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sin|sin]]**. When **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/adam|Adam]]** and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/eve|Eve]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sin|sinned]]**, it affected all of their **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/descendant|descendants]]**. As a result, every person in the world sins and **is separated from God**. Therefore, everyone has become an enemy of God.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**is separated from God**  - This can also be translated as, “cannot live with God” or, “cannot be near God” or, “cannot have a relationship with God.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__49-07|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/49-gods-new-covenant|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__49-09|>>]]**


===== God Gave His Son [49-09] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-49-09.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=7a2c8a?nolink&640x360}}


But **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/love|loved]]** everyone in the world so much that he **gave his only [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god-son|Son]]** so that **whoever [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/believe|believes]] in [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]] will not be [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/punish|punished]] for his [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sin|sins]], but will [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/life|live]] with God forever**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**gave his only Son**  - This could also be translated as, “offered his only Son to the world as a sacrifice for sins” or, “gave us his only Son to be a sacrifice for our sins.”
    * 


**whoever believes**  - This could also be translated as, “anyone who believes.”
    * 


**whoever believes in Jesus will not be punished for his sins, but will live with God forever**  - This could also be translated as, “When anyone believes in Jesus, God will not punish that person for his sins, but will allow him to live with God forever.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__49-08|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/49-gods-new-covenant|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__49-10|>>]]**


===== Jesus Died in Our Place [49-10] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-49-10.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=9958d3?nolink&640x360}}
