**Because of your [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sin|sin]]**, you are **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/guilt|guilty]]** and deserve to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/death|die]]**. **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]] should be angry**with you, but he **poured out his anger on**  **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** instead of on you. When Jesus died on the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/cross|cross]]**, he **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/receive|received]] your [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/punish|punishment]]**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**Because of your sin**  – This can also be translated as, “Because you have sinned.” To make it clear that this is talking about all people, for some languages it may be more clear to translate this as, “Because all people have sinned, they are guilty. They deserve death.”
    * 


**God should be angry**  – This can also be translated as, “It would be right for God to be angry.”
    * 


**poured out his anger on**  - That is, “directed his anger at” or, “placed all of his anger upon” or, “was angry only with.”
    * 


**received your punishment**  - This could also be translated as, “was punished instead of you” or, “was punished for your sin.” To make it clear that this applies to everyone, it could also be translated as, ”was punished for everyone's sin.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__49-09|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/49-gods-new-covenant|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__49-11|>>]]**


===== The Sinless Sacrifice [49-11] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-49-11.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=bd292d?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** never **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sin|sinned]]**, but he chose to be **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/punish|punished]]** and to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/death|die]]** as the perfect **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sacrifice|sacrifice]]** to **take away**  your sins and the sins of every person in the world. Because Jesus sacrificed himself, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** can **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/forgive|forgive]]** any sin, even terrible sins.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**take away**  - That is, “remove the penalty of” or, “remove the punishment for.” The sacrifice of Jesus causes God to look at our sin as if it never existed.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__49-10|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/49-gods-new-covenant|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__49-12|>>]]**


===== Jesus Died and Rose Again [49-12] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-49-12.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=44b75f?nolink&640x360}}


**Good works cannot [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/save|save]] you**. There is nothing you can do to have a relationship with **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]**. Only **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** can **wash away your [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sin|sins]]**. You must **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/believe|believe]]** that Jesus is the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god-son|Son of God]]**, that he **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/death|died]]** on the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/cross|cross]]****instead of you**, and that God **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/raise|raised]] him to [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/life|life]] again**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**Good works cannot save you**  - That is, “Doing good things cannot save you from your sins” or, “You cannot do anything good enough to save yourself from the penalty for your sins.”
    * 


**wash away your sins**  - That is, “completely remove your sins” or, “take away your sins and make you clean.” This is talking about God purifying people in their spirit by completely removing their sins. It does not mean physical washing.
    * 


**instead of you**  – That is, “ in your place.”
    * 


**raised him to life again**  - This could also be translated as, “made him alive again.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__49-11|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/49-gods-new-covenant|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__49-13|>>]]**


===== God Loves You [49-13] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-49-13.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=30474b?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** will **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/save|save]]** everyone who **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/believe|believes]]** in **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/receive|receives]]** him as their **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/lord|Master]]**. But he will not save anyone who does not believe in him. It does not matter if you are rich or poor, man or woman, old or young, or where you live. God **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/love|loves]]** you and wants you to believe in Jesus so **he can have a close relationship with you**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**he can have a close relationship with you**  - This can also be translated as, “so that you can be his child” or, “so that you can be his friend” or, “so you can belong to him.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__49-12|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/49-gods-new-covenant|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__49-14|>>]]**


===== Believe in Jesus [49-14] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-49-14.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=11e9d6?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** invites you to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/believe|believe]] in him**and to **be [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/baptize|baptized]]**. Do you **believe that**  Jesus is the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/messiah|Messiah]]**, the only **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god-son|Son of God]]**? Do you believe that you are a **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sin|sinner]]** and that you deserve for **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/punish|punish]]** you? Do you believe that Jesus **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/death|died]]** on the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/cross|cross]]** to **take away**  your sins?


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**believe in him**  - This can also be translated as, “trust in him” or, “trust in him to save you” or, “entrust your whole life to him.”
    * 


**be baptized**  - This could also be translated as, “have someone baptize you” or, “let them baptize you.”
    * 


**believe that**  - This can also be translated as, “acknowledge that” or, “agree that.”
    * 


**take away**  - See note on **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__49-11|[49-11]]]**.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__49-13|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/49-gods-new-covenant|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__49-15|>>]]**


===== God's Kingdom of Light [49-15] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-49-15.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=51e5de?nolink&640x360}}


If you **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/believe|believe]]** in **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** and what he has done for you, you are a **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/christian|Christian]]**! **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** has taken you out of **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/satan|Satan's]] [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/kingdom|kingdom]] of darkness**and put you into **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/kingdom-of-god|God’s kingdom]] of light**. God has taken away your old, sinful ways of doing things and has given you new, righteous ways of doing things.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**Satan's kingdom of darkness**  - “Darkness” is used here to refer to sin and everything that is evil. This could be translated as, “Satan's evil rule over people, which is like darkness.”
    * 


**God's kingdom of light**  - “Light” here refers to God's holiness and goodness. This could be translated as, “God's righteous rule over people, which is like light.” The Bible often compares evil to darkness, and goodness to light.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__49-14|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/49-gods-new-covenant|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__49-16|>>]]**


===== Sins Are Forgiven [49-16] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-49-16.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=54f7b2?nolink&640x360}}


If you are a **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/christian|Christian]]**, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** has **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/forgive|forgiven]]** your **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sin|sins]]** because of what **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** did. Now, God **considers you to be**  a close friend instead of an enemy.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**considers you to be**  - That is, “thinks of you as” or, “regards you as” or, “calls you.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__49-15|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/49-gods-new-covenant|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__49-17|>>]]**


===== Follow Jesus' Teachings [49-17] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-49-17.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=d149b4?nolink&640x360}}


If you are a friend of **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** and a **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/servant|servant]]** of **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/lord|Master]]**, you will want to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/obey|obey]]** what Jesus teaches you. Even though you are a **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/christian|Christian]]**, you will still **be [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/tempt|tempted]] to [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sin|sin]]**. But God **is [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/faithful|faithful]]** and says that if you **confess your sins**, he will **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/forgive|forgive]]** you. **He will give you strength to fight against sin**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**be tempted to sin**  - That is, ““be tempted to sin even though you know sin is wrong.”
    * 


**is faithful**  - In this context this means that God, “keeps his promises.”
    * 


**confess your sins**  - This could be translated as, “admit to God what you have done wrong.”
    * 


**He will give you strength to fight against sin**  - That is, “He will give you spiritual strength to refuse to sin.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__49-16|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/49-gods-new-covenant|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__49-18|>>]]**


===== Grow as a Christian [49-18] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-49-18.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=a30dda?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** tells you to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/pray|pray]]**, to study **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/word-of-god|his word]]**, to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/worship|worship]]** him with other **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/christian|Christians]]**, and to tell others what he has done for you. All of these things help you **to have a deeper relationship with him**.


//A Bible story from: Romans 3:21-26, 5:1-11; John 3:16; Mark 16:16; Colossians 1:13-14; 2 Corinthians 5:17-21; 1 John 1:5-10//


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**to have a deeper relationship with him**  - This could also be translated as, “to love him more” or, “to know him more” or, “to become more faithful to him.”
    * 


//A Bible story from//  - These references may be slightly different in some Bible translations.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__49-17|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/49-gods-new-covenant|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__50-01|>>]]**


===== The Church Is Growing [50-01] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-50-01.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=34e404?nolink&640x360}}


For almost 2,000 years, more and more people around the world have been hearing the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/good-news|good news]]** about **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/messiah|Messiah]]**. **The [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/church|Church]] has been growing**. Jesus **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/promise|promised]]** he would return **at the end of the world**. Though he has not yet come back, he will keep his promise.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**The Church has been growing**  - This could also be translated as, “The number of people in the Church around the world has been increasing” or, “The number of believers in Jesus has been increasing.”
    * 


**at the end of the world**  - This phrase means, “right before the present world comes to an end” or, “in the final days of this world.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__49-18|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/50-jesus-returns|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__50-02|>>]]**


===== The Good News [50-02] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-50-02.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=bee14b?nolink&640x360}}


As we wait for **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** to return, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** wants us to live in a way that is **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/holy|holy]]** and that honors him. He also wants us to tell others about his **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/kingdom-of-god|kingdom]]**. When Jesus was living on earth he said, “My **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/disciple|disciples]]** will **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/preach|preach]]** the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/good-news|good news]]** about the kingdom of God to people everywhere in the world, and then **the end will come**.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**the end will come**  - This could be translated as, “the end of this world will come” or, “the end of this world will happen” or, “this present world will end.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__50-01|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/50-jesus-returns|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__50-03|>>]]**


===== The Fields Are Ripe [50-03] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-50-03.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=a3e790?nolink&640x360}}


Many **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/people-group|people groups]]** still have not heard about **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]**. Before he returned to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/heaven|heaven]]**, Jesus told **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/christian|Christians]]** to proclaim the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/good-news|good news]]** to people who have never heard it. He said, “Go and **make [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/disciple|disciples]]** of all people groups!” and, “**The fields are ripe for harvest**!”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**make disciples**  - This has the meaning, “help people to become my disciples.”
    * 


**The fields are ripe for harvest**  - This could also be translated as, “They are ready to be brought to God like fields that are ripe for harvest” or, “They are ready to be gathered and brought to God like fields whose crops are ripe and ready to be gathered.”
    * 


**The fields**  - In this expression, “The fields” represents the people in the world.
    * 


**ripe**  - “Ripe” here represents being ready to believe in Jesus.
    * 


**harvest**  - “Harvest” here represents the work of bringing people to God by teaching them about Jesus.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__50-02|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/50-jesus-returns|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__50-04|>>]]**


===== Remain Faithful [50-04] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-50-04.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=c83ede?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** also said, “A **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/servant|servant]]** is **not greater than**  his **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/lord|master]]**. Just as the authorities of this world have hated me, they will torture and kill you **because of me**. Although **in this world**  you will **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/suffer|suffer]]**, be encouraged because I have defeated **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/satan|Satan]]**, the one who rules this world. If you **remain [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/faithful|faithful]] to me****to the end**, then **God will [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/save|save]] you**!”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**not greater than**  - That is, “not more important than” or, in this case, “not treated better than.”
    * 


**because of me**  - That is, “because you obey me” or, “because you teach people about me” or, “because you belong to me.”
    * 


**in this world**  - This could also be translated as, “in this lifetime.”
    * 


**remain faithful to me**  - That is, “Keep obeying me.”
    * 


**to the end**  - That is, “to the end of your life.”
    * 


**will save you**  - This refers to spiritual salvation rather than physical deliverance from harm. It has already been stated that many believers will be killed or tortured.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__50-03|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/50-jesus-returns|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__50-05|>>]]**


===== The Enemy [50-05] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-50-05.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=6a9df6?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** told his **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/disciple|disciples]]** a story to explain what will happen to people when the world ends. He said, “A man planted **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/good|good]] seed**in his field. While he was sleeping, his enemy came and planted **weed seeds**  along with the **wheat**, and then he went away.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**good seed**  – This seed was wheat grain. If this type of seed is not known in your language area, it is best to use a general term for “seed.” If there is no general term, it may be necessary to choose a type of grain seed that is known and say, for example, “good seed like rice.”
    * 


**weed seeds**  - The weed seeds that were planted would grow up as tall grass but could not be eaten. They were useless.
    * 


**wheat**  – That is, “wheat seeds.” Wheat is a kind of grain that grows like a tall grass. It has seeds that people use for food.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__50-04|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/50-jesus-returns|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__50-06|>>]]**


===== The Weeds [50-06] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-50-06.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=8eb37e?nolink&640x360}}


“When the plants sprouted, the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/servant|servants]]** of the man said, ‘**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/lord|Master]]**, you planted **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/good|good]]** seed in that field. So why are there weeds in it?’ The master answered, ‘**An enemy must have planted them**.’”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


(Jesus continues to tell the story.)


    * 


**An enemy must have planted them**  - If possible, translate this in a way that indicates that the speaker did not see this happen.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__50-05|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/50-jesus-returns|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__50-07|>>]]**


===== Wait for the Harvest [50-07] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-50-07.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=6db756?nolink&640x360}}


“The **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/servant|servants]]** responded to their **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/lord|master]]**, ‘Should we pull out the weeds?’ The master said, ‘No. If you do that, **you will pull out some of the wheat as well**. Wait **until the harvest**  and then gather the weeds into piles to be burned, but bring **the wheat**  into my **barn**.’”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


(Jesus continues to tell the story.)


    * 


**you will pull out some of the wheat as well**  - That is, “you will accidentally pull out some of the wheat also.” It would be too difficult to distinguish young wheat from the weeds, and to pull the weeds without uprooting the wheat.
    * 


**until the harvest**  - That is, “until the time when the wheat is ready to harvest” or, “until the wheat has grown enough to be harvested.”
    * 


**the wheat**  – That is, “the harvested wheat grains.”
    * 


**barn**  - This refers to the building where the harvested wheat grain was saved and stored. It could also be called a “storehouse.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__50-06|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/50-jesus-returns|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__50-08|>>]]**


===== The Field Is the World [50-08] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-50-08.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=a45057?nolink&640x360}}


The **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/disciple|disciples]]** did not understand the meaning of the story, so they asked **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** to explain it to them. Jesus said, “The man who planted the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/good|good]]** seed represents the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/messiah|Messiah]]**. The field represents the world. The good seed represents **the people of [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/kingdom-of-god|God’s kingdom]]**.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**the people of God's kingdom**  - This can also be translated as, “the people who live under God's authority” or, “the people who have submitted to God's rule” or, “the people who will live with God in his Kingdom.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__50-07|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/50-jesus-returns|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__50-09|>>]]**


===== The Enemy Is the Devil [50-09] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-50-09.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=bc6be8?nolink&640x360}}


“The weeds represent the people **who belong to the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/evil|evil]] one**. The enemy who planted the weeds represents **the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/satan|devil]]**. The harvest **represents the end of the world**, and **the harvesters**  represent **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God's]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/angel|angels]]**.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**who belong to the evil one**  - That is, “who obey the evil one” or, “who are ruled by the evil one.”
    * 


**the evil one**  - This is another title for Satan. It could be translated as, “Satan,” but the title, “evil one” describes his character.
    * 


**the devil**  - This could also be translated as, “Satan.”
    * 


**represents the end of the world**  - That is, “represents what will happen to people at the end of the world.”
    * 


**the harvesters**  – This could also be translated as, “the men who harvest the ripe grain” or, “the workers who gather in the ripe grain.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__50-08|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/50-jesus-returns|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__50-10|>>]]**


===== Evil People Will Be Judged [50-10] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-50-10.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=dbb834?nolink&640x360}}


“When the world ends, the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/angel|angels]]** will gather together all the people **who belong to the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/satan|devil]]** and throw them into **a raging fire**, where they will cry and grind their teeth in terrible **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/suffer|suffering]]**. Then **the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/righteous|righteous]] ones**will **shine like the sun**  in the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/kingdom-of-god|kingdom]]** of **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god-father|God their Father]]**.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**who belong to the devil**  - This could also be translated as, “who obey the devil” or, “who are ruled by the devil.” This refers to those who do not believe in Jesus but follow the evil ways of the devil.
    * 


**a raging fire**  - That is, “a very hot, burning fire” or, “a large, very hot fire.”
    * 


**the righteous ones**  - This refers to the people who belong to the Messiah. See **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__50-08|[50-08]]]**.
    * 


**shine like the sun**  - This could also be translated as, “be glorious like the sun” or, “show pure goodness as the sun shows bright light.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__50-09|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/50-jesus-returns|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__50-11|>>]]**


===== Dead Believers Will Rise Again [50-11] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-50-11.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=ead181?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** also said that he would return to earth just before the world ends. He will come back the same way that **he left**, that is, he will have a physical body and **will come on the clouds in the sky**. **When Jesus returns**, every **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/christian|Christian]]** who has **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/death|died]]** will **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/raise|rise]]** from the dead and **meet him in the sky**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**he left**  - This could also be translated as, “he left the earth” or, “he left to go back to heaven.”
    * 


**will come on the clouds in the sky**  - That is, “the clouds in the sky will surround him as he comes” or, “the clouds of the sky will carry him along.”
    * 


**when Jesus returns**  - That is, “when Jesus returns to the earth.”
    * 


**meet him in the sky**  - That is, “join him in the sky.” Those who believe in Jesus will go up to be near Jesus while he is in the sky.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__50-10|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/50-jesus-returns|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__50-12|>>]]**


===== We Will Meet Jesus in the Sky [50-12] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-50-12.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=234089?nolink&640x360}}


Then the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/christian|Christians]]** who are **still [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/life|alive]]** will rise up into the sky and join with the other Christians who **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/raise|rose]]** from the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/death|dead]]**. They will all be with **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** there.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**still alive**  - That is, “still alive when Jesus returns.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__50-11|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/50-jesus-returns|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__50-13|>>]]**


===== Our Crown [50-13] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-50-13.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=b8b6d7?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/promise|promised]]** to give a **crown**  to everyone who **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/believe|believes]]** in him. They will **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/life|live]]** and reign with **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** in **perfect**  **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/peace|peace]]** forever.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**crown**  - This crown represents our reward for believing in Jesus and serving him in this life.
    * 


**perfect**  – That is, “complete” or, “total.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__50-12|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/50-jesus-returns|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__50-14|>>]]**


===== The Fire of Hell [50-14] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-50-14.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=97e93a?nolink&640x360}}


But **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** will **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/judge|judge]]** everyone who does not **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/believe|believe]]** in **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]**. He will throw them into **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/hell|hell]]**, where they will **weep and grind their teeth in anguish**  forever. A fire that never goes out will continually burn them, and worms will never stop eating them.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**weep and grind their teeth in anguish**  - See note on **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__50-10|[50-10]]]**.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__50-13|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/50-jesus-returns|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__50-15|>>]]**


===== God Will Judge Satan [50-15] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-50-15.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=ff0fa9?nolink&640x360}}


When **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** returns, he will completely destroy **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/satan|Satan]]** and **his [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/kingdom|kingdom]]**. He will throw Satan into **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/hell|hell]]** where he will burn forever, along with everyone who chose to follow him rather than to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/obey|obey]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**his kingdom**  - This could also be translated as, “Satan's evil rule over people” or, “all the evil things he does and the evil people he controls.”
    * 


**rather than**  - That is, “instead of.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__50-14|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/50-jesus-returns|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__50-16|>>]]**


===== The New Heaven and Earth [50-16] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-50-16.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=5ee41c?nolink&640x360}}


Because **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/adam|Adam]]** and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/eve|Eve]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/disobey|disobeyed]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** and **brought [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sin|sin]] into**this world, God **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/curse|cursed]]** it and decided to destroy it. But some day God will create **a new [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/heaven|heaven]]** and **a new earth**  that will be perfect.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**brought sin into**  - This could be translated as, “caused sin to enter.”
    * 


**a new heaven**  - This could also be translated as, “a new sky” or, “a new universe”. It refers to a new set of stars and everything else in the sky.
    * 


**a new earth**  - This current earth on which we live will be replaced by a new and improved one.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__50-15|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/50-jesus-returns|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__50-17|>>]]**


===== Jesus Will Reign Forever [50-17] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-50-17.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=906a95?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jesus|Jesus]]** and his people will live on the new earth, and he will reign forever over everything that exists. He will **wipe away every tear**  and **there will be no more [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/suffer|suffering]], sadness, crying, [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/evil|evil]], pain, or [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/death|death]]**. Jesus will **rule his [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/kingdom-of-god|kingdom]] with [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/peace|peace]] and [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/justice|justice]]**, and he will be with his people forever.


//A Bible story from: Matthew 24:14; 28:18; John 15:20, 16:33; Revelation 2:10; Matthew 13:24-30, 36-42; 1 Thessalonians 4:13-5:11; James 1:12; Matthew 22:13; Revelation 20:10, 21:1-22:21//


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**wipe away every tear**  - This could also be translated as, “bring an end to all of our grief” or, “make trouble end” or, “tenderly take away any sadness people have.”
    * 


**there will be no more suffering, sadness, crying, evil, pain, or death**  - This could also be translated as, “people will no longer suffer, be sad, cry, do evil things, feel pain, or die.”
    * 


**rule his kingdom with peace and justice**  – This could also be translated as, “rule over his people fairly, in a way that brings them peace.”
    * 


//A Bible story from//  - These references may be slightly different in some Bible translations.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__50-16|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/50-jesus-returns|Up]]**
